[842|Body Text] This Extension covers Damage to Exhibition Property at any exhibition, seminar, conference, publicity promotions or similar functions attended by the Insured in connection with the Business anywhere within the United Kingdom or whilst in direct Transit Inland to or from such functions
[843|Body Text] provided that:
[844|Body Text] the Insurer shall not be liable for the Excess payable by the Insured for each and every claim; and
[845|Body Text] the Insurer shall not be liable for property more specifically insured elsewhere.
[846|## Heading 3] Fire Extinguishing Expenses
[847|Body Text] This Extension covers the reasonable costs incurred by the Insured as a result of Damage in:
[848|Body Text] refilling fire extinguishing appliances;
[849|Body Text] replacing used sprinkler heads;
[850|Body Text] refilling sprinkler tanks;
[851|Body Text] recharging gaseous flooding systems or water-based suppression systems; or
[852|Body Text] resetting fire alarms.
[853|## Heading 3] Garden and Ornamental Features Expenses
[854|Body Text] This Extension covers the costs incurred by the Insured for the restoration of gardens and ornamental features as a result of Damage caused by any emergency service provided that this Extension shall only apply where Damage to Property Insured has otherwise occurred and is the subject of a valid claim.
[855|## Heading 3] Inadvertent Omission to Insure
[856|Body Text] This Extension covers Property Insured which the Insured has inadvertently omitted to notify to the Insurer, subject to the payment of an additional premium charged by the Insurer on all such Property Insured as from the commencement of this Section or from the date of the Insured’s interest in such Property Insured if it is erected or purchased after the commencement of this Section
[857|Body Text] provided that:
[858|Body Text] it was the Insured’s intention to insure all Property Insured (other than Stock) in which the Insured has any interest;
[859|Body Text] the value of the Property Insured that has been inadvertently omitted shall for the purpose of the condition of Average be added to the Sum Insured on the Item that the Property Insured relates to or in the case of the Day One Uplift Extension the Declared Value.
[860|## Heading 3] Leased and Rented Premises
[861|Body Text] This Extension covers Damage to leased or rented premises for which the Insured is responsible, including landlords’ fixtures and fittings, provided that the Insurer shall not be liable for such Damage if liability is assumed by the Insured under a tenancy or other agreement and would not have attached in the absence of such agreement.
[862|## Heading 3] Metered Water
[863|Body Text] This Extension covers the cost for which the Insured is responsible in respect of loss of metered water provided that the Insured maintains a record of readings from the water authority meter at intervals of not more than 7 (seven) days.
[864|Body Text] The amount payable in respect of any one of the Premises is limited to such excess water charges demanded by the water authority resulting from the escape of water from pipes, apparatus or tanks as a result of Damage.
[866|Normal] Other Interests
[867|Normal] The interests of various parties are noted in this insurance, with the nature and extent of the interest to be disclosed at the time of Damage or, in respect of Information Technology Property, Breakdown.
[868|Normal] This Extension includes any party who has a financial interest in the insurance granted by this Section, provided that the Insured declares the name, nature and extent of the interest of any such party at the time of the Damage or Breakdown.
[869|## Heading 3] Removal of Debris
[870|Body Text] This Extension covers the costs and expenses necessarily incurred by the Insured with the consent of the Insurer in:
[871|Body Text] removing debris from;
[872|Body Text] dismantling or demolishing;
[873|Body Text] shoring up or propping; or
[874|Body Text] boarding up;
[875|Body Text] the portion or portions of the Property Insured by this Section following Damage.
[876|Body Text] The Insurer shall not pay any costs and expenses:
[877|Body Text] incurred in removing debris, except from the site of such Property Insured destroyed or damaged and the area immediately adjacent to such site; or
[878|Normal] arising from Pollution of property or land not insured by this Section.
[879|Normal] Removal of Information Technology Property
[880|Normal] In respect of Information Technology Property, this Extension also covers the costs necessarily and reasonably incurred in the removal of Property Insured as a result of Damage or Breakdown, provided that the Insurer’s approval of such costs has first been obtained in writing.
[881|## Heading 3] Replacement of Locks
[882|Body Text] This Extension covers the costs of any necessary replacement of all locks at the Premises following theft of the keys from any director, partner or Employee authorised to hold such keys.
[883|## Heading 3] Seventy-Two Hours
[884|Body Text] Any Damage occurring within 72 (seventy-two) consecutive hours and arising from storm, tempest or flood shall be regarded as one claim under this Policy.
[885|Body Text] The Insured has the right to select the moment from which the 72 (seventy-two) hour period commences subject to the terms of this Section and provided that such Damage occurred prior to the expiry of the Period of Insurance.
[886|## Heading 3] Temporary Removal
[887|Body Text] This Extension covers Damage to:
[888|Body Text] Contents whilst temporarily removed for cleaning, renovation, repair, testing, servicing or other similar purposes anywhere within the United Kingdom including whilst in Transit Inland; and
[889|Body Text] documents, manuscripts, business books and plans are covered whilst temporarily removed anywhere within the United Kingdom
[890|Body Text] provided that:
[891|Body Text] the Insurer shall not be liable for property more specifically insured; and
[892|Body Text] the Insurer shall not be liable for property held by the Insured in trust.
[893|## Heading 3] Theft Damage to Buildings
[894|Body Text] This Extension covers Damage caused by theft or attempted theft to Buildings which is/are not insured by this Section, provided the Insured is the owner of the Buildings or is legally liable for such Damage.
[895|## Heading 3] Trace and Access
[896|Body Text] This Extension covers the costs necessarily and reasonably incurred by the Insured in locating the source of the escape of water from any tank, apparatus or pipe and the subsequent making good of Damage caused by such locating.
[897|## Heading 3] Transfer of Interest
[898|Body Text] If at the time of Damage the Insured shall have contracted to sell his interest in any Building insured by this Section and such purchase is subsequently completed, the purchaser on completion of the purchase (if and so far as the property is not otherwise insured by or on behalf of the purchaser against such Damage) shall be entitled to the benefit of this Section so far as it relates to such Damage, without prejudice to the rights and liabilities of the Insured or the Insurer under this Section up to the date of completion.
[899|## Heading 1] Exclusions
[900|## Heading 3] Excluded Causes
[901|Normal] This Section does not cover:
[902|Body Text] Damage or Breakdown caused by or consisting of:
[904|Body Text] faulty or defective design, materials or inherent vice, latent defect, gradual deterioration, wear, tear, frost and any other gradually operating cause;
[905|Body Text] explosion occasioned by the bursting of a boiler (unless used for domestic purposes only), economiser or other vessel, machine or apparatus in which internal pressure is due to steam only and belonging to or under the control of the Insured; or
[906|Body Text] change solely in the water table level;
[907|Body Text] but this shall not exclude subsequent Damage or Breakdown which itself results from a cause not otherwise excluded.
[909|Body Text] corrosion, rust, change in temperature, dampness, humidity, dryness, wet or dry rot, shrinkage, evaporation, loss of weight, change in colour, flavour, texture or finish, or vermin or insects, marring or scratching;
[910|Body Text] joint leakage, failure of welds, cracking, fracturing, deformation or distortion;
[911|Body Text] collapse of or overheating of boilers, (unless used for domestic purposes only) economisers, super-heaters, pressure vessels or any range of steam and feed piping;
[912|Body Text] mechanical or electrical breakdown, derangement or overloading in respect of the particular machine, apparatus or equipment in which such breakdown or derangement originates but this shall not exclude Damage to surrounding property not forming part of the same machine, apparatus or equipment; or
[913|Body Text] faulty or defective workmanship or operational error or omission on the part of the Insured or any Employee of the Insured;
[914|Body Text] but this shall not exclude:
[915|Body Text] such Damage or Breakdown which itself results from a Defined Peril or from any other cause not otherwise excluded; or
[916|Body Text] subsequent Damage or Breakdown which itself results from a cause not otherwise excluded;
[917|Body Text] theft or attempted theft of Property Insured:
[918|Body Text] from any garden, yard or outbuilding;
[919|Body Text] from vending, amusement or gaming machines; or
[920|Body Text] from any Unoccupied Buildings;
[921|Body Text] theft or attempted theft of portable equipment from motor vehicles owned by or under the control of the Insured or their Employees whilst such vehicles are left unattended unless the vehicle is securely locked and all alarm devices are activated and such equipment is concealed or placed in a locked boot;
[923|Body Text] disappearance, unexplained or inventory shortage, misfiling or misplacing of information, clerical error, book keeping, accounting or billing errors or omissions;
[924|Body Text] acts of fraud or dishonesty by the Insured or by any director or Employee of the Insured;
[925|Body Text] the voluntary parting with title or possession of any property or rights to property;
[926|Body Text] escape of water from any water tanks, apparatus or pipes when the Buildings are Unoccupied and not being used for any of the Business activities of the Insured or any tenant;
[927|Body Text] malicious damage (other than fire or explosion) when the Buildings are Unoccupied and not being used for any of the Business activities of the Insured or any tenant;
[928|Body Text] subsidence, ground heave or landslip:
[929|Body Text] occasioned by the settlement or movement of made-up ground or by coastal or river erosion; or
[930|Body Text] occurring as a result of the construction, demolition or excavation work, structural alteration or structural repair of any property at the Premises or property immediately adjacent to the Premises.
[931|Body Text] The Insured shall give immediate notice to the Insurer in the event of construction, demolition or excavation work operations being commenced on any adjoining site.
[932|Body Text] In such event the Insurer shall have the right to vary or cancel the cover provided under this Section against Damage caused by subsidence, heave or landslip.
[933|Body Text] arising from the normal settlement or bedding down of new structures;
[934|Body Text] commencing prior to the granting of cover under this insurance.
[935|Body Text] Damage or Breakdown by wind, rain, hail, sleet, snow, flood or dust to fences and gates or moveable property in the open or in open-sided Buildings;
[936|Body Text] Consequential Loss except loss of Rent when such loss of Rent is included in the Schedule to this Section;
[937|Body Text] breakage of fixed glass directly or in any way resulting from:
[938|Body Text] defects in framework, beadings or other fittings;
[939|Body Text] disfiguration or Damage or Breakdown other than fracture extending through the entire thickness of the fixed glass; or
[940|Body Text] any attempt to remove any fixed glass, change its position or carry out any work on it or its framework, beadings or other fittings.
[941|Body Text] Damage or  respect of Buildings or structures caused by their own collapse or cracking, unless such Damage or  from a Defined Peril and is not otherwise excluded;
[942|Body Text] Damage or  any Property Insured by fire resulting from its undergoing any process involving the application of heat;
[943|Body Text] Damage or  any Property Insured (other than by fire) resulting from its undergoing any process of production, packing, treatment, testing, commissioning, cleaning, service or repair;
[944|Body Text] Damage or  any Property Insured (other than by fire) caused by or consisting of the freezing, solidification or inadvertent escape of molten materials; or
[945|Body Text] Damage or  any Property Insured where the Damage or  prior to the commencement of cover.
[946|## Heading 3] Excluded Property
[947|Body Text] This Section does not cover Damage to:
[948|Body Text] explosives;
[949|Body Text] fixed glass that is etched or stained or neon, or other electrical light fittings, signs or tubes;
[950|Body Text] vehicles licensed for road use (including accessories thereon), caravans, trailers, railway locomotives or rolling stock, watercraft, aircraft, spacecraft or satellites;
[951|Body Text] Property Insured whilst in transit unless covered by a specific Extension (other than internal movement within the Buildings at the Premises that does not involve loading and unloading onto or into a carrying conveyance);
[952|Body Text] property or structures in the course of construction or erection and materials or supplies in connection with all such property unless covered by a specific Extension;
[953|Body Text] land, piers, jetties, wharves, bridges, tunnels, culverts, excavations, railways, dams or bodies of water other than water which is normally contained within any tank, piping system or other process equipment;
[954|Body Text] livestock, birds, animals, landscapes, growing crops, plants or trees;
[955|Body Text] Property Insured which at the time of the happening of such Damage is insured by any other insurance;
[956|Body Text] any property more specifically insured by or on behalf of the Insured or by any other Section of this Policy;
[957|Body Text] jewellery, precious stones, precious metals, bullion, furs, curiosities, works of art, rare books, paintings, etchings or prints or Money;
[958|Body Text] china, earthenware, marble, statuary or other fragile or brittle objects;
[959|Body Text] Computer Equipment, software, Data Carrying Materials, Ancillary Equipment or Business Machines, unless insured as Information Technology Property under this Section;
[960|## Heading 1] Conditions
[961|## Heading 3] Cessation of Cover
[962|Body Text] This Section shall be terminated upon any Cessation of Business unless agreed otherwise by the Insurer in writing.
[964|Normal] Data Storage
[965|Normal] In respect of Information Technology Property, data, software or programs insured under this Section, it is a condition precedent to liability under this Section that the Insured shall store data and software programs and maintain adequate back-up copies on the following basis:
[966|Normal] the original disk or media shall be backed up and stored in a fire-resistant data safe and a copy removed to another secure location away from the Premises; and
[967|Normal] software or programs shall be backed up at least once every 7 (seven) days or any other period agreed by the Insurer.
[968|## Heading 3] Stock Premium Adjustment Condition
[969|Body Text] If the Stock Sum Insured stated in the Schedule applicable to this Section is on a declaration basis, then the first and annual premiums are provisional, having been calculated on a 75% (seventy five percent) deposit amount, and subject to adjustment at the expiry of the Period of Insurance.
[970|Body Text] The Insured shall submit to the Insurer a declaration of the Insured’s Stock amount for each quarter covered by the Period of Insurance.
[971|Body Text] Where no declaration is submitted within 30 (thirty) days after the expiry of each quarter, then the Insured shall have been deemed to have declared the Sum Insured as the value.
[972|Body Text] The actual premium shall be calculated on the average amount declared (i.e. the total of the amounts declared divided by the number of declarations) and using the agreed rate(s) applicable throughout the Period of Insurance.
[973|Body Text] If the actual premium is greater than the deposit amount paid the Insured shall pay to the Insurer the difference.
[974|Body Text] If the actual premium is less than the deposit amount paid the Insurer shall repay to the Insured the difference, which shall not exceed 1/3rd (one third) of the deposit amount paid.
[975|Body Text] Every insurance on such property which covers Damage must be on a materially similar wording with this Condition.
[978|## Subtitle] Section 2: Property & Equipment “All Risks” Section
[979|## Heading 1] Definitions
[980|## Heading 3] Geographical Limits
[981|Body Text] Anywhere in the world.
[982|## Heading 3] General Average Contributions
[983|Body Text] A legal principle of maritime law to which all parties in a sea venture proportionally share any losses resulting from a voluntary sacrifice of part of the ship’s cargo to save the whole adventure in an emergency.
[984|## Heading 3] Location
[985|Body Text] means the period of time between leaving the Premises for the purposes of the Business and return to the Premises including any overnight stay between these times.
[986|## Heading 3] Property Insured
[987|Body Text] Technical Equipment, Props, Sets and Wardrobes (including stock and merchandise) and Specified Articles all as stated in the Schedule and all the property of the Insured or for which they are responsible.
[988|## Heading 3] Props, Sets and Wardrobe
[989|Body Text] Props, sets, scenery, costumes, models, wardrobe and similar theatrical property owned by the Insured or for which they are responsible.
[990|## Heading 3] Specified Articles
[991|Body Text] As described in the Schedule.
[992|## Heading 3] Salvage Charges
[993|Body Text] Charges which apply in maritime law to compensate a third party in the event of a successful salvage due to a voluntary act by that third party independent of any contract.
[994|## Heading 3] Technical Equipment
[995|## Heading 3] Technical Equipment means property of the types described below, used in connection with the Insured’s business, any musical performance, production, conference, exhibition, event, festival or product launch, and which is owned by the Insured, held by the Insured in trust, hired, leased or borrowed by the Insured, or for which the Insured is legally responsible:
[996|## Heading 3] (a) musical instruments and associated cases, accessories   and ancillary equipment;
(b) microphones, sound, amplification and public address equipment;
(c) lighting, staging, projection and visual effects equipment;
(d) computer equipment, laptops, tablets, peripherals and business machines;
(e) mixing, editing, recording, sound production and post-production equipment;
(f) audio-visual, video, filming, streaming and broadcast equipment;
(g) stock, merchandise, promotional goods and display materials;
(h) props, scenery, sets, costumes and wardrobe;
() equipment, materials and other property used in connection with conferences, exhibitions, events, festivals and product launches; and
(j) any other similar property agreed by the Insurer in writing.
[998|## Heading 3] The Cover
[999|Body Text] If any of the Property Insured suffers Damage covered by this Policy within the Geographical Limits during the Period of Insurance, the Insurer will pay to the Insured the value of the Property Insured at the time of any Damage or at the Insurer’s option reinstate or replace such Property Insured or any part of the Property Insured.
[1000|## Heading 1] Basis of Settlement
[1001|Body Text] (The following Basis of Settlement are applicable as shown in the Schedule)
[1002|## Heading 3] Agreed Value Basis
[1003|Body Text] If Agreed Value is provided for in the Schedule the amount payable shall be the Sum Insured stated for that Item which shall be the value accepted by the Insurer.
[1004|Body Text] The Insurer shall not be liable for more than the relevant Sum Insured.
[1005|Body Text] Any Agreed Value is agreed for the purpose of this Policy only and no representations are made by the Insurer that they are the values which the relevant Items would attain if sold and they should not be relied upon for any purpose but this Policy.
[1006|Body Text] The condition of Average shall not apply to this Basis of Settlement.
[1007|## Heading 3] Indemnity Basis
[1008|Body Text] The amount payable for all claims shall be the amount representing the value of the Property Insured at the time of Damage.
[1009|## Heading 3] Reinstatement Basis
[1010|Body Text] If reinstatement is provided for in the Schedule the amount payable shall be calculated on the following basis:
[1011|Body Text] where Property Insured is destroyed or lost its cost of replacement by similar property in a condition equal to or substantially the same as but not better or more extensive than its condition when new;
[1012|Body Text] where Property Insured is damaged the cost of repairing or restoring the damaged portions to a condition equal to or substantially the same as but not better or more extensive than its condition when new.
[1013|Body Text] Subject to the following Reinstatement Basis Special Provisions
[1014|Body Text] where Property Insured suffers partial Damage the liability of the Insurer shall not exceed the amount that the Insurer could have been called upon to pay for reinstatement if such Property Insured had been wholly destroyed;
[1015|Body Text] the reinstatement of the Property Insured upon another site may be carried out in any manner suitable to the requirements of the Insured, provided that it is commenced and carried out with reasonable despatch, and the Insurer’s liability shall not exceed the amount of the value of the Property Insured at the time of the Damage;
[1016|Body Text] no payment beyond the amount that would have been payable in the absence of this Basis of Settlement shall be made:
[1017|Body Text] unless reinstatement commences and proceeds without unreasonable delay;
[1018|Body Text] until the cost of reinstatement shall have been actually incurred; and
[1019|Body Text] where the Property Insured is at the time of Damage insured by any other insurance effected by or on behalf of the Insured if it is not upon the same basis of reinstatement;
[1020|Body Text] the Sum Insured shown against each item described in the Schedule will not be less than the new replacement cost of such item.
[1021|Body Text] For the purpose of this Special Provision the new replacement cost will mean the present valid list price plus the cost of any freight, import duty and installation costs.
[1022|Body Text] In the event of the insured Item being obsolete the Sum Insured should represent the current list price plus the cost of any freight, import duty and installation costs of the nearest equivalent model.
[1023|## Heading 1] Extensions
[1024|## Heading 3] Alternative Hire
[1025|Body Text] This Extension covers the necessary and reasonable costs involved in hiring alternative Property Insured in the event of Damage as insured hereby under this Section, including ancillary and transit costs to enable the Insured to:
[1026|Body Text] continue shooting; or
[1027|Body Text] to fulfil future commitments;
[1028|Body Text] always provided that the liability of the Insurer shall commence from the date of the Damage and end when such Property Insured has been repaired or replaced.
[1029|Body Text] This is provided always that the Insurer’s maximum liability will not exceed the amount shown in the Schedule in respect of any one accident or series of accidents arising out of any one occurrence.
[1030|## Heading 3] Artists Equipment
[1031|Normal] This Extension covers Damage to Technical Equipment owned by artists, including but not limited to musical instruments, art supplies, and performance tools, brought onto the festival site, provided that such equipment is under the care, custody, or control of the Insured during the Period of insurance. Cover applies only where the Insured is legally responsible for such equipment. The Indemnity under this Extension is limited to a maximum of GBP 20,000 per occurrence and in the aggregate during the Period of insurance and is subject to the conditions and exclusions applicable to Technical Equipment.
[1032|## Heading 3] Automatic Reinstatement
[1033|Body Text] All or part of the Sum Insured that is reduced by the amount of any payment as a result of Damage shall be reinstated, upon payment by the Insured of the additional premium charged by the Insurer therefor proportionately for the period between the date of the Damage to the date of expiry of the Period of Insurance.
[1034|Body Text] In respect of theft losses, this Extension shall only apply to the first claim.
[1035|## Heading 3] Brands and Labels
[1036|Body Text] If branded or labelled merchandise is covered by this Section and is damaged the Insured may at their option:
[1037|Body Text] elect to destroy the salvage; or
[1038|Body Text] elect to take all or part of such merchandise at the value established by the terms of this Section of this Policy;
[1039|Body Text] provided that at the expense of the Insured, the Insured:
[1040|Body Text] shall stamp ‘salvage’ on the merchandise or the containers;
[1041|Body Text] shall remove or obliterate the brands or labels only if such stamp removal or obliteration will not Damage the merchandise; and
[1042|Body Text] must re-label the merchandise or the containers in accordance with the requirements of the law.
[1043|## Heading 3] Capital Additions or Acquisitions
[1044|Body Text] This Extension covers alterations and additions to the Property Insured
[1045|Body Text] provided that the Insured undertakes to advise the Insurer on the last day of each quarter of all such alterations and additions and to pay the appropriate additional premium on the amount of all increases advised.
[1046|## Heading 3] Customs Duty
[1047|Body Text] This Extension covers customs’ duty payable by the Insured in the event that they are unable to produce Property Insured they have imported for the purpose of their Business and detailed on the inventory agreed on arrival in consequence of Damage to the Property Insured.
[1048|## Heading 3] Consequential Loss Following Declaration of General Average
[1049|Body Text] This Extension covers the reasonable costs necessarily incurred by the Insured as a result of delay to the Property Insured whilst in transit caused by the Master of the carrying vessel declaring General Average subject to a maximum of GBP 10,000 in the aggregate during any one Period of Insurance. The Insured will bear the first 10% of any payable loss subject to a minimum of GBP 250.
[1050|## Heading 3] Exhibition Extension
[1051|Body Text] This Extension covers Damage to Exhibition Property at any exhibition, seminar, conference, publicity promotions and similar functions attended by the Insured in connection with the Business anywhere within the world or whilst in direct Transit Inland to or from such functions
[1052|Body Text] provided that:
[1053|Body Text] the Insurer shall not be liable for the Excess payable by the Insured for each and every claim; and
[1054|Body Text] the Insurer shall not be liable for property more specifically insured elsewhere.
[1055|Body Text] For the purposes of this Extension:
[1056|Body Text] Exhibition Property means any exhibits (including demonstration and sample stock) stands, marquees, furniture, furnishings, display materials, office equipment, stationery and other similar property on the stands.
[1057|## Heading 3] Fine Arts
[1058|Body Text] This Extension covers Damage to Fine Arts the property of or belonging to the Insured whilst anywhere within the Geographical Limits
[1059|Body Text] provided that:
[1060|Body Text] the liability of the Insurer shall not exceed the cost of repairing or restoring the Fine Art to its condition that existed immediately prior to the Damage or the cost of replacing the Fine Art whichever is the lesser; and
[1061|Body Text] in the event of Damage to Fine Art which forms or is part of a pair or set the measure of Damage shall be a reasonable and fair proportion of the total value of the pair or set allowing for the importance of such pair or set but such Damage shall not be deemed to mean the total loss of the pair or set.
[1062|Body Text] For the purposes of this Extension:
[1063|Body Text] Fine Art shall mean paintings, pictures, tapestries, etchings, and other bona fide works of art including bronzes, marble, porcelain, statuary, rare books, manuscripts, antique furniture, antique silver, rare glass and rare objects of a historical value or artistic merit or of a precious nature.
[1064|## Heading 3] Involuntary Betterment
[1065|Body Text] This Extension covers more extensive replacement Property Insured of a like kind and quality where replacement is not obtainable.
[1066|Body Text] New Property Insured which is as similar as possible to that suffering Damage and which is capable of performing the same function is deemed to be new property of a like kind and quality and in no event shall this be considered as a betterment to the Insured.
[1067|Body Text] The Insurer will also pay the cost of purchasing and installing technologically current Property Insured which is necessitated by the incompatibility between:
[1068|Body Text] new Property Insured installed to replace Property Insured that has sustained Damage; and
[1069|Body Text] undamaged existing Property Insured at the same Premises or an interdependent premises;
[1070|Body Text] provided that the Insurer will only be liable for:
[1071|Body Text] the amount sufficient to enable the Insured to resume Business operations in substantially the same manner as before the Damage;
[1072|Body Text] the difference between:
[1073|Body Text] the highest sales value of the undamaged existing Property Insured at the same Premises or an interdependent premises; and
[1074|Body Text] the installed cost of the technologically current Property Insured.
[1075|Normal] Incompatibility
[1076|Normal] This Extension covers the costs of:
[1077|Normal] modification of Computer Equipment; or
[1078|Normal] replacement of Data Carrying Materials together with reinstatement of data contained thereon;
[1079|Normal] whichever is the lesser to achieve compatibility in the event that loss of Computer Equipment indemnified by this Section has resulted in undamaged Data Carrying Materials being incompatible with the replacement Computer Equipment.
[1080|Normal] Provided that the Insurer’s approval of such costs has first been obtained in writing.
[1081|## Heading 3] Loan Property Insured
[1082|Body Text] This Extension covers Property Insured loaned to the Insured in substitution of existing Property Insured which is being serviced, maintained, cleaned or repaired.
[1083|## Heading 3] Marine General Average
[1084|Body Text] This Extension will indemnify the Insured for General Average Contributions and Salvage Charges whist the Property Insured is being transported by sea between any countries within the Territorial Limits, provided that the Property Insured is otherwise covered for loss or Damage under this Policy and the liability of the Insurer does not exceed the Sum Insured for the Insured items.
[1085|## Heading 3] Transit Extension
[1086|Body Text] This Extension covers Damage to the Property Insured whilst the same is in transit anywhere in the world, always provided that such transits are undertaken in connection with moving the Property Insured to and from the Insured’s Premises to a location where the Insured is undertaking work.
[1087|Body Text] This Extension is in addition to the transit cover provided under the Exhibitions and Temporary Removal Extensions
[1088|## Heading 1] Optional Extensions
[1089|Body Text] (Operative only if stated in the Schedule)
[1090|## Heading 3] Hired-in Property
[1091|Body Text] This Extension covers payments to the Insured in respect of:
[1092|Body Text] legal liability for Damage to hired-in Property Insured under the terms of the hiring agreement or otherwise to pay compensation for Damage to property Insured described in the Schedule;
[1093|Body Text] legal liability under the terms of the hiring agreement to pay continuing hire charges incurred under the terms of the hiring in agreement in consequence of Damage to hired-in Property Insured for which the Insurer have admitted liability;
[1094|Body Text] provided that the Insurer’s maximum liability will:
[1095|Body Text] commence from the date of the Damage, and end when such Property Insured has been repaired or replaced,
[1096|Body Text] not exceed the amount shown in the Schedule in respect of any one accident or series of accidents arising out of any one occurrence.
[1097|## Heading 3] Hired-out Property
[1098|Body Text] This Extension covers Damage to Property Insured whilst hired out by the Insured, provided always that all such hires remain subject to conditions of hire in line with current industry standards and that such conditions have been lodged with and agreed by the Insurer.
[1099|Body Text] The Insurer will not exercise rights of subrogation against the hirer where the Insured’s hire invoice so specifies.
[1100|Body Text] Whenever the Property Insured is hired in for rehire by the Insured the hiring conditions will be no less onerous than those under which the Insured hired in such Property Insured.
[1101|Body Text] This is provided always that the Insurer’s maximum liability will not exceed the amount shown in the Schedule in respect of any one accident or series of accidents arising out of any one occurrence.
[1102|## Heading 3] Mechanical and Electrical Breakdown
[1103|Body Text] Notwithstanding anything contained herein to the contrary this Extension covers Damage to the Property Insured caused by the Breakdown thereof provided that:
[1104|Body Text] all Property Insured is fully maintained in accordance with the manufacturer’s instructions;
[1105|Body Text] all Property Insured is fully tested in accordance with the industry’s highest standards and is deemed to be in good working order prior to the use of the Property Insured; and
[1106|Body Text] the Insurer shall not be liable under this Extension for Breakdown of Property Insured caused by or occasioned through:
[1107|Body Text] the intentional act or wilful neglect of the Insured;
[1108|Body Text] wear and tear gradual deterioration, gradually developing defects, corrosion, rust or scratching or chipping of painted or polished surfaces; or
[1109|Body Text] any testing, repairing, adjusting, servicing or maintenance operation.
[1110|Body Text] This is provided always that the Insurer’s maximum liability will not exceed the amount shown in the Schedule in respect of any one accident or series of accidents arising out of any one occurrence.
[1111|Body Text] For the purposes of this Optional Extension “Breakdown” shall mean damage to an item of Property Insured resulting from the actual breaking, distortion or electrical burn-out of any part of it whilst in use arising from the defects in the item of Property Insured causing the sudden stoppage of its function and requiring its repair or replacement but excluding Damage caused by any cause external to the Property Insured.
[1112|## Heading 3] Sub-Limit Restriction
[1113|Body Text] Notwithstanding anything contained herein to the contrary it is understood and agreed that the Insurer’s maximum Limit of Liability in respect of Damage to Property Insured occurring away from the Insured’s Premises shall not exceed:
[1114|Body Text] the amount shown in the Schedule in respect of any one location nor
[1115|Body Text] the amount shown in the Schedule in respect of any one single item of Property Insured
[1116|Body Text] or as otherwise agreed in writing by the Insurer.
[1117|## Heading 1] Optional Conditions
[1118|## Heading 3] Fraudulent Hire – Vetting Requirements
[1119|Body Text] (If shown in the Schedule as applicable, this Condition will apply)
[1120|Body Text] In respect of Damage to Technical Equipment, hired out under a standard hire contract, arising as a result of the theft of such Technical Equipment by the hirer’s deception, It is a condition precedent to liability under this Policy that the Insured has:
[1121|Body Text] obtained and verified at least 2 (two) trade references for each  hirer; and
[1122|Body Text] retained a copy of the third party’s letterhead and a copy of at least 2 (two) utility bills for the  hirer relating to the same premises; and
[1123|Body Text] retained a copy of the credit card details of the  hirer; and
[1124|Body Text] only allowed the actual  hiring company to collect the hired out Technical Equipment and has upon collection taken a copy of the  hirer’s identification and have also taken their photograph.
[1125|## Heading 3] Amended Property in Unattended Vehicle Condition
[1126|Body Text] (If shown in the Schedule as applicable, this Condition replaces the default Property in Unattended Vehicle Condition below)
[1127|Body Text] It is a Condition Precedent to liability under this Policy that in respect of Property Insured whilst contained in an unattended road vehicle that:
[1128|Body Text] all doors, windows and other openings are fully closed and locked whenever the conveying vehicle is left unattended and any property concealed from view wherever possible;
[1129|Body Text] between the hours of 21:00 and 06:00 unless the conveying vehicle is on Location it will be:
[1130|Body Text] fully alarmed and the alarm placed in full and effective operation, or
[1131|Body Text] kept in a locked garage or building or secure compound.
[1132|## Heading 1] Conditions
[1133|## Heading 3] Average
[1134|Body Text] The Sum Insured by each item of this Section, other than Optional Extension - Hired-in Property, is declared to be separately subject to Average.
[1135|## Heading 3] Property in Unattended Vehicle Condition
[1136|Body Text] It is a condition precedent to liability under this Policy that in respect of Property Insured whilst contained in an unattended road vehicle:
[1137|Body Text] all doors, windows and other openings are fully closed and locked and, unless the vehicle is a van or is fitted with a cage, that the Property Insured is situated in an enclosed luggage compartment capable of concealing the Property Insured from view;
[1138|Body Text] and
[1139|Body Text] between the hours of 21:00 and 06:00 unless the vehicle is on Location it shall be:
[1140|Body Text] fully alarmed and the alarm placed in full and effective operation; and
[1141|Body Text] kept in a locked garage or building or security compound.
[1142|## Heading 3] Technical Equipment Hired Out
[1143|Body Text] It is a condition precedent to liability under this Policy that in the circumstances where Technical Equipment is hired out to a third party by the Insured without such Technical Equipment being accompanied by the Insured or an Employee of the Insured then a signed hiring agreement:
[1144|Body Text] holding the  hirer responsible for Damage caused to such Technical Equipment; and
[1145|Body Text] showing that the  hirer will indemnify the Insured;
[1146|Body Text] must be obtained by the Insured.
[1147|## Heading 3] Technical Equipment Hired In
[1148|Body Text] It is a condition precedent to liability under this Policy that in the circumstances where Technical Equipment is hired in by the Insured from a third party, to be used at a  Location that:
[1149|Body Text] a written inventory or checklist accepting responsibility for all Technical Equipment hired in, is in place and signed by the Insured upon delivery or receipt; and
[1150|Body Text] a full inventory must be taken and signed by a representative of the Insured prior to leaving the Location or contract site and before return or collection by the hire company.
[1151|## Heading 1] Exclusions
[1152|## Heading 3] Exclusions applicable to Technical Equipment
[1153|Body Text] This Section does not cover:
[1154|Body Text] loss of use of the Property Insured or any other Consequential Loss unless more specifically insured by this Section;
[1155|Body Text] Damage to:
[1156|Body Text] light sources and other expendable parts unless accompanied by other Damage insured hereby;
[1157|Body Text] film, video and sound recording tape whilst contained within any camera, sound or video recording equipment or whilst undergoing any form of processing;
[1158|Body Text] film, video and sound recording tape which suffers Damage at custom points as a result of exposure by surveillance machines;
[1159|Body Text] Damage caused by insufficiency or the unsuitability of packing or preparation of the Property Insured;
[1160|Body Text] Damage recoverable under any guarantee or maintenance, rental, hire or lease agreement;
[1161|Body Text] Damage caused by:
[1162|Body Text] the intentional act or  neglect of the Insured;
[1163|Body Text] gradually developing defects, cracks, flaws or fractures;
[1164|Body Text] experiments involving the imposition of any abnormal conditions on the Property Insured;
[1165|Body Text] penalties for delay or detention or in connection with guarantees of performance or efficiency;
[1166|Body Text] unaccountable losses discovered on the occasion of stock or inventory checks;
[1167|Body Text] the amount of the Excess;
[1168|Body Text] mechanical or electrical breakdown, wear, tear or gradual deterioration.
[1169|Body Text] aircraft, other mechanically propelled vehicles or conveyances, unless full details have been submitted to and accepted by the Insurers.
[1170|## Heading 3] Exclusions applicable to Props, Sets and Wardrobes
[1171|Body Text] This Section does not cover:
[1172|Body Text] Damage directly or in any way caused by or resulting from:
[1173|Body Text] mechanical or electrical breakdown, wear, tear, gradual deterioration, the process of cleaning, repairing or restoring any article, the action of light or atmosphere conditions, vermin or moth;
[1174|Body Text] property being worked upon;
[1175|Body Text] shortage of inventory or any unexplained loss or mysterious disappearance;
[1176|Body Text] rain, sleet, snow or hail to Property Insured stored in the open;
[1177|Body Text] short circuit or other electrical damage or disturbance or failure (however this Exclusion does not apply to Damage caused by resultant fire or explosion);
[1178|Body Text] Consequential Loss;
[1179|Body Text] the amount of the Excess;
[1180|Body Text] breakage of property wholly or partly of a brittle nature unless details have been submitted to and accepted by the Insurer;
[1181|Body Text] unsuitability or insufficiency of packing.
[1182|Body Text] Damage to:
[1183|Body Text] camera, camera equipment, sound and lighting equipment, grip equipment, portable electrical equipment and generators;
[1184|Body Text] animals;
[1185|Body Text] currency, money and other negotiable instruments, credit cards, passports, deeds, letters of credit or travel tickets;
[1186|Body Text] permanent buildings or structure;
[1187|Body Text] aircraft, other mechanically propelled vehicles or conveyances unless full details have been submitted to and accepted by the Insurer;
[1188|Body Text] film or  or
[1189|Body Text] jewellery, furs, precious metals, precious stones, curiosities, rare books and works of art collectively in excess of GBP 10,000 (ten thousand pounds sterling) unless details have been submitted to and accepted by the Insurer.
[1190|## Heading 3] Exclusions applicable to Specified Articles
[1191|Body Text] This Section does not cover:
[1192|Body Text] Damage caused by or consisting of:
[1193|Body Text] mechanical or electrical breakdown or derangement or its own overrunning, short circuiting or self-heating;
[1194|Body Text] corrosion, rust, wet or dry rot, shrinkage, evaporation, loss of weight, dampness, marring, scratching, vermin or insects;
[1195|Body Text] depreciation;
[1196|Body Text] change in temperature, colour, , texture or finish;
[1197|Body Text] any process of cleaning, dyeing, repairing, restoring, alteration or adjusting;
[1198|Body Text] atmosphere or climatic conditions or action of light;
[1199|Body Text] inherent vice, latent defect, gradual deterioration, wear and tear, frost, its own faulty or defective design, workmanship or materials;
[1200|Body Text] Consequential Loss; or
[1201|Body Text] theft where any person in the employ or service of the Insured or members of their family are concerned as principal or accessory.
[1202|Body Text] The amount of the Excess.
[1205|## Subtitle] Section 3: Business Interruption “All Risks” Section
[1206|## Heading 1] Definitions
[1207|## Heading 3] Accounts Receivable
[1208|Body Text] The total amount of the balances debited to customers in the Insured’s accounts and declared in the statement last given after allowances have been made for bad debts and for amounts debited (or invoiced but not debited) and credited (including credit notes and cash not passed through the books at the time of the Incident) to customers’ accounts in the period between the date of said statement and the date of the Incident.
[1209|## Heading 3] Estimated Gross Profit
[1210|Body Text] The amount declared by the Insured to the Insurer as representing not less than the Gross Profit which it is anticipated will be earned by the Business during the financial year most nearly concurrent with the Period of Insurance or a proportionately increased multiple where the Maximum Indemnity Period exceeds 12 (twelve) months.
[1211|## Heading 3] Estimated Gross Revenue
[1212|Body Text] The amount declared by the Insured to the Insurer as representing not less than the Gross Revenue which it is anticipated will be earned by the Business during the financial year most nearly concurrent with the Period of Insurance or a proportionately increased multiple where the Maximum Indemnity Period exceeds 12 (twelve) months.
[1213|## Heading 3] Exhibition Property
[1214|Body Text] Exhibits (including demonstration and sample Stock), stands, marquees, furniture, furnishings, display materials, office equipment, stationery and other similar property on the stands.
[1215|## Heading 3] Gross Profit
[1216|Body Text] The amount by which the sum of the amount of the Turnover and the amounts of the closing stock and work in progress shall exceed the sum of the amounts of the opening stock and work in progress and the amount of the Uninsured Working Expenses.
[1217|Body Text] The amounts of the opening and closing stocks (including work in progress) shall be arrived at in accordance with the Insured’s normal accounting methods.
[1218|## Heading 3] Gross Revenue
[1219|Body Text] The money paid or payable to the Insured for work done and services rendered in the course of the Business.
[1220|## Heading 3] Indemnity Period
[1221|Body Text] The period beginning with the occurrence of the Incident and ending not later than the end of the Maximum Indemnity Period thereafter during which the results of the Business shall be affected as a result of the Incident.
[1222|## Heading 3] Maximum Indemnity Period
[1223|Body Text] The period stated in the Schedule to this Section.
[1224|## Heading 3] Rent Receivable
[1225|Body Text] The money paid or payable to the Insured for tenancies and other charges for services rendered in the course of the Business at the Premises.
[1226|## Heading 3] Specified Illness
[1227|Body Text] Acute encephalitis, acute poliomyelitis, anthrax, chickenpox, cholera, diphtheria, dysentery, leprosy, leptospirosis, malaria, measles, meningococcal infection, mumps, ophthalmia neonatorum, paratyphoid fever, plague, rabies, rubella, scarlet fever, smallpox, tetanus, tuberculosis, typhoid fever, viral hepatitis, whooping cough or yellow fever.
[1228|## Heading 3] Trends and Variations
[1229|Body Text] Rate of Gross Profit
[1230|Body Text] The Rate of Gross Profit earned on the Turnover during the financial year immediately before the date of the Incident
[1231|Body Text] Annual Turnover (not applicable to Declaration Linked Basis of Settlement)
[1232|Body Text] The Turnover during the 12 (twelve) months immediately before the date of the Incident
[1233|Body Text] Standard Turnover
[1234|Body Text] The Turnover during that period in the 12 (twelve) months immediately before the date of the Incident which corresponds with the Indemnity Period
[1235|Body Text] Annual Gross Revenue (not applicable to Declaration Linked Basis of Settlement)
[1236|Body Text] The Gross Revenue during the 12 (twelve) months immediately before the date of the Incident
[1237|Body Text] Standard Gross Revenue
[1238|Body Text] The Gross Revenue during that period in the 12 (twelve) months immediately before the date of the Incident which corresponds with the Indemnity Period
[1239|Body Text] Annual Rent Receivable
[1240|Body Text] The Rent Receivable during the 12 (twelve) months immediately before the date of the Incident
[1241|Body Text] Standard Rent Receivable
[1242|Body Text] The Rent Receivable during the period in the 12 (twelve) months immediately before the date of the Incident which corresponds with the Indemnity Period
[1243|Body Text] to which such adjustments shall be made where necessary to provide for the trend of the Business and for variations in or other circumstances affecting the Business either before or after the Incident or which would have affected the Business had the Incident not occurred so that the adjusted figures shall represent as nearly as may be reasonably practicable the results which but for the Incident would have been obtained during the relative period after the Incident.
[1244|## Heading 3] Turnover
[1245|Body Text] The money paid or payable to the Insured for goods sold and delivered and for services rendered in the course of the Business at the Premises.
[1246|## Heading 3] Uninsured Working Expenses
[1247|Body Text] If any charges of the Business not insured by this Policy have been deducted when calculating the Sum Insured, then in computing the amount recoverable as Increase in Cost of Working that proportion only of any additional expenditure shall be brought into account (in the ratio that the Sum Insured bears to the sum of the Sum Insured and the Uninsured Working Expenses as stated in the Schedule to this Section).
[1248|## Heading 3] The Cover
[1249|Body Text] If the Business carried on by the Insured at the Premises is interrupted or interfered with as a consequence of an Incident during the Period of Insurance, the Insurer will indemnify or compensate the Insured in accordance with the provisions stated in this Section
[1250|Body Text] provided that at the time of the happening of the interruption of or interference with the Business there shall be in force an insurance covering the insurable interest of the Insured in the property at the Premises against such Incident and that:
[1251|Body Text] payment shall have been made or liability admitted thereunder; or
[1252|Body Text] payment would have been made or liability admitted thereunder but for the operation of a proviso in such insurance excluding liability for losses below a specified amount;
[1253|## Heading 1] Basis of Settlement
[1254|Body Text] The following Basis of Settlement shall apply only if the paragraph title appears in the Schedule to this Section.
[1255|## Heading 3] Accounts Receivable
[1256|Body Text] The amount payable as compensation under this Item shall be:
[1257|Body Text] loss of Accounts Receivable (being the difference solely due to an Incident between the amount of the Accounts Receivable at the date of the Incident and the total amount received by the Insured in payment of Accounts Receivable during the Indemnity Period); and
[1258|Body Text] the additional expenditure necessarily and reasonably incurred for the sole purpose of avoiding or diminishing the loss of Accounts Receivable which but for that expenditure would have occurred as a result of the Incident but not exceeding the amount of reduction in Accounts Receivable avoided.
[1259|Body Text] If the Sum Insured by the Item on Accounts Receivable is less than the total amount of the Accounts Receivable, the amount payable shall be proportionately reduced.
[1260|## Heading 3] Additional Increase in Cost of Working
[1261|Body Text] The amount payable under this Item shall be the further additional expenses beyond those recoverable under Item 2 of the Gross Profit, Gross Revenue or Rent Receivable Basis of Settlement, necessarily and reasonably incurred during the Indemnity Period as a result of an Incident for the sole purpose of avoiding or diminishing a reduction in Turnover, Gross Revenue or Rent Receivable, but not exceeding the Sum Insured stated in the Schedule relating to this cover. At Your option, this may include any overtime payments at the employee’s standard rate or any payments for time in lieu.
[1262|## Heading 3] Declaration Linked
[1263|Body Text] (only applicable if operative in the Schedule to this Section)
[1264|Body Text] If the Insured has opted for the Declaration Linked Basis of Settlement, then the insurance provided by Gross Profit or Gross Revenue shall be subject to:
[1265|Body Text] Premium Adjustment 1 Condition;
[1266|Body Text] Renewal Condition; and
[1267|Body Text] Limit of Liability Condition increasing the estimated Sum Insured by 33.33% (thirty-three point three percent).
[1268|## Heading 3] Gross Profit
[1269|Body Text] The amount payable as compensation under this Item shall be:
[1270|Body Text] in respect of a reduction in Turnover, which is the sum produced by applying the Rate of Gross Profit to the amount by which the Turnover during the Indemnity Period shall fall short of the Standard Turnover as a result of an Incident; and
[1271|Body Text] the additional expenditure (subject to the provisions of the Uninsured Working Expenses) necessarily and reasonably incurred for the sole purpose of avoiding or diminishing the reduction in Turnover which but for that expenditure would have taken place during the Indemnity Period as a result of an Incident but not exceeding the sum produced by applying the Rate of Gross Profit to the amount of the reduction avoided;
[1272|Body Text] less any sum saved during the Indemnity Period in respect of such charges and expenses of the Business payable out of Gross Profit as may cease or be reduced as a result of an Incident;
[1273|Body Text] provided that if the Sum Insured on Gross Profit is less than the sum produced by applying the Rate of Gross Profit to the Annual Turnover or to a proportionately increased multiple where the Maximum Indemnity Period exceeds 12 (twelve) months, the amount payable shall be proportionately reduced.
[1274|## Heading 3] Gross Revenue
[1275|Body Text] The amount payable as compensation under this Item shall be:
[1276|Body Text] loss of Gross Revenue being the amount by which the Gross Revenue during the Indemnity Period shall fall short of the Standard Gross Revenue as a result of an Incident; and
[1277|Body Text] the additional expenditure (subject to the provisions of the Uninsured Working Expenses) necessarily and reasonably incurred for the sole purpose of avoiding or diminishing the reduction in Gross Revenue which but for that expenditure would have taken place during the Indemnity Period as a result of an Incident but not exceeding the amount of the reduction in Gross Revenue avoided
[1278|Body Text] less any sum saved during the Indemnity Period in respect of such charges and expenses of the Business payable out of Gross Revenue as may cease or be reduced as a result of an Incident;
[1279|Body Text] provided that if the Sum Insured on Gross Revenue is less than the Annual Revenue or to a proportionately increased multiple where the Maximum Indemnity Period exceeds 12 (twelve) months the amount payable shall be proportionately reduced.
[1280|## Heading 3] Increase in Cost of Working
[1281|Body Text] The amount payable as compensation under this Item shall be the additional expenditure (including the cost of removal to and from and the additional rent of temporary premises, additional rates and taxes and expenses incurred in equipping the temporary premises to make them suitable for the Insured’s Business additional cost in respect of additional staff and overtime and allowances for meals to existing staff) necessarily and reasonably incurred in order to minimise any interruption to or interference with the Business during the Indemnity Period but only insofar as such additional expenditure:
[1282|Body Text] is not recoverable under any other Item of this Policy;
[1283|Body Text] is incurred for the sole purpose of avoiding or diminishing the reduction in Turnover/Gross Revenue/Rent Receivable which but for that expenditure would have taken place during the Indemnity Period as a result of the Incident but not exceeding either:
[1284|Body Text] the sum produced by applying the Rate of Gross Profit to the amount of the reduction reasonably avoided; or
[1285|Body Text] the amount of the reduction in Gross Revenue or Rent Receivable reasonably avoided.
[1286|## Heading 3] Increase in Cost of Working (Computers)
[1287|Body Text] The insurance by this Section is in respect of additional expenditure necessarily and reasonably incurred by the Insured to:
[1288|Body Text] prevent or minimise the interruption of or interference with the work normally carried out by or on the Computer Equipment or Electronic Office Equipment excluding additional expenditure more specifically insured elsewhere in this Policy;
[1289|Body Text] recompile or restore data or software or replace third party proprietary software
[1290|Body Text] in consequence of an Incident which manifests itself during the Period of Insurance.
[1291|## Heading 1] Definitions applicable to this Basis of Settlement only
[1292|## Heading 3] Approved Maintenance Agreement
[1293|Body Text Indent] An agreement which provides on-call remedial maintenance encompassing free repair or replacement in the event of breakdown arising out of normal use.  The Insured shall supply to the Insurer a copy of any such agreement.
[1294|## Heading 3] Breakdown
[1295|Body Text Indent] The actual breaking or failure of any part of the equipment whilst in ordinary use arising from either mechanical or electrical defect causing stoppage of the function thereof which necessitates repair or replacement in order to continue normal working.
[1296|## Heading 3] Computer Equipment
[1297|Body Text Indent] Computer equipment (including fixed disks and interconnecting wiring but not Computer Media) used for electronic processing communication and storage of data the property of the Insured or leased hired or rented to the Insured.
[1298|## Heading 3] Computer Media
[1299|Body Text Indent] Computer media of all types (other than paper records) the property of the Insured or leased hired or licensed to the Insured.
[1300|## Heading 3] Electronic Office Equipment
[1301|Body Text Indent] Electronically operated office equipment (other than Computer Equipment) the property of the Insured or leased hired or rented to the Insured.
[1302|## Heading 3] Incident
[1303|Body Text] Damage to any item of Computer Equipment at the Premises caused by its Breakdown;
[1304|Body Text] Damage to Computer Media at the Premises or at any other premises anywhere in the world including whilst in transit;
[1305|Body Text] erasure, destruction, corruption or distortion of software contained or data stored on fixed disks or Computer Media;
[1306|Body Text] the failure or fluctuation of the supply of electricity to the Computer Equipment; or
[1307|Body Text] the failure of any telecommunication system linked to the Computer Equipment.
[1308|## Heading 1] Exclusions
[1309|Body Text] The Insurers shall not be liable under this Basis of Settlement in respect of:
[1310|Body Text] the amount shown in the Schedule as the Excess in respect of each and every loss;
[1311|Body Text] any additional expenditure in consequence of the use by the Insured of software in respect of which development has not been finalised or which has not passed all testing procedures or which has not been successfully proven;
[1312|Body Text] any additional expenditure in consequence of failure to comply with manufacturers’ recommendations relating to storage of Computer Media;
[1313|Body Text] any additional expenditure commencing more than 12 (twelve) months after the date on which the Incident manifests itself;
[1314|Body Text] the costs of rectifying programming errors or design defects in software;
[1315|Body Text] (in the case of  proprietary software only) any additional expenditure in consequence of programming errors or design defects but this Exclusion shall not apply to additional expenditure consequent upon erasure, destruction, corruption or distortion of other software caused by programming errors or design defects in third party proprietary software;
[1316|Body Text] the value to the Insured of data stored on Computer Equipment or Computer Media;
[1317|Body Text] any additional expenditure in consequence of a failure of the public supply of electricity directly or in any way due to:
[1318|Body Text] a deliberate act of the supply authority not performed for the sole purpose of safeguarding life or protecting any part of the supply system;
[1319|Body Text] a scheme of rationing not necessitated by accidental damage to the supply authority generating or supply equipment;
[1320|Body Text] the inability of the supply authority to maintain the supply system due to industrial action by any of its employees;
[1321|Body Text] any additional expenditure in consequence of a failure of any telecommunications system directly or in any way due to:
[1322|Body Text] a deliberate act of the telecommunications authority or the exercise by the telecommunications authority of its power to withhold or restrict operation of the system;
[1323|Body Text] the inability of the telecommunications authority to maintain the system due to industrial action by any of its employees;
[1324|Body Text] the use by the Insured of equipment which is not approved by the telecommunications authority;
[1325|Body Text] failure of any satellite prior to its obtaining its full operating function or while in or beyond the final year of its design life;
[1326|Body Text] atmospheric solar or lunar conditions causing temporary interference with transmission to or from any satellite;
[1327|Body Text] the cost of rectification or making good wear and tear gradual deterioration due to atmospheric conditions or otherwise rust, corrosion or oxidisation or scratching of painted or polished surfaces but insured damage or additional expenditure in consequence of damage resulting therefrom is not excluded.

[1336|Body Text] store all Computer Media in accordance with the manufacturers’ recommendations.

[1340|Body Text] the additional expenditure (subject to the provisions of the Uninsured Working Expenses) necessarily and reasonably incurred for the sole purpose of avoiding or diminishing the reduction in Rent Receivable which but for that expenditure would have taken place during the Indemnity Period as a result of an Incident but not exceeding the amount of the reduction in Rent Receivable avoided;

[1345|## Heading 1] Extensions
[1346|## Heading 3] Alternative Trading
[1347|Body Text] If during the Indemnity Period goods shall be sold or services shall be rendered elsewhere than at the Premises for the benefit of the Business either by the Insured or by others on their behalf, the money paid or payable in respect of such sales or services shall be brought into account in arriving at the Turnover during the Indemnity Period.
[1348|## Heading 3] Automatic Reinstatement
[1349|Body Text] All or part of the Sum Insured that is reduced by the amount of any payment as a result of any Incident shall be reinstated, upon payment by the Insured of the additional premium charged by the Insurer therefor proportionately for the period between the date of the Incident to the date of expiry of the Period of Insurance.
[1350|## Heading 3] Customers and Suppliers
[1351|Body Text] For the purposes of this Section an Incident covers Damage to property at the premises of those customers or suppliers who are stated in the Schedule to this Section provided that the Insurer shall not be liable for any interruption or interference with the Business arising from Damage to the property at the premises of the specified suppliers as stated in the Schedule which does not involve an interruption or interference of at least 72 (seventy-two) consecutive hours.
[1352|## Heading 3] Denial of Access
[1353|Body Text] For the purposes of this Section an Incident includes Damage to property within the distance from the Premises as stated in the Schedule to this Section, which shall prevent or hinder the use of or access to the Premises or property of the Insured whether the Insured’s property is damaged or not, provided that:
[1354|Body Text] the Insurer shall not be liable for Damage to the property of any supply undertaking from which the Insured obtains gas, electricity, water or telecommunications;
[1355|Body Text] the Insurer shall not be liable for interruption of or interference with the Business arising from Damage lasting less than 8 (eight) consecutive hours of prevention or hindrance.
[1356|## Heading 3] Departmental
[1357|Body Text] If the Business is conducted in departments whose independent trading results are ascertainable, the Basis of Settlement for Gross Profit or Gross Revenue shall apply separately to each department affected by an Incident.
[1358|## Heading 3] Specified Illness and Miscellaneous Contingencies
[1359|Body Text] Definitions applicable to this Extension
[1360|Body Text] Specified Incident shall mean:
[1361|Body Text] any person who whilst at the Premises contracts a Specified Illness, an outbreak of which the local authority has stipulated shall be notified to them;
[1362|Body Text] an outbreak of any Specified Illness manifested within the distance, as stated in the Schedule to this Section, from the Premises;
[1363|Body Text] murder, rape or suicide occurring at the Premises;
[1364|Body Text] injury or illness sustained by any person arising from or traceable to foreign or injurious matter in food or drink provided on the Premises;
[1365|Body Text] any discovery of an organism at the Premises likely to result in an occurrence of legionnaires’ disease; or
[1366|Body Text] the closing of the whole or part of the Premises by the order or on the advice of a competent public authority as a result of:
[1367|Body Text] defects in the drains or other sanitary arrangements at the Premises; or
[1368|Body Text] the Premises becoming infested with vermin or pests.
[1369|Body Text] Indemnity Period shall mean the period during which the results of the Business shall be affected as a result of any of the Specified Incidents beginning:
[1370|Body Text] (in the case of Specified Incident 3) with the occurrence or discovery of the Specified Incident; or
[1371|Body Text] (in the case of Specified Incidents 1, 2, 4, 5 and 6) with the date from which the restrictions on the Premises are applied and ending not later than 3 (three) months thereafter.
[1372|Body Text] This Extension covers interruption of or interference with the Business following a Specified Incident which has not resulted in Damage during the Indemnity Period
[1373|Body Text] provided that:
[1374|Body Text] in relation to any claim arising directly or in any way from an occurrence of legionellosis or legionnaires disease at the Premises, the Insured will lose their right to compensation or payment for that claim unless they have ensured compliance at all times with the Health Safety Commission Approved Code of Practice ‘The Prevention and Control of Legionellosis (including legionnaires disease)’ Ref ISBN-0-7176-1772-6 or any supplementary replacement or amending Code of Practice;
[1375|Body Text] the Insurer shall not indemnify the Insured in respect of the costs incurred in cleaning or repair or replacement or recall or checking of property arising from interruption of or interference with the Business following a Specified Incident.
[1376|Body Text] the Insurer shall not indemnify the Insured in respect of any interruption of or interference with the Business after the WHO (World Health Organization) makes the assessment that the specific infectious or contagious disease can be characterised as a pandemic.
[1377|Body Text] Notwithstanding anything contained herein to the contrary for the purposes of this Extension the Communicable Disease Policy Exclusion is deemed not to apply to this Extension.

[1387|Body Text] Payments on account may on application by the Insured and at the Insurer’s discretion be made to the Insured during the Indemnity Period.
[1388|## Heading 3] Professional Accountants

[1390|Body Text] The Insurer will pay to the Insured the reasonable charges payable by the Insured to their professional accountants for producing such particulars or details.
[1391|## Heading 3] Public Utilities

[1393|Body Text] generating station or substation of an electricity supply undertaking;
[1394|Body Text] land based premises of any gas supply undertaking or the premises of any natural gas producer linked directly with the  premises of any gas supply undertaking;
[1395|Body Text] water works or pumping station of any water supply undertaking; and
[1396|Body Text] land based premises of telecommunications services (other than satellite services);
[1397|Body Text] from which the Insured obtains electricity, gas, water or telecommunication services
[1398|Body Text] provided that the Insurer shall not be liable for interruption of or interference with the Business arising from Damage:
[1399|Body Text] to lines, cables or pipes conveying the said supplies;
[1400|Body Text] that does not involve a total cessation of supply for at least 3 (three) consecutive hours;
[1401|Body Text] due to the following causes:
[1402|Body Text] the deliberate act of any supply undertaking of its power to withhold or restrict supply or services;
[1403|Body Text] strikes or any labour or trade dispute;
[1404|Body Text] drought; or
[1405|Body Text] other atmospheric or weather conditions but this shall not exclude an Incident to property caused by such conditions.

[1425|## Heading 3] Public Utilities – Terminal Ends

[1432|Body Text] Service Provider, which processes, maintains, protects or stores the Insured’s Digital Assets, within the United Kingdom;
[1433|Body Text Indent] provided that the Insurer shall not be liable for interruption or interference with the Business arising from Damage:
