[1440|Body Text] Digital Assets shall mean Electronic Data including any Insured or third Party trade secrets, data, designs, processes, records, reports, documents subject to legal privilege or other item that is not available to the general public and Electronic Data carrying intellectual property rights, which is in the Insured’s care, custody or control, including in the custody of outsourcers and independent contractors (provided that it is in the scope/course of their employment or agency contract with the Insured). Digital Assets do not include the physical components of any Computer System including CPU’s, memory, storage devices, storage media, and input/output devices and other peripheral devices and components including but not limited to cable, connectors, fibre optics, wire, power supply units, keyboards, display monitors and audio speakers.
[1441|Body Text] Service Provider shall mean any third Party that is responsible for the processing, maintenance, protection or storage of any Digital Assets pursuant to a written contract directly with the Insured.  A Service Provider does not include any provider of telecommunications services, including internet access.
[1442|## Heading 3] Business interruption Limit
[1443|Normal] It is noted and agreed that the Basis of Settlement provisions
[1444|Normal] under Section 3: Business Interruption “All Risks” are amended as follows solely in respect of the items listed in this Endorsement. All other Definitions, Conditions, Extensions and Exclusions of Section 3 and of the Policy remain unaltered unless expressly stated herein.
[1445|Normal] 1. Insuring Clause
[1446|Normal] Subject to the Flexible Business Interruption Limit stated in paragraph 5 of this Endorsement, the Insurer will indemnify the Insured for the following loss or additional expenditure arising from an Interruption resulting from an Incident during the Indemnity Period:
[1447|Normal] Loss of Income
[1448|Normal] Loss of Gross Profit
[1449|Normal] Loss of Fees
[1450|Normal] Increased Costs of Working
[1451|Normal] Additional Increased Costs of Working
[1452|Normal] Additional Research Expenditure
[1453|Normal] Outstanding Debts
[1454|Normal] For the purposes of this Extension, these items are deemed to be added to Section 3 as insurable heads of cover.
[1455|Normal] All amounts payable collectively shall not exceed the Flexible Business Interruption Limit as shown in the Schedule.
[1456|Normal] 2. Basis of Settlement
[1457|Normal] The amounts payable under this Extension shall be:
[1458|Normal] a. Loss of Income
[1459|Normal] The shortfall between the income that would have been earned during the Indemnity Period had the Incident not occurred and the actual income earned, adjusted for Trends and Variations, and less any savings during the Indemnity Period.
[1460|Normal] b. Loss of Gross Profit
[1461|Normal] The reduction in Gross Profit during the Indemnity Period, calculated by applying the appropriate Gross Profit rate to the reduction in trading results attributable to the Incident, and less any savings during the Indemnity Period.
[1462|Normal] c. Loss of Fees
[1463|Normal] The shortfall between fees that would have been received during the Indemnity Period and the fees actually received, less any savings.
[1464|Normal] d. Increased Costs of Working
[1465|Normal] Additional expenditure necessarily and reasonably incurred for the sole purpose of avoiding or minimising a reduction in Loss of Income, Loss of Gross Profit or Loss of Fees, but not exceeding the loss avoided.
[1466|Normal] e. Additional Increased Costs of Working
[1467|Normal] Additional expenditure necessarily and reasonably incurred beyond that recoverable under sub-paragraph (d), provided it is incurred for the purpose of sustaining the Business following the Incident.
[1468|Normal] f. Additional Research Expenditure
[1469|Normal] Additional expenditure necessarily and reasonably incurred to restore research or development activities interrupted by the Incident.
[1470|Normal] g. Outstanding Debts
[1471|Normal] The amount by which Accounts Receivable or similar receivables become irrecoverable as a direct consequence of the Incident, including necessary and reasonable additional expenditure incurred to reduce such loss.
[1472|Normal] 3. Indemnity Period
[1473|Normal] For the purposes of this Extension, the Indemnity Period applicable to all items listed in paragraph 1 shall be as shown in the Schedule
[1474|Normal] 4. Deleted Provisions
[1475|Normal] The following provisions of the Policy and Section 3 shall not apply to the items insured under this Endorsement:
[1476|Normal] The Average Condition.
[1477|Normal] The Automatic Reinstatement Extension.
[1478|Normal] All other provisions of Section 3 and the Policy remain in full force and effect.
[1479|Normal] 5. Limit of Liability
[1480|Normal] The most the Insurer will pay in total under this Endorsement for all loss and expenditure arising from any one Incident, and in the aggregate during the Period of Insurance, shall be:
[1481|Normal] The Flexible Business Interruption Limit as shown in the Schedule
[1520|## Subtitle] Section 4: Terrorism Section
[1521|## Heading 1] Definitions
[1522|## Heading 3] Computer Systems
[1523|Body Text] A computer or other equipment or component or system or item which processes, stores, transmits or receives Data.
[1524|## Heading 3] Data
[1525|Body Text] Data of any sort whatever, including without limitation tangible or intangible data, and any programs or software, bandwidth, cryptographic keys, databases, documents, domain names or network addresses or anything similar, files, interfaces, metadata, platforms, processing capability, storage media, transaction gateways, user credentials, websites, or any information whatever.
[1526|## Heading 3] Denial of Service Attack
[1527|Body Text] Any actions or instructions constructed or generated with the ability to damage, interfere with or otherwise affect the availability or performance of networks, network services, network connectivity or Computer Systems.
[1528|Body Text] Denial of Service Attacks include, but are not limited to, the generation of excess traffic into network addresses, the exploitation of system or network weaknesses, the generation of excess or non-genuine traffic between and amongst networks and the procurement of such actions or instructions by other Computer Systems.
[1529|## Heading 3] Event
[1530|Body Text] All individual losses arising in respect of a continuous period of 72 (seventy-two) hours of which the proximate cause is the same act of Terrorism.
[1531|## Heading 3] Nuclear Installation
[1532|Body Text] Any installation of such class or description as may be prescribed by regulation through statutory instruments made by the relevant Secretary of State from time to time, being an installation designed or adapted for:
[1533|Body Text] the production or use of atomic energy;
[1534|Body Text] the carrying out of any process that is preparatory or ancillary to the production or use of atomic energy and which involves or is capable of causing the emission of ionising radiations; or
[1535|Body Text] the storage processing or disposal of nuclear fuel or of bulk quantities of other radioactive matter being matter that has been produced or irradiated in the course of the production or use of nuclear fuel.
[1536|## Heading 3] Nuclear Reactor
[1537|Body Text] Any plant (including any machinery, equipment or appliance whether affixed to land or not) designed or adapted for the production of atomic energy by a fission process in which a controlled chain reaction can be maintained without any additional source of neutrons.
[1538|## Heading 3] Private Individual
[1539|Body Text] Any person other than:
[1540|Body Text] a trustee or body of trustees where insurance is arranged under the terms of a trust except where such trustee or body of trustees occupy the Premises as their own private residence; or
[1541|Body Text] a person who owns Residential Property for the purposes of their business as a sole trader except where such sole trader occupies the Premises as his own private residence.
[1542|Body Text] This definition of Private Individual shall also include 2 (two) or more persons where insurance is arranged in their several names or the title of the Insured includes the name of a bank or building society or other financial institution, or for the purpose of noting their interest in the Property Insured.
[1543|## Heading 3] Property Insured
[1544|Body Text] As defined in the relevant Sections.
[1545|## Heading 3] Residential Property
[1546|Body Text] Houses and blocks of flats and other dwellings insured in the name of a Private Individual; and
[1547|Body Text] Household goods and personal effects of every description.
[1548|Body Text] Where the property is occupied part commercially and part residentially and is insured in the name of a Private Individual, this property shall not be deemed to be a Residential Property provided that the commercially occupied proportion of the property exceeds 20% (twenty percent).
[1549|## Heading 3] Territorial Limits
[1550|Body Text] England, Scotland and Wales but not the territorial seas adjacent thereto as defined by the Territorial Seas Act 1987.
[1551|## Heading 3] Terrorism
[1552|Body Text] Acts of persons acting on behalf of or in connection with any organisation which carries out activities directed towards the overthrowing or influencing by force or violence of Her Majesty’s government in the United Kingdom or any other government de jure or de facto.
[1553|## Heading 3] Virus or Similar Mechanism
[1554|Body Text] Program code, programming instruction or any set of instructions constructed with the purpose and ability, or purposely used to damage, interfere with, adversely affect, infiltrate or monitor computer programs, Computer Systems, Data or operations, whether involving self-replication or not.
[1555|Body Text] This definition of Virus or Similar Mechanism includes but is not limited to trojan horses, worms and logic bombs and the exploitation of bugs or vulnerabilities in a computer program to damage, interfere with, adversely affect, infiltrate or monitor as above.
[1556|## Heading 3] The Cover
[1557|Body Text] The Insurer will cover Damage to:
[1558|Body Text] Property Insured or interruption of the Business;
[1559|Body Text] Money; and
[1560|Body Text] property in transit;
[1561|Body Text] anywhere in the Territorial Limits as a result of a Terrorism Event during the Period of Insurance
[1562|Body Text] provided that:
[1563|Body Text] the liability of the Insurer shall not exceed the relevant limits or Sums Insured stated in the Schedule applicable to the:
[1564|Body Text] Business “All Risks” Section;
[1565|Body Text] Property & Equipment “All Risks” Section;
[1566|Body Text] Business Interruption “All Risks” Section;
[1567|Body Text] Information Technology Section;
[1568|Body Text] Money Section;
[1569|Body Text] Goods in Transit Section; or
[1570|Body Text] Production Indemnity “All Risks” Section.
[1571|Body Text] the cover provided by this Section is not subject to any of the exclusions of this Policy except:
[1572|Body Text] the exclusions stated below; or
[1573|Body Text] excluded property under this Policy.
[1574|## Heading 1] Exclusions
[1575|Body Text] This Section does not cover:
[1576|Body Text] loss or Damage, or interruption or interference as a consequence of Damage:
[1577|Body Text] to any Residential Property insured in the name of a Private Individual;
[1578|Body Text] to any Nuclear Installation or Nuclear Reactor and all fixtures and fittings situated thereon or attached thereto and all pipes, wires, cables, drains or other conduits or service media of any description that are fixed or connected to or in any way serve such Nuclear Installation or Nuclear Reactor; or
[1579|Body Text] occasioned by riot or civil commotion, war, invasion, act of foreign enemy, hostilities (whether war be declared or not), civil war, rebellion, revolution, insurrection or military or usurped power;
[1580|Body Text] any loss whatsoever directly or in any way caused by or contributed to  or arising from or occasioned by or resulting from:
[1581|Body Text] Damage to or the destruction of any Computer System; or
[1582|Body Text] any alteration, modification, distortion, erasure or corruption of Data;
[1583|Body Text] in each case whether the property of the Insured or not where such Damage is directly or in any way caused by or contributed to or arising from or occasioned by or resulting from Virus or Similar Mechanism or Hacking or Phishing or Denial of Service Attack;
[1584|Body Text] provided that Damage otherwise falling within this Exclusion 2 will not be treated as excluded by this Exclusion solely to the extent that such Damage is caused by remote digital interference with Computer Systems which emanates from either within or outside the Territorial Limits;
[1585|Body Text] and results directly from fire, explosion, flood, escape of water from any tank, apparatus or pipe (including any sprinkler system), impact of aircraft or any aerial devices or articles dropped from them, impact of any sea-going or water-going vessel or of any vehicle whatsoever or of any goods or cargo carried in or on such vessel or vehicle, destruction of, damage to or movement of Buildings or structures, plant or machinery other than any Computer System; and
[1586|Body Text] comprises:
[1587|Body Text] the cost of reinstatement, replacement or repair in respect of damage to or destruction of Property Insured; or
[1588|Body Text] the amount of business interruption loss suffered directly by the Insured itself by way of loss of or reduction in profits, revenue or turnover or increased cost of working as a direct result of Damage to Property Insured or as a direct result of denial, prevention or hindrance of access to or use of the Property Insured by reason of an act of Terrorism causing Damage to other property within 1 (one) mile of the Property Insured to which access is affected;
[1589|Body Text] and is not proximately caused by an Act of Terrorism in relation to which the relevant organisation or any persons acting on behalf of or in connection with that organisation are controlled by, acting on behalf of or part of any de jure or de facto government of any nation, country or state;
[1590|Body Text] "Property Insured" for the purposes of this proviso shall exclude:
[1591|Body Text] any money, currency, electronic cryptographic or virtual currency including Bitcoin or anything similar, negotiable or non-negotiable instruments, financial securities or any other financial instrument of any sort whatever; and
[1592|Body Text] any Data;
[1593|Body Text] notwithstanding the exclusion of Data from Property Insured, to the extent that Damage to Property Insured within the meaning of sub-paragraph (ii) above in any way results from any alteration, modification, distortion, erasure or corruption of Data, because the occurrence of one or more of the matters referred to in sub-paragraph () above results directly or in any way from any alteration, modification, distortion, erasure or corruption of Data, that shall not prevent cost or business interruption loss directly resulting from Damage to such Property Insured and otherwise falling within sub-paragraphs () and (ii) above from being recoverable under this Section.
[1594|Body Text] In no other circumstances than the previous sentence, however, will any loss or losses directly or in any way caused by, contributed to or arising from or occasioned by or resulting from any alteration, modification, distortion, erasure or corruption of Data be recoverable under this Section;
[1595|Body Text] for the avoidance of doubt, the burden of proof shall be on the Insurer to prove or establish all the matters referred to in sub-paragraphs () and (ii) above.
[1596|## Heading 1] Conditions
[1597|## Heading 3] Adjustable Premiums
[1598|Body Text] Any terms in this Policy that provide for adjustment of premium based upon declarations on expiry or during the Period of Insurance do not apply to this Section.
[1599|## Heading 3] Automatic Reinstatement
[1600|Body Text] All or part of the Sum Insured that is reduced by the amount of any payment as a result of Damage shall be reinstated, upon payment by the Insured of the additional premium charged by the Insurer therefor proportionately for the period between the date of the Damage to the date of expiry of the Period of Insurance.
[1601|## Heading 3] Burden of Proof
[1602|Body Text] If the Insurer alleges that any Damage, cost or expense is not covered by this Section the burden of proving the contrary shall be upon the Insured.
[1603|## Heading 3] Further Claims Procedure
[1604|Body Text] Any claim or proceedings or any Damage or loss of or interruption to the Business which might give rise to a claim must be notified in writing as soon as practicable to the Insurer.
[1605|Body Text] The Insured must submit a detailed statement of any claim within 30 (thirty) days of the happening of any Damage or interruption or such further time as the Insurer may allow in writing.
[1606|## Heading 3] Long Term Agreement
[1607|Body Text] Any  agreement or undertaking applying to this Policy shall not apply to this Section.
[1608|## Heading 3] Period of Insurance
[1609|Body Text] The Period of Insurance shall be as stated in the Schedule and shall not exceed 12 (twelve) months for any one period.

[1614|## Heading 3] Geographical Limits
[1615|Body Text] The United Kingdom.

[1617|Body Text] From the point of embarkation onto a conveyance at the point of final departure to an offshore rig, offshore platform or offshore installation until disembarkation from a conveyance onto land following return from an offshore rig, offshore platform or offshore installation.
[1618|## Heading 3] The Cover
[1619|Body Text] The Insurer agrees to indemnify or compensate the Insured for the Insured’s liability to pay:
[1620|Body Text] Compensation for Bodily Injury caused to an Employee during the Period of Insurance and arising out of and in the course of his employment by the Insured in connection with the Business within or whilst working temporarily outside the Geographical Limits; and
[1621|Body Text] Costs and Expenses
[1622|Body Text] provided that:
[1623|Body Text] the Compensation payable by the Insurer under this Section is in accordance with the legal obligations relating to compulsory insurance of liability to employees but the Insured shall repay to the Insurer all sums paid by the Insurer which the Insurer would not have been liable to pay but for the provisions of such law; and
[1624|Body Text] the proceedings in relation to Bodily Injury are brought in a court of law in the United Kingdom.

[1633|Body Text] At the Insured’s request this Extension covers the Insured and any Employee or director of the Insured against the legal fees and expenses incurred with the Insurer’s prior written approval in defending any of them in respect of a prosecution within the definition of Criminal Prosecution Defence Costs and subject to the specified sub-limits, for an offence alleged to be first committed during the Period of Insurance in connection with the Business in respect of a liability that may form the subject of Compensation under this Section.
[1634|## Heading 3] Data Protection Act
[1635|Body Text] This Extension covers the Insured’s liability to pay Compensation in respect of damage or distress under sections 168 and 169 of the Data Protection Act 2018 or material or non-material damage under Article 82 of the General Data Protection Regulation EU Regulation 2016/679 (together “the Data Privacy Legislation”) to an Employee and the Employee is entitled to compensation under the Data Privacy Legislation, and Costs and Expenses
[1636|Body Text] provided that:
[1637|Body Text] an offence is first committed by the Insured during the Period of Insurance in connection with the Business;
[1638|Body Text] this Extension shall not apply in respect of:
[1639|Body Text] the cost of replacing, reinstating, rectifying or erasing any personal data;
[1640|Body Text] claims which arise out of circumstances notified to previous insurers or known to the Insured at the commencement of this insurance; or
[1641|Body Text] liability for which compensation is provided under any other insurance.
[1642|Body Text] any cost relating to the investigation of a data breach, or obligation to report a data breach to the Information Commissioner’s Office or other appropriate supervisory authority or regulatory body or to data subjects;
[1643|Body Text] liability arising from any deliberate act or omission of any party entitled to indemnity or Compensation under this Policy who knew at the relevant time that it would or could result in liability or compensation under the Data Privacy Legislation; or
[1644|Body Text] any person who is not an Employee at the date of the offence; or
[1645|Body Text] claims, investigations or prosecutions instituted against the Insured outside the courts of the United Kingdom;
[1646|Body Text] the Insured has taken all reasonable care to comply with the provisions of the Data Privacy Legislation; and
[1647|Body Text] the Insurer’s liability for such Extension shall be limited to GBP 250,000 (two hundred and fifty thousand pounds sterling) any one event giving rise to Compensation in total for all Employees affected by such offence.
[1648|## Heading 3] Indemnity to Principals
[1649|Body Text] This Extension covers any principal as though he was also the Insured in respect of liability arising out of Bodily Injury resulting from the performance of work by the Insured but only to the extent required by any contract or agreement entered into for the performance of such work
[1650|Body Text] provided that the principal shall observe, fulfil and be subject to the Section terms, Conditions, limitations and Exclusions and this Policy’s Conditions and Exclusions.
[1651|## Heading 3] Unsatisfied Court Judgments
[1652|Body Text] This Extension covers judgments for damages obtained by an Employee in respect of Bodily Injury caused during the Period of Insurance and arising out of and in the course of his employment in the Business against any company or individual in any court, if remaining unsatisfied in whole or in part 6 (six) months after the date of such judgment, the Insurer will pay to the Employee or the personal representatives of the Employee at the request of the Insured the amount of any such damages and any awarded costs to the extent that they remain unsatisfied
[1653|Body Text] provided that:
[1654|Body Text] there is no appeal outstanding; and
[1655|Body Text] the Employee or his personal representatives assign the judgment and all rights arising out of it to the Insurer.

For the purposes of this Exclusion the expressions “vehicle”, “use” and “road” shall have the same meaning as in Part VI of the Road Traffic Act 1988.

[1724|## Heading 3] Legionella Liability
[1725|Body Text] The Insurer agrees to indemnify or compensate the Insured against legal liability for Compensation and Costs and Expenses in respect of Bodily Injury caused by legionellosis arising out of the Business and occurring during the Period of Insurance
[1726|Body Text] provided that:
[1727|Body Text] in connection with any premises owned, hired or rented by the Insured that the Insured complies with the Health and Safety Commissions Approved Code of Practice - Legionnaires' Disease: The control of legionella bacteria in water systems - Ref ISBN-0-7176-1772-6 or any amending Code of Practice;
[1728|Body Text] the Insurer may at any time pay the Limit of Liability (less any sums already paid) or any lesser amount for which a claim can be settled.  The Insurer will then relinquish control of such claim and be under no further liability in respect thereof;
[1729|Body Text] all claims arising out of the same isolated, repeated or continuing incidence of legionellosis shall be deemed to have occurred during the Period of Insurance; and
[1730|Body Text] the Limit of Liability applicable to this Extension shall be inclusive of Costs and Expenses and not in addition.
[1731|Body Text] The Compensation provided by this Extension shall not apply to legal liability where such liability has been accepted by contract or other agreement unless liability would have attached in the absence of such contract or agreement.
[1732|## Heading 3] Motor Vehicle Contingent Liability
[1733|Body Text] This Extension covers the Insured for liability arising from Bodily Injury or Damage to material property arising from the ownership, possession or use of mechanically propelled vehicles used in connection with the Business of the Insured and that are neither the property of or provided by the Insured nor being driven by the Insured, but only to the extent where there is no entitlement to compensation under any motor policy or other more specific insurance
[1734|Body Text] provided that:
[1735|Body Text] the Insurer shall not be liable in respect of Damage to such vehicle or to goods conveyed therein or thereon and shall compensate the Insured and no other person; and
[1736|Body Text] the Insurer shall not be liable whilst such vehicle is being driven by any person who to the knowledge of the Insured does not hold a licence to drive such vehicle unless such person has held and is not disqualified from holding or obtaining such a licence.

[1751|## Heading 1] Optional Extension
[1752|Body Text] (Operative only if stated in the Schedule)
[1753|Body Text] Inclusion of United States of America/Canada Jurisdiction — Non-Manual Activities Only
[1754|Body Text] Operative only if stated in the Schedule
[1755|Body Text] For the purposes of this Optional Extension only, the following definitions apply:
[1756|Body Text] Manual Work means any work, service or activity involving physical labour, installation, erection, dismantling, assembly, construction, alteration, repair, maintenance, servicing, cleaning, catering, stewarding, security, loading, unloading, lifting, carrying, rigging, de-rigging, operation or handling of plant, machinery, production equipment, staging, sets, scenery, temporary structures, lighting rigs, sound rigs, camera cranes, vehicles or other equipment, or any work at height, work involving heat, fire, pyrotechnics, special effects, stunts, weapons, animals, waterborne activities, aerial activities, underground activities or other hazardous activity.
[1757|Body Text] Manual Work does not include ordinary clerical, administrative, management, consultancy, advisory, design, editorial, creative, marketing, sales, account handling, scheduling, booking, rights clearance, production management, post-production, office-based or computer-based activities.
[1758|Body Text] Manual Work also does not include Low Risk Filming and Musical Performance Activities.
[1759|Body Text] Low Risk Filming and Musical Performance Activities means filming, photography, broadcasting, recording, presenting, interviewing, podcasting, rehearsing, singing, playing a musical instrument or other performance activity of a non-hazardous nature, provided that such activity does not involve:
[1760|Body Text] (a) stunts, staged fighting, weapons, firearms, explosives, pyrotechnics, fire or hazardous special effects;
(b) aerial, underwater, marine, underground, remote-location or other hazardous activities;
(c) work at height, other than ordinary access to a stage, platform or performance area intended for that purpose;
(d) the erection, dismantling, rigging, de-rigging, installation, repair, maintenance or operation of staging, scaffolding, temporary structures, lighting rigs, sound rigs, camera cranes or similar equipment;
(e) the operation of motorised vehicles, plant, machinery, cranes, hoists, forklift trucks or lifting equipment;
(f) crowd control, door supervision, stewarding or security activities; or
(g) physical labour or manual handling other than that ordinarily incidental to the filming, recording, rehearsal or musical performance itself.
[1761|Body Text] Non-Manual Activities means activities carried out by or on behalf of the Insured in the course of the Business which are primarily clerical, administrative, managerial, professional, consultancy, advisory, design, editorial, creative, marketing, sales, account handling, scheduling, booking, rights clearance, production management, post-production, office-based or computer-based in nature and which do not involve Manual Work. Non-Manual Activities include Low Risk Filming and Musical Performance Activities.
[1762|Body Text] The Worldwide Jurisdiction excluding the United States of America/Canada Condition is deleted and of no further effect, but only in respect of any claim arising out of Non-Manual Activities.
[1763|Body Text] The insurance by this Section extends to indemnify the Insured for legal proceedings brought or originating in the United States of America/Canada or in any territory within their jurisdiction, but only in respect of any claim arising out of Non-Manual Activities.
[1764|Body Text] This Optional Extension does not apply to any claim arising out of, based upon or attributable to Manual Work, unless the activity falls within the definition of  Filming and Musical Performance Activities.
[1765|Body Text] Provided that:
[1766|Body Text] () the liability of the Insurer in respect of Compensation and Costs and Expenses shall not exceed the limit stated in the Schedule;
[1767|Body Text] (ii) the amount payable under this Optional Extension in respect of each and every claim shall be reduced by the amount stated in the Schedule as the Excess;
[1768|Body Text] (iii) the Insurer shall not be liable for punitive or exemplary damages;
[1769|Body Text] (iv) the Insurer shall not be liable for claims arising from any mould or fungi or its spores, bacteria, yeasts, mildew, algae, mycotoxins or any other metabolic products, enzymes or protein secreted whether toxic or otherwise;
[1770|Body Text] (v) the Insurer shall not be liable for claims arising from the sale or supply of contraceptives;
[1771|Body Text] (vi) the Insurer shall not be liable for:
[1772|Body Text] (a) any liability arising out of the discharge, dispersal, release or escape of smoke, vapours, soot, fumes, acids, alkalis, toxic chemicals, liquids or gases, waste materials or other irritants, contaminants or pollutants into or upon land, atmosphere or any watercourse or body of water; or
[1773|Body Text] (b) any cost or expense arising out of any governmental demand or request that an Insured test for, assess, monitor, clean up, remove, contain, treat, detoxify or neutralise any irritants, contaminants or pollutants;
[1774|Body Text] and the Insurer shall not have the duty to defend any claim or suit seeking to impose such costs, expenses, liability for such damages or any other relief;
[1775|Body Text] (vii) the Insurer shall not be liable for any claim arising out of any work, contract, project, event, production or performance where Manual Work caused or materially contributed to the injury, damage, loss, liability or expense giving rise to the claim; and
[1776|Body Text] (viii) the Insurer and the Insured agree that the premium for this inclusion will be calculated accordingly.

[1778|Body Text] This Section shall not apply to liability or Compensation in respect of or arising out of:
[1779|## Heading 3] Abuse
[1780|Body Text] the mental or physical intentional or neglectful mistreatment of a person which results in Bodily Injury including any act which amounts to an offence under the Sexual Offences Act 2003.
[1781|## Heading 3] Advice and Professional Negligence
[1782|Body Text] advice, design, plan, formula, specification or omission to perform a professional duty provided for a fee or in circumstances where a fee would normally be charged.
[1783|## Heading 3] Asbestos
[1784|Body Text] asbestos or related in any way to asbestos or asbestos fibres or particles or any derivatives of asbestos or any materials containing such in any form whatsoever.
[1785|Body Text] However, this Exclusion will not apply in respect of a claim for Bodily Injury against the Insured arising out of exposure to asbestos fibres, caused by a fire or explosion which occurs during the Period of Insurance, subject to a maximum Insurer’s liability of GBP 500,000 (five hundred thousand pounds sterling)
[1786|## Heading 3] Contractual Liability
[1787|Body Text] or attaching by virtue of any contract or agreement (whether written, oral, implied or otherwise) but which would not have attached in the absence of such agreement unless the Insurer has approved such contract or agreement by endorsement.
[1788|## Heading 3] Defective Workmanship
[1789|Body Text] the cost of rectifying defective work carried out by or on behalf of the Insured.
[1790|## Heading 3] Employees
[1791|Body Text] Bodily Injury sustained by an Employee and arising out of and in the course of his employment by the Insured.
[1792|## Heading 3] Medical Malpractice
[1793|Body Text] Bodily Injury arising from an act or omission in the provision of or failure to provide Healthcare as defined in this Exclusion.
[1794|Body Text] For the purposes of this Exclusion the words:
[1795|Body Text] Healthcare shall mean healthcare (but not First Aid) rendered by members of the healthcare and allied services or by others consequent on decisions or judgements made by such members;
[1796|Body Text] Such members shall include:
[1797|Body Text] medical and dental practitioners;
[1798|Body Text] nurses;
[1799|Body Text] midwives;
[1800|Body Text] pharmacists;
[1801|Body Text] professions allied to medicine;
[1802|Body Text] care assistants and nursing auxiliaries;
[1803|Body Text] ambulance personnel;
[1804|Body Text] laboratory technicians; or
[1805|Body Text] social workers.
[1806|Body Text] First Aid shall mean emergency care (other than planned emergency treatment for specific individuals) given immediately to an injured or sick person by any director, partner or Employee of the Insured in the course of carrying out their duties when undertaking the Business.
[1807|## Heading 3] Pollution
[1808|Body Text] Pollution unless such Pollution is caused by a sudden, identifiable, unintended and unexpected incident which occurs in its entirety at a specific time and place during the Period of Insurance.
[1809|## Heading 3] Products
[1810|Body Text] any of the Insured’s Products (other than food or drink for consumption on the Premises).
[1811|## Heading 3] Terrorism
[1812|Body Text] Terrorism unless the occurrence giving rise to the claim takes place wholly within the United Kingdom.
[1813|## Heading 3] Vehicles, Vessels or Craft
[1814|Body Text] Bodily Injury or Damage to material property arising from the ownership, possession or use by or on behalf of the Insured of:
[1815|Body Text] any mechanically propelled vehicle used in circumstances where insurance or security is required by law or where compensation is provided under any motor policy or other more specific insurance provided that this Exclusion shall not apply to:
[1816|Body Text] the loading or unloading of any vehicle or trailer or delivery or collection of goods in connection with any vehicle or trailer;
[1817|Body Text] such vehicle whilst the same is being used as a tool of trade.
[1818|Body Text] any vessel or craft or oil rig made or intended to float on or in or travel through water or air or space or the loading or unloading of such vessel or craft other than:
[1819|Body Text] any watercraft owned by others and used by the Insured for Business entertainment not exceeding 30 (thirty) metres in length; or
[1820|Body Text] non-powered watercraft barges and motor launches not exceeding 30 (thirty) metres in length;
[1821|Body Text] whilst on inland waterways or 3 (three) miles offshore.
[1822|## Heading 1] Conditions
[1823|## Heading 3] Terrorism
[1824|Body Text] The liability of the Insurer for all Compensation and Costs and Expenses arising out of Terrorism within the United Kingdom shall not exceed the limit stated in the Schedule to this Section.
[1825|## Heading 3] Worldwide Jurisdiction
[1826|Body Text] (Excluding the United States of America/Canada)
[1827|Body Text] The indemnity provided by this Section shall apply to judgements against the Insured in any court in the world, excluding judgements obtained in the courts or under the laws of the United States of America, its territories (including Puerto Rico) or possessions, or Canada, or orders obtained in the said courts for the enforcement of foreign judgements whether by way of reciprocal agreements or otherwise (“Foreign Judgements”). The premium for this insurance has been calculated accordingly and no consideration has been paid in respect of liabilities that may arise under any “Foreign Judgements”.
[1828|## Heading 3] Hazardous Activities
[1829|Body Text] It is a condition precedent to liability under this Policy that prior to the Insured undertaking or arranging any activities involving a hazardous location or of a hazardous nature including the use of pyrotechnics or special effects which produce a naked flame or involve stunt work, heat work or height work, a risk assessment must be carried out by the Insured for each such activity and that such risk assessment must be accepted by the Insurers in the event that any residual risk rating, after the application of control measures, remains medium to high (Amber or Red).
[1830|## Heading 3] Heat Work Condition
[1831|Body Text] The Insurer shall not be liable to indemnify or compensate the Insured in respect of liability arising from or caused by Heat Work undertaken by the Insured away from premises owned by or leased or rented to the Insured unless the following precautions are taken at all times:
[1832|Body Text] a responsible worker is appointed to facilitate compliance with all requirements of these conditions;
[1833|Body Text] prior permission from the occupier or owner of the site has been granted for Heat Work to take place and suitable and adequate fire extinguishing appliances are provided at the point of use. Suitable and adequate fire extinguishing appliances shall as a minimum mean a 9 (nine) litre water or a 2 (two) kilogram multi-purpose fire extinguisher;
[1834|Body Text] all workers are aware of the location of fire alarms and firefighting equipment provided on site which shall be ready for operation at the time Heat Work is undertaken;
[1835|Body Text] the item being worked on and the area where Heat Work is taking place including the other side of any ceiling, floor, wall or partition and within and on the other side of any tank, pipe, drum or apparatus are checked to ensure that no combustible materials or inflammable liquids or gas is in danger of ignition directly or through conducted heat;
[1836|Body Text] all combustible materials or inflammable liquids or gases in the vicinity of where Heat Work is taking place, other than gas or fuel connected to the Heat Work equipment, shall be removed to a point at least 8 (eight) metres from the area where the Heat Work is taking place. Any combustible material or inflammable liquid or gases which cannot be reasonably moved shall be covered and fully protected by overlapping sheets or screens of non-combustible material. Where the nature of materials or liquids or gases cannot be properly verified by a suitably qualified person as non-combustible or non- they must be assumed as combustible or inflammable and all stated precautions shall be carried out in full;
[1837|Body Text] all equipment involved in Heat Work is to be examined prior to use and any defects found are to be repaired or replaced prior to Heat Work taking place;
[1838|Body Text] all equipment involved in Heat Work is to be attended at all times whilst Heat Work is taking place and only used in accordance with the manufacturer’s instructions and by a worker who is trained and experienced in their use;
[1839|Body Text] whilst Heat Work involving bitumen heaters is being undertaken the bitumen heaters must be kept in the open or if within a building or on a roof then placed on a surface of non-combustible material;
[1840|Body Text] the area where the Heat Work has been undertaken including on the other side of any floor, wall, ceiling or partition and within and on the other side of any tank, pipe, drum or apparatus is to be examined immediately following the completion of Heat Work and then at regular intervals of at least 1 (one) hour to ensure that there is no risk of fire.
[1841|Body Text] For the purposes of this Condition “heat work” shall mean any work undertaken by the Insured involving the use of:
[1842|Body Text] grinding wheels, cutting discs, angle grinders, electric, oxy-acetylene or other welding or cutting equipment, blow torches, blow lamps or flame guns or hot air guns in each case howsoever powered or driven including all gas or fuel containers and hose connections; or
[1843|Body Text] bitumen heaters including all vessels for the heating of tar, bitumen or bituminous compounds
[1846|## Subtitle] Section 7: Products Liability Section
[1847|## Heading 3] The Cover
[1848|Body Text] The Insurer agrees to indemnify or compensate the Insured for all sums that the Insured shall become legally liable to pay as Compensation in respect of accidental:
[1849|Body Text] Bodily Injury to any person; or
[1850|Body Text] Damage to material property not belonging to or in the custody or under the control of the Insured or any Employee;
[1851|Body Text] occurring during the Period of Insurance and arising out of any of the Insured’s Products but solely in respect of Products sold in or from the United Kingdom.
[1852|Body Text] The Insurer shall also indemnify or compensate the Insured in respect of Costs and Expenses. Costs and Expenses are payable in addition to the Limit of Liability other than in respect of claims made or brought in the United States of America or Canada where the Limit of Liability will be inclusive of Costs and Expenses.
[1853|## Heading 1] Extensions
[1854|## Heading 3] Criminal Prosecution Defence Costs
[1855|Body Text] At the Insured’s request this Extension covers the Insured and any Employee or director of the Insured against the legal fees and expenses incurred with the Insurer’s prior written approval in defending any of them in respect of a prosecution under the Acts set out in the definition of Criminal Prosecution Defence Costs and subject to the specified sub-limits, for an offence alleged to be first committed during the Period of Insurance in connection with the Business in respect of a liability that may form the subject of Compensation under this Section.
[1856|## Heading 3] Cross Liabilities
[1857|Body Text] Where more than one party is named as the Insured, each party will be indemnified as though they were individually insured
[1858|Body Text] provided that:
[1859|Body Text] the total liability of the Insurer shall not exceed the limit stated in the Schedule to this Section;
[1860|Body Text] this Extension shall not apply to liability for which compensation is or would be granted but for the existence of this insurance under any employers’ liability insurance; and
[1861|Body Text] this Extension shall not apply to liability arising directly or in any way in connection with Damage to premises (including contents) the occupancy of which is shared between 2 (two) or more parties named as the Insured.
[1862|## Heading 1] Optional Extension
[1863|Body Text] (Operative only if stated in the Schedule)
[1864|Body Text] Inclusion of United States of America / Canada Jurisdiction
[1865|Body Text] the Worldwide Jurisdiction (excluding the United States of America/Canada) Condition is deleted and of no further effect;
[1866|Body Text] the North American Exports Exclusion is deleted and of no further effect;
[1867|Body Text] the insurance by this Section extends to indemnify the Insured for legal proceedings brought or originating in the United States of America/Canada or in any territory within their jurisdiction;
[1868|Body Text] provided that:
[1869|Body Text] the liability of the Insurer in respect of Compensation and Costs and Expenses shall not exceed the limit stated in the Schedule;
[1870|Body Text] the Insurer shall not be liable for the amount stated in the Schedule to this Section as the Excess;
[1871|Body Text] the Insurer shall not be liable for punitive or exemplary damages;
[1872|Body Text] the Insurer shall not be liable for claims arising from any mould or fungi or its spores, bacteria, yeasts, mildew, algae, mycotoxins or any other metabolic products, enzymes or protein secreted whether toxic or otherwise;
[1873|Body Text] the Insurer shall not be liable for claims arising from the sale or supply of contraceptives;
[1874|Body Text] the Insurer shall not be liable for:
[1875|Body Text] any liability arising out of the discharge, dispersal, release or escape of smoke, vapours, soot, fumes, acids, alkalis, toxic chemicals, liquids or gases, waste materials or other irritants, contaminants or pollutants into or upon land, atmosphere or any water course or body of water;
[1876|Body Text] any cost or expense arising out of any governmental demand or request that an Insured test for, assess, monitor, clean up, remove, contain, treat, detoxify or neutralise any irritants, contaminants or pollutants;
[1877|Body Text] and the Insurer shall not have the duty to defend any claim or suit seeking to impose such costs, expense, liability for such damages or any other relief;
[1878|Body Text] The Insurer and the Insured agree that the premium for this inclusion will be calculated accordingly.

[1914|## Subtitle] Section 8: Money Section
[1915|## Heading 1] Sub-Section 1 - Money
[1916|## Heading 1] Definitions
[1917|## Heading 3] Non-Negotiable Money
[1918|Body Text] Crossed cheques, crossed giro cheques, crossed bankers’ drafts, crossed giro drafts, crossed postal and crossed money orders, national savings, certificates, premium bonds, unexpired units in franking machines, stamped national insurance cards, credit card sales vouchers, debit card sales vouchers, bills of exchange, VAT purchase invoices, all belonging to the Insured or for which the Insured has accepted responsibility.
[1919|## Heading 3] Situation(s)
[1920|Body Text] In transit directly to or from the Premises and bank;
[1921|Body Text] In the bank night safe and subsequently within the bank premises until at the bank’s risk;
[1922|Body Text] At any of the Insured’s contract sites during Business Hours;
[1923|Body Text] In the homes of the Insured or any partner, director or Employee of the Insured; or
[1924|Body Text] In the Premises;
[1925|Body Text] anywhere within the United Kingdom.
[1926|## Heading 3] The Cover
[1927|Body Text] The Insurer agrees to indemnify or compensate the Insured during the Period of Insurance against:
[1928|Body Text] Damage to Money;
[1929|Body Text] Damage to:
[1930|Body Text] any safe, strongroom or franking machine;
[1931|Body Text] any container, money waistcoat or money belt whilst being used for carrying Money;
[1932|Body Text] as a result of theft or attempted theft of Money unless such cost is more specifically insured
[1933|Body Text] clothing, personal effects and personal Money belonging to the Insured or any partner, director or Employee of the Insured resulting from an assault in an attempt to steal Money;
[1934|Body Text] occurring in the Situation(s).
[1935|## Heading 1] Extension
[1936|## Heading 3] Loss of Keys
[1937|Body Text] This Sub-Section covers the cost of replacement keys or lock mechanisms of safes or strongrooms with the consent of the Insurer following theft of keys by force or violence.
[1938|## Heading 1] Exclusions
[1939|Body Text] This Sub-Section does not cover any:
[1940|Body Text] loss resulting from the use of any form of payment which proves to be counterfeit, false, fraudulent, invalid, uncollectable or irrecoverable for any reason;
[1941|Body Text] loss or shortage arising from fraud or dishonesty of any Employee of the Insured:
[1942|Body Text] unless discovered within 7 (seven) working days after its occurrence; or
[1943|Body Text] covered by a fidelity guarantee insurance.
[1944|Body Text] loss resulting directly or in any way from forgery, fraudulent alteration, substitution, use of a computer or electronic transfer;
[1945|Body Text] loss resulting from a safe or strongroom being opened by a key left on the Premises out of Business Hours;
[1946|Body Text] loss or shortage due to errors or omissions in receipts, payments or accountancy, depreciation or currency fluctuations;
[1947|Body Text] Consequential Loss;
[1948|Body Text] loss resulting from an Unattended Vehicle; or
[1949|Body Text] Damage to any machine that uses coins, notes or tokens.
[1950|## Heading 1] Conditions
[1951|## Heading 3] Carryings Condition
[1952|Body Text] It is a condition precedent to liability under this Policy that when Money (other than Non-Negotiable Money) is in transit:
[1953|Body Text] by the Insured’s own Employees:
[1954|Body Text] up to GBP 2,000 (two thousand pounds sterling), it shall be accompanied at all times by at least 1 (one) responsible able-bodied Employee;
[1955|Body Text] up to GBP 5,000 (five thousand pounds sterling) but in excess of GBP 2,000 (two thousand pounds sterling), it shall be accompanied at all times by at least 2 (two) responsible able-bodied Employees; and
[1956|Body Text] up to GBP 10,000 (ten thousand pounds sterling) but in excess of GBP 5,000 (five thousand pounds sterling), it shall be accompanied at all times by at least 3 (three) responsible able-bodied Employees; and
[1957|Body Text] in excess of GBP 10,000 (ten thousand pounds sterling), it shall be carried by a professional security company.
[1958|## Heading 3] Contract with a Security Company
[1959|Body Text] If the Insured enters into a contract with a professional security company for the transport of Money whereby that security company is liable for any losses, and any losses occur which the Insured is unable to recover from the security company for any reason either in part or in full, then the Insurer will compensate the Insured for any unrecoverable amount.
[1960|## Heading 3] Records
[1961|Body Text] The Insured shall keep a complete record of Money in the Situation(s) and such record shall be kept in a place other than in a safe or strongroom containing Money.
[1962|## Heading 1] Sub-Section 2 – Personal Assault
[1963|## Heading 1] Definitions
[1964|## Heading 3] Insured Person
[1965|Body Text] The Insured, and any partner, director or Employee of the Insured aged between 16 (sixteen) and 70 (seventy) years at the commencement of this Policy.
[1966|Body Text] Loss of Use of One or More Limbs
[1967|Body Text] in the case of a lower limb loss by physical severance of each and every toe through or above the metatarsophalangeal joints or permanent total loss of use of an entire leg or foot;
[1968|Body Text] in the case of an upper limb loss by physical severance of the entire 4 (four) fingers through or above the metacarpophalangeal joints or permanent total loss of use of an entire arm or hand.
[1969|## Heading 3] Medical Expenses
[1970|Body Text] Expenses necessarily incurred by the Insured Person for medical, surgical, manipulative massage, therapeutic X-ray or nursing treatment including the cost of medical supplies and ambulance hire.
[1971|## Heading 3] Permanent
[1972|Body Text] Lasting not less than 1 (one) year and then being beyond hope of improvement or disablement lasting less than 1 (one) year which at the Insurer’s discretion is beyond hope of improvement.
[1973|## Heading 3] Permanent Total Disablement
[1974|Body Text] Disablement that will entirely prevent the Insured Person from attending to his usual Business or occupation for the remainder of his life.
[1975|## Heading 3] Temporary Partial Disablement
[1976|Body Text] Disablement that prevents the Insured Person from attending to a substantial part of his Business or occupation.
[1977|## Heading 3] Temporary Total Disablement
[1978|Body Text] Disablement that temporarily prevents the Insured Person from attending to his usual Business or occupation.
[1979|## Heading 3] The Cover
[1980|Body Text] The Insurer agrees to pay the applicable benefit to the Insured if the Insured Person sustains accidental Bodily Injury by violent, external and visible means (including unavoidable exposure to the natural elements) caused by an assailant as a result of robbery, holdup or any attempt thereat or whilst the Insured Person attempts to protect the Insured’s Money which independently of any other cause results within 12 (twelve) months from the date of such Bodily Injury in the death, Loss of Use of 1 (one) or More Limb(s), loss of sight in one or both eyes or Permanent Total Disablement.
[1981|Body Text] Table of Benefits
[1982|Normal] * occurring within 12 (twelve) months of the happening of the Insured Event.
[1983|## Heading 1] Conditions
[1984|Body Text] Benefit will only be payable if either:
[1985|Body Text] under Insured Events 1 to 4 as stated in the Table of Benefits Bodily Injury is sustained by violent, external and visible means (including unavoidable exposure to the natural elements) caused by an assailant as a result of robbery, hold up or any attempt thereat of whilst the Insured Person attempts to protect the Insured’s Money; or
[1986|Body Text] under Insured Events 5 and 6 as stated in the Table of Benefits in respect of one continuous period of Disablement.
[1987|Body Text] The Insurer will cease paying Benefits under Insured Events 5 and 6 as stated in the Table of Benefits immediately an Insured Person becomes entitled to Benefit under Insured Events 1 to 4 as stated in the Table of Benefits.
[1988|Body Text] Benefits under Insured Events 5 and 6 as stated in the Table of Benefits in respect of any one Insured Person for all periods of disablement arising from one event, source or original cause will not be paid for more than the number of weeks as stated in the Schedule to this Section.
[1989|Body Text] Benefit as payable under Insured Events 5 and 6 as stated in the Table of Benefits shall not exceed the average weekly wage or salary (including where applicable average bonuses and overtime payments) of the Insured Person.
[1990|## Heading 1] Claims Conditions
[1991|Body Text] The Insured Person as often as required shall submit to medical examination on behalf of the Insurer at the Insurer’s own expense.
[1992|Body Text] The Insurer shall in the case of the death of the Insured Person be entitled to have a post-mortem examination at the Insurer’s own expense.
[1995|## Subtitle] Section 9: Goods in Transit Section
[1996|## Heading 1] Definitions
[1997|## Heading 3] Geographical Limits
[1998|Body Text] Anywhere in the world.
[1999|## Heading 3] In Transit
[2000|Body Text] From the time the Property Insured is loaded into the carrying conveyance and continues during the ordinary course of transit until the time it is unloaded at its destination including the period during loading and unloading on to or from the carrying conveyance including Temporary Storage.
[2001|## Heading 3] Property Insured
[2002|Body Text] Goods relating to the Business belonging to the Insured or for which the Insured has accepted responsibility.
[2003|## Heading 3] Temporary Storage
[2004|Body Text] Property Insured stored whilst en route for no longer than 72 (seventy-two) hours.
[2005|## Heading 3] The Cover
[2006|Body Text] The Insurer agrees to cover Damage to the Property Insured occurring during the Period of Insurance whilst In Transit by any method of conveyance stated in the Schedule to this Section within the Geographical Limits.
[2007|## Heading 1] Basis of Claims Settlement
[2008|Body Text] The amount payable shall be the value of the Property Insured at the time of its Damage, or at the Insurer’s option the reinstatement or replacement of such Property Insured or any part of it.
[2009|## Heading 1] Extensions

[2033|Body Text] the deterioration of Property Insured whilst In Transit in frozen, chilled or insulated condition due to variations in temperature unless directly consequent upon fire, theft or overturning or collision of the carrying vehicle;
[2034|Body Text] theft or attempted theft from any Unattended Vehicle or Trailer owned or operated by the Insured:
[2035|Body Text] during normal working hours, unless all doors, windows and other openings are securely locked and fastened and any immobiliser or alarm fitted to the vehicle is correctly set to operate and all keys removed from the vehicle; and in addition
[2036|Body Text] outside of normal working hours, unless the conveying vehicle is garaged in a securely locked building of a substantial construction or a compound which has secure walls or fences and securely fixed gates; or
[2037|Body Text] mechanical or electrical breakdown failure or derangement.
[2038|Body Text] Damage due to:
[2039|Body Text] insufficient or faulty packing, loading or stowing or wrongful addressing labelling or delivery; or
[2040|Body Text] delay, loss of market or other Consequential Loss.
