[2057|Body Text] bullion;
[2058|Body Text] Money;
[2059|Body Text] property in or on soft-topped, open-topped or curtain-sided vehicles or trailers owned or operated by the Insured or in the care, custody or control of the Insured if caused by:
[2060|Body Text] storm, tempest or flood;
[2061|Body Text] theft or attempted theft unless the vehicle or trailer is stolen at the same time;
[2062|Body Text] malicious persons in respect of an Unattended Vehicle or Trailer.
[2063|## Subtitle] Section 10: Loss of Licence Section
[2064|## Heading 1] Definitions
[2065|## Heading 3] Designated Premises Supervisor
[2066|Body Text] The individual specified in the Licence as the premises supervisor as defined under section 15 of the Licensing Act 2003.
[2067|## Heading 3] Licence
[2068|Body Text] The premises licence granted to the Insured for the sale of excisable liquors and or the provision of entertainment in connection with the Business at the Premises.
[2069|## Heading 3] Licensing Authorities
[2070|Body Text] Those authorities authorised under section 3 of the Licensing Act 2003.
[2071|## Heading 3] Operating Schedule
[2072|Body Text] The document that sets out the relevant licensable activities as defined under section 17 of the Licensing Act 2003.
[2073|## Heading 3] The Cover
[2074|Body Text] The Insurer agrees that if the Insured’s Licence is:
[2075|Body Text] forfeited, suspended or withdrawn; or
[2076|Body Text] refused renewal after due and proper application;
[2077|Body Text] during the Period of Insurance, the Insurer will indemnify or compensate the Insured for:
[2078|Body Text] the reduction in value of the interest of the Insured in the Premises as a result of the forfeiture, suspension, withdrawal or refusal to renew the Licence; and
[2079|Body Text] all costs and expenses incurred by the Insured with the Insurer’s consent in connection with any appeal.
[2080|## Heading 1] Exclusions
[2081|Body Text] This Section does not cover any loss:
[2082|Body Text] if the Insured is entitled to obtain compensation under any legislation or bye-law in respect of refusal to renew the Licence;
[2083|Body Text] if any alterations to the Premises are made without the consent of the Licensing Authorities;
[2084|Body Text] if the Premises are not maintained in a good state of sanitary condition or repair;
[2085|Body Text] where any direction or requirement of Licensing Authorities or other authorities is not complied with;
[2086|Body Text] where the forfeiture, suspension or withdrawal of the Licence is attributable wholly or in part to any act of or omission by the Insured or the Insured’s failure to take all reasonable action to maintain the Licence in force;
[2087|Body Text] where the Licence is forfeited, suspended, withdrawn or lapsed as a result of:
[2088|Body Text] actual or proposed compulsory acquisition of the Premises;
[2089|Body Text] any scheme of town or country planning, improvement or redevelopment;
[2090|Body Text] the failure to notify the authorities about changes to the Operating Schedule;
[2091|Body Text] failure other than for good cause to keep the Premises open during the permitted hours;
[2092|Body Text] the Designated Premises Supervisor losing their personal licence;
[2093|Body Text] the death or insolvency of the Licence holder; or
[2094|Body Text] any alteration to legislation or regulations governing the grant, renewal, transfer, surrender, forfeiture, suspension or withdrawal of the Licence after the commencement of the Period of Insurance unless the Insurer confirms in writing that this coverage will continue to apply after such alteration.
[2095|## Heading 1] Conditions
[2096|## Heading 3] Claims Condition
[2097|Body Text] On becoming aware of the forfeiture, suspension, withdrawal, lapsing or refused renewal of the Licence the Insured shall:
[2098|Body Text] give the Insurer notice in writing within 48 (forty-eight) hours with a full explanation of the circumstances;
[2099|Body Text] give all such assistance as the Insurer may reasonably require to appeal against such forfeiture, suspension, withdrawal, lapsing or refused renewal of the Licence;
[2100|Body Text] apply if practicable and required by the Insurer for the grant of a new Licence for the same or alternative premises to ensure the continuance of the Business in a similar or alternative form;
[2101|Body Text] provide a statement of loss if any together with such documents, statements and accounts as may be reasonably required by the Insurer to verify the same;
[2102|Body Text] allow the Insurer such access to the Premises and to the Insured’s books that the Insurer may require to quantify the amount of the loss.
[2103|## Heading 3] Notification to the Insurer
[2104|Body Text] The Insured must as soon as practicable give notice in writing and supply such additional information and assistance as the Insurer may reasonably require on becoming aware of any:
[2105|Body Text] complaint against the Premises or the control of the Business at the Premises;
[2106|Body Text] legal proceedings against or conviction of the Licence holder, manager, tenant, Designated Premises Supervisor or occupier of the Premises for any breach of legislation or regulations relating to licensing laws or any other circumstance whereby the character or reputation of the person is affected or called into question in respect of their honesty, moral standing or sobriety;
[2107|Body Text] change in the management or tenancy of the Premises;
[2108|Body Text] transfer or proposed transfer of the Licence;
[2109|Body Text] alteration in the Business at the Premises; or
[2110|Body Text] objection to renewal or any other circumstance which might prejudice renewal of the Licence.
[2111|## Heading 3] Replacement of Licensee
[2112|Body Text] In the event of the death, insolvency or incapacity of or the conviction or absconding of any Licence holder, manager, tenant, Designated Premises Supervisor or occupier of the Premises, the Insured will at the Insurer’s request take all practicable steps to secure a replacement for such person such replacement being acceptable to the Licensing Authorities or to any other like authority governing transfer of the Licence.
[2115|## Subtitle] Section 11: Production Indemnity “All Risks” Section
[2116|## Heading 1] Definitions
[2117|## Heading 3] Gross Production Cost
[2118|Body Text] All costs including overheads chargeable directly to the Production(s) but excluding:
[2119|Body Text] costs of scenario, story rights, musical rights, dialogue, royalties, scripts, typing schedules or plans (unless such costs are rendered entirely valueless), insurance premiums, taxes, completion guarantee fees, interest or finance charges;
[2120|Body Text] costs and expenses relating to sets, props, wardrobes or equipment owned by the Insured unless specifically designed for a Production and subsequently rendered entirely valueless;
[2121|Body Text] any amount which the Insured may be liable to pay to any director or partner of the Insured for salary or other payments incurred by reason of the Production(s) being interrupted or extended unless the services rendered by such person are in the capacity of producer, director, writer, actor or are directly related to the cost of the Production(s);
[2122|Body Text] costs of replacement of  proprietary software. In the event of abandonment, Gross Production Cost shall mean the amount of the contract value less:
[2123|Body Text] savings in costs and expenses between the date of abandonment and the anticipated completion date;
[2124|Body Text] the amounts, costs and expenses described in (a), (b), (c) and (d) above subject to the contract price having been reflected in the Insured’s estimate of Gross Production Costs.
[2125|## Heading 3] Principal Persons
[2126|Body Text] Any principal recording artiste, film star, director, producer, leading cameraman or recording effects man or any other person on whom the Production substantially depends.
[2127|## Heading 3] Production
[2128|Body Text] Any film, video, multimedia production or conference or event (other than where income is generated by speculative ticket sales) undertaken by the Insured.
[2129|## Heading 3] Property Insured
[2130|Body Text] Raw film or tape stock, exposed film (developed or undeveloped), videotape (including time coded tapes and offline copies), matrices, lavenders, positives, inter-positives, working prints, cutting copies, fine grain prints, transparencies, cells, artwork and drawings and computer media of all types (excluding third party proprietary software) soundtracks and tapes used in connection therewith all the property of the Insured or for which they are responsible.
[2131|## Heading 3] The Cover
[2132|Body Text] The Insurer will indemnify the Insured for:
[2133|Body Text] any net increase in the Gross Production Cost necessarily incurred by the Insured in completion of the Production(s) so far as reasonably practicable in the manner originally intended;
[2134|Body Text] and/or
[2135|Body Text] the amount of the Gross Production Cost expended prior to the Production(s) being unavoidably interrupted, postponed, cancelled or abandoned with the prior written consent of the Insurer;
[2136|Body Text] and/or
[2137|Body Text] additional expenditure necessarily and reasonably incurred to recompile or restore data or software which has been produced or developed directly in connection with an insured Production(s);
[2138|Body Text] arising as a result of:
[2139|Body Text] Multimedia Sub-Section
[2140|Body Text] Damage (including impairment or distortion of image) not otherwise excluded to the Property Insured whilst within the Geographical Limits stated in the Schedule occurring during the Period of Insurance.
[2141|Body Text] Producers Indemnity Sub-Section
[2142|Body Text] any cause beyond the control of the Insured not otherwise excluded occurring during the Period of Insurance.
[2143|## Heading 3] Amount Payable
[2144|Body Text] (Annual)
[2145|Body Text] The Insurer’s maximum liability in respect of any one Production will not exceed the Limit of Indemnity as stated in the Schedule.
[2146|## Heading 1] Extensions
[2147|## Heading 3] Agency and Talent Costs
[2148|Body Text] This Extension covers the reasonable agency costs (as specified in Item 17() of the APA agreement) up to 25% with a maximum of GBP 30,000 (thirty thousand pounds sterling) any one Production or as otherwise stated in the Schedule following Damage to the Property Insured.
[2149|Body Text] This Extension also covers talent costs in excess of the declared Sum Insured for each Production of up to 25% but not exceeding GBP 30,000 (thirty thousand pounds sterling) any one Production or as otherwise stated in the Schedule in all where the Insured is contractually responsible for such costs.
[2150|## Heading 3] Archive Material
[2151|Body Text] This Extension covers the cost of reduplicating or reprinting archive material on loan/hire to the Insured in the event of its Damage.
[2152|## Heading 3] Automatic Reinstatement
[2153|Body Text] In consideration of the insurance not being reduced by the amount of any loss the Insured shall pay the appropriate extra premium on the amount of the loss from the date thereof to the date of the expiry of the Period of Insurance.
[2154|## Heading 3] Storage
[2155|Body Text] This Extension covers the extra expenses sustained as a result of Damage to the Property Insured for a period of 12 (twelve) months after completion of the edited master unless contractual responsibility exists with the Agency to arrange insurance or at the expiration of the Period of Insurance whichever occurs soonest.
[2156|## Heading 1] Exclusions
[2157|Body Text] (applicable to Multimedia Sub-Section only)
[2158|Body Text] The Insurer will not be liable for Damage to the Property Insured or any loss or expense whatsoever or Consequential Loss:
[2159|Body Text] occasioned by or happening through:
[2160|Body Text] theft from any unattended unlocked vehicle;
[2161|Body Text] errors of judgment in exposure, lighting, sound recording selection or use of equipment or faulty manipulation by the Insured;
[2162|Body Text] directly or in any way caused by airport or customs security checks or apparatus unless properly labelled and beyond the control of the Insured;
[2163|Body Text] occasioned by or happening through:
[2164|Body Text] the costs of rectifying programming errors or design defects in software;
[2165|Body Text] in respect of  proprietary software only programming errors or design defects but this Exclusion will not apply to additional expenditure consequent upon erasure, destruction, corruption or distortion of other software caused by programming errors or design defects in third party proprietary software;
[2166|Body Text] in consequence of the use by the Insured of software in respect of which development has not been finalised or which has not passed all testing procedures or which has not been successfully proven;
[2167|Body Text] in consequence of failure to comply with manufacturers’ recommendations relating to the storage of computer media;
[2168|Body Text] arising directly or in any way as a result of or contributed to by foot and mouth disease.
[2169|## Heading 1] Exclusions
[2170|Body Text] (applicable to the Producers Indemnity Sub-Section only)
[2171|Body Text] The Insurer will not be liable:
[2172|Body Text] for any loss or expense or Consequential Loss arising from the incapacity of any person:
[2173|Body Text] due to any hazardous act, feat or performance undertaken in connection with an insured Production unless the Insurer has specifically agreed to provide such cover;
[2174|Body Text] due to venereal disease, AIDS, the illicit taking of drugs or the effects or influence of intoxicating liquor;
[2175|Body Text] caused by or contributed to by menstruation, pregnancy, childbirth or conditions pertaining thereto;
[2176|Body Text] directly or in any way caused by or contributed to by mumps, chicken pox, measles, German measles, whooping cough, scarlet fever, tonsillitis or diphtheria if such person is less than 15 (fifteen) years of age;
[2177|Body Text] who at the commencement of any insured Production or at the time of engagement is less than 4 (four) years of age or more than 70 (seventy) years of age unless details of such persons’ involvement have been agreed by the Insurer;
[2178|Body Text] arising from any illness, disease or condition known to or which was manifest to the Insured or the person at the time of engagement;
[2179|Body Text] for any loss or expense or Consequential Loss caused or contributed to by:
[2180|Body Text] variations in the rate of exchange or stability of any currency;
[2181|Body Text] the insolvency of the Insured or insufficient finance whenever or however such insufficiency may occur, or lack of support;
[2182|Body Text] for any claim for:
[2183|Body Text] the cost of repair or replacement of any material property of any kind including loss or destruction of or damage to exposed and/or unexposed film negatives, prints and/or sound tapes or videotapes;
[2184|Body Text] liability for payment of continuing hire charges under a hire agreement following loss or destruction of or damage to equipment used in connection with an insured Production;
[2185|Body Text] for any loss or expense or Consequential Loss occasioned by or happening through the failure of any videotape film or recording or any special effect used in its Production to fulfil its intended function or to create the desired effect;
[2186|Body Text] for any loss or expense or Consequential Loss occasioned by or happening through cancellation, interruption, postponement or abandonment of filming or recording due to weather conditions resulting in unsuitable photographic or recording conditions;
[2187|Body Text] for any loss or expense or Consequential Loss directly or in any way caused by or contributed to by:
[2188|Body Text] the failure of any animal to perform its intended function in an insured Production unless due to death, accidental injury or illness or disease first manifesting itself after the date of engagement for an insured Production;
[2189|Body Text] electrical or mechanical breakdown of any aircraft, helicopter, hovercraft, waterborne vessel, motorcycle, motor vehicle, railway locomotive, robot, lifting machinery or contractors’ plant which is intended to appear in an insured Production unless full details have been agreed by the Insurer;
[2190|Body Text] for any loss or expense or Consequential Loss occasioned by reason of claims made upon the Insured for failure to fulfil any contract;
[2191|Body Text] for the amount of the Excess;
[2192|Body Text] for any loss or expense or Consequential Loss arising from the incapacity or inadequate performance of any person unless due to mental stress as a result of serious accidental bodily injury to or illness requiring hospitalisation or death of that person’s spouse, fiancé(e), child, parent, brother or sister;
[2193|Body Text] for the costs of rectifying programming errors or design defects in software;
[2194|Body Text] for any additional expenditure in consequence of programming errors or design defects in respect of  proprietary software only but this Exclusion will not apply to additional expenditure consequent upon erasure, destruction, corruption or distortion of other software caused by programming errors or design defects in third party proprietary software
[2195|Body Text] for any additional expenditure in consequence of the use by the Insured of software in respect of which development has not been finalised or which has not passed all testing procedures or which has not been successfully proven;
[2196|Body Text] for any additional expenditure in consequence of failure to comply with manufacturer’s recommendations relating to storage of computer media;
[2197|Body Text] for any loss arising directly or in any way as a result of or contributed to by foot and mouth disease.
[2198|## Heading 1] Conditions
[2199|## Heading 3] Production Planning
[2200|Body Text] It is a condition precedent to liability under this Policy that:
[2201|Body Text] all travel and filming arrangements including purchase of tickets, reservation of accommodation, receipt of passports, visas, filming permits and consents and required or recommended immunisations are completed prior to departure to the first shoot location of any insured Production and that all other necessary and appropriate arrangements have been made for  of the insured Production(s);
[2202|Body Text] the Principal Persons are under contract to complete the insured Production(s).
[2203|## Heading 3] Duplicates
[2204|Body Text] It is a condition precedent to liability under this Policy that no original work, animation artwork, drawings, prints or offshoots are intentionally destroyed until a protection print and/or duplicate tape and/or disc has been completed.
[2205|## Heading 3] Rushes
[2206|Body Text] It is a condition precedent to liability under this Policy that all rushes are kept in the possession or control of the Insured, their professional representatives or their Employees at all times and carried in hand luggage throughout the duration of any return air flight from a shoot location unless deemed otherwise by the conveying Airline.
[2207|## Heading 3] Pre-Filming Testing
[2208|Body Text] It is a condition precedent to liability under this Policy that immediately prior to filming all cameras, lenses, raw film stock and video tape and associated equipment must be checked to ensure that they are satisfactory for the purpose and manner in which they are intended to be used.
[2209|## Heading 3] Full Value Declaration
[2210|Body Text] The Insured declared that to the best of their knowledge and belief the Sum Insured or Limit of Indemnity represent an accurate estimate of the gross production cost of the insured Production(s).
[2211|## Heading 3] Short Period only
[2212|Body Text] If in the event of loss insured hereby the Insured is found to be in breach of the Full Value Declaration clause then the Insured shall be considered their own insurer for the difference between the Sum Insured and the Gross Production Cost and will bear a rateable share of the amount of the loss accordingly.
[2213|## Heading 3] Premium Adjustment
[2214|Body Text] If any part of the premium is calculated on estimates, the Insured shall within 60 (sixty) days after the expiry of the Period of Insurance supply details as the Insurer may require.
[2215|Body Text] The premium for such period will be adjusted and the difference paid by or refunded to the Insured as the case may be any refund not exceeding 50% (fifty percent) of the premium paid.
[2216|## Heading 3] Processing
[2217|Body Text] The Insured will send unprocessed negative film for processing as soon as reasonably practical but in any event such material will not be accumulated by the Insured for more than 48 (forty-eight) hours or as otherwise agreed by the Insurer.
[2218|## Heading 3] Geographical Limit
[2219|Body Text] The Geographical Limit applicable to the failure of any person to appear as a result of death, personal injury or illness prior to that person’s arrival at the filming location is anywhere in the world.
[2222|## Subtitle] Section 12: Media Liability Section
[2223|## Heading 1] Definitions
[2224|## Heading 3] Advertising
[2225|Body Text] Advertising, publicity, or promotion of the Insured’s Media Business Activities and of the products and services of others.
[2226|## Heading 3] Circumstance
[2227|Body Text] Any circumstance, incident, occurrence, fact, matter, act, omission, state of affairs or event which is likely to give rise to a claim against the Insured or a claim by the Insured under this Policy.
[2228|## Heading 3] Computer System
[2229|Body Text] Any computer, data processing equipment, media or part thereof, or system of data storage and retrieval, or communications system, network, protocol or part thereof, or any computer software (including but not limited to application software, operating systems, runtime environments or compilers), firmware or microcode, or any electronic documents utilised in the ownership, security and management of the Insured’s electronic communications system, world-wide web site, internet site, intranet site, extranet site or web address(es).
[2230|## Heading 3] Damages
[2231|Body Text] Monetary relief
[2232|## Heading 3] Defence Costs and Expenses
[2233|Body Text] All reasonable costs and expenses incurred, with the Insurer’s prior written consent, in the investigation, defence and settlement of any claim first made against the Insured or of any Circumstance first notified during the Period of insurance. It does not include the Insured’s own overhead costs and expenses.
[2234|## Heading 3] Employee
[2235|Body Text] any person employed by the Insured under a contract of service, training or apprenticeship, and
[2236|Body Text] any voluntary worker; and
[2237|Body Text] any locum, seasonal or temporary personnel; and
[2238|Body Text] any self-employed person or entity acting as freelance consultant but only if such person or entity is working under the Insured’s direction, control and supervision.
[2239|## Heading 3] Financially Associated Person or Entity
[2240|Body Text] any business controlled or managed by the Insured or in which the Insured has an executive interest;
[2241|Body Text] any company in which the Insured directly or in any way owns or controls more than 15% of the issued share capital;
[2242|Body Text] any person having an executive or managerial role in the Insured or who would be considered to be a shadow director of the Insured;
[2243|Body Text] any company that directly or in any way owns or controls any of the issued share capital of the Insured or any of whose issued share capital is directly or in any way owned or controlled by any other company or person who directly or in any way owns or controls any of the issued share capital of the Insured.
[2244|## Heading 3] Indemnity Limit
[2245|Body Text] The Insurer’s total liability to pay damages and claimant’s costs, and shall not exceed:
[2246|Body Text] in the case of any claim arising directly or in any way from any Virus the Sum stated in the Schedule or GBP 500,000 (five hundred thousand pounds sterling) (whichever is less) in respect of any one claim or series of claims arising out of one originating cause and in total for all claims first made during the Period of insurance;
[2247|Body Text] in all other cases (except where specific Sums are stated in the Insuring Clauses) the Sum stated in the Schedule in respect of any one claim or series of claims arising out of one originating cause regardless of the number of persons claiming an indemnity from the Insurer under the terms of this Section.
[2248|Body Text] If more than one person is entitled to an indemnity under the terms of this Section, then the Insurer’s total liability to all such persons shall not exceed the Indemnity Limit. For the avoidance of doubt, the Indemnity Limit in a. above is not additional to and shall not increase the Sum stated in the Schedule.
[2249|## Heading 3] Virus
[2250|Body Text] means any unauthorised executable code uploaded to, or replicated through, a Computer System or network whether termed a virus or known by any other name and whether it is self-replicating or non-replicating which causes damage or loss to data or the Computer System.
[2251|## Heading 1] Insuring Clauses
[2252|Body Text] In consideration of the premium having been paid to the Insurer, the Insured is indemnified up to the Indemnity Limit (unless otherwise specified below) as follows:
[2253|## Heading 3] Indemnity
[2254|Body Text Indent] For damages and claimant’s costs for which the Insured is legally liable to pay resulting from claims first made against the Insured during the Period of Insurance and arising out of the ordinary course of the Media Business Services or associated Advertising activities in consequence of:
[2255|Body Text Indent] breach of contract or liability assumed by the Insured in the form of hold harmless or indemnity agreements executed with any party with whom the Insured has contracted to provide Media Business Services but only in respect of indemnity provided by Insuring Clauses 1. (Indemnity) and 2. (Legal Defence Costs and Expenses);
[2256|Body Text Indent] defamation or other tort related to disparagement of character, harm to reputation or feelings of any person or organisation including libel, slander or defamation, product disparagement and malicious falsehood, trade libel or any claim relating to outrage or emotional distress;
[2257|Body Text Indent] unintentional breach of confidentiality or other invasion, infringement or interference with rights of privacy or publicity including false light, intrusion upon a person’s seclusion and the public disclosure of private facts;
[2258|Body Text Indent] unintentional infringement of intellectual property rights including copyright, title, slogan, trademark, domain name or metatag, moral rights, misappropriation of, formats, characters, trade names, character names, titles, plots, musical compositions, voices, slogans, graphic material or artwork, passing off and plagiarism and commercial appropriation of name or likeness;
[2259|Body Text Indent] unintentional breach of a license to use a third party’s trademarked or copyrighted material but only to the extent that use exceeds the express limitations in the license regarding territory, duration or media in which the material may be used and only when made as a part of a claim under d. above;
[2260|Body Text Indent] breach of comparative advertising regulations;
[2261|Body Text Indent] the loss of or damage to Documents;
[2262|Body Text Indent] unintentional transmission of a Virus;
[2263|Body Text Indent] the failure to protect against unauthorised access to, unauthorised use of, a  attack against the Insured’s Computer System;
[2264|Body Text Indent] misuse of any information which is either confidential or subject to statutory restrictions;
[2265|Body Text Indent] breach of professional duty, negligent act, negligent error, negligent omission, negligent misstatement or negligent misrepresentation;
[2266|Body Text Indent] dishonest, fraudulent or malicious act or omission of any former or present Employee (which term, for the purpose of this clause alone, shall not include any principal, partner, member or director of the Insured) provided that no indemnity shall be given in the event that any principal, partner, member or director of the Insured conspired to commit or condoned any such dishonest, fraudulent or malicious act or omission;
[2267|Body Text Indent] any other civil liability not otherwise excluded.
[2268|## Heading 3] Legal Defence Costs and Expenses
[2269|Body Text Indent] The Insurer will pay in addition to any indemnity under Insuring Clause 1. (Indemnity) all Defence Costs and Expenses provided that:
[2270|Body Text Indent] if the amount paid or agreed to be paid by or on behalf of the Insured to dispose of a claim exceeds the Indemnity Limit the Insurer will only be liable for that proportion of the Defence Costs and Expenses which the Indemnity Limit bears to the amount paid or agreed to be paid;
[2271|Body Text Indent] in the event that the Insurer elects to make a payment to the Insured pursuant to Notification and Claims Condition – Applicable to this Section then the Insurer shall have no liability to pay Defence Costs and Expenses incurred after the date upon which such payment is made.
[2272|## Heading 3] Rectification
[2273|Body Text Indent] For additional expenses, other than those covered under Insuring Clause 8. (Withdrawal of Content) of this Section directly incurred, with the prior written consent of the Insurer, in successfully rectifying a problem which otherwise would lead to a claim in excess of such expenses under Insuring Clause 1. (Indemnity) of this Section.
[2274|Body Text Indent] If the Insured is unable to get approval from the Insurer due to time constraints or lack of detailed information, the Insurer will pay such expenses provided that the Insured can demonstrate that:
[2275|Body Text Indent] such expenses were less than the amount of a potential claim; and
[2276|Body Text Indent] the amount is reasonable; and
[2277|Body Text Indent] the Insured’s client has received the same level and quality of service or deliverables that they were originally entitled to receive.
[2278|Body Text Indent] Any payment made under this Clause will exclude the Insured’s lost profit, mark-up, or VAT or its equivalent and compensation for management time or any lost files or commissions from any other client or potential client. If a claim is later made the amount of expenses paid under this Section will be deducted from the Indemnity Limit for that claim.
[2279|## Heading 3] Irrecoverable fees
[2280|Body Text Indent] For amounts owed to the Insured, including amounts legally owed by the Insured to sub-contractors or suppliers, due to the refusal of the Insured’s client to pay for work done by the Insured for them where such client has reasonable grounds for being dissatisfied with the work and threatens to bring a claim for more than the amount owed, and which would otherwise be covered under Insuring Clause 1. (Indemnity), provided that such threat is first made against the Insured and notified to the Insurers during the Period of Insurance. In such circumstances, if it is possible to settle the dispute by agreeing not to pursue the outstanding amount, the Insurer will agree to pay the amount owed if they consider that it will avoid a legitimate claim under Insuring Clause 1. (Indemnity) for a greater amount. If, following this, a claim under Insuring Clause 1. (Indemnity) still arises then the amount paid under this Section will be deducted from the Indemnity Limit. If the Insured eventually recovers part or all of the debt then such recovered amount shall be repaid to the Insurer less the Insured’s reasonable expenses of recovering the debt due.
[2281|## Heading 3] Commitment to Media Space or Print Time
[2282|Body Text Indent] For claims first notified by the Insured, during the Period of Insurance relating to amounts that the Insured is committed to pay for media space or print time, but where the Insured’s client refuses to pay due to allegations that the Insured has acted outside its authority, the Insurer will pay such an amount if it can be shown, by the Insured, that it cannot legally be recovered from the client and that all reasonable steps have been taken to reduce or avoid the loss.
[2283|## Heading 3] Data Protection Defence Costs
[2284|Body Text Indent] Up to a maximum of GBP 250,000 (two hundred and fifty thousand pounds sterling) in the aggregate in the Period of Insurance, in respect of legal costs and expenses incurred with the Insurer’s prior written consent in the defence of any criminal proceedings brought against the Insured during the Period of Insurance under The Data Protection Act 1998 or amending or superseding legislation provided always that:
[2285|Body Text Indent] the act, error or omission giving rise to the proceedings shall have been committed by the Insured in the ordinary course of their Media Business Services;
[2286|Body Text Indent] the Insurer shall be entitled to appoint solicitors and counsel to act on behalf of the Insured;
[2287|Body Text Indent] the Insurer shall have no liability to pay costs incurred subsequent to a plea or finding of guilt on the part of the Insured, or in the event that counsel should advise that there are no reasonable prospects of successfully defending the proceedings, except for costs incurred solely for the purpose of making a plea in mitigation before sentencing or costs incurred in making an appeal if counsel shall advise that the prospects of a successful appeal following a finding of guilt are reasonable.
[2288|## Heading 3] Reputation Management
[2289|Body Text Indent] Following a claim under Insuring Clause Indemnity), up to a maximum of GBP 250,000 (two hundred and fifty thousand pounds sterling), for all reasonable costs incurred with the Insurer’s prior written consent for a public relations and/or crisis management consultant to avert or mitigate any material damage to the Insured’s Media Business Services reputation.
[2290|## Heading 3] Withdrawal of Content
[2291|Body Text Indent] Up to a maximum of GBP 250,000 (two hundred and fifty thousand pounds sterling) for expenses necessarily incurred, with the prior written consent of the Insurer, in the withdrawal or alteration of any data, text, sounds, images or similar content as a result of or in mitigation of a claim or potential claim which would otherwise be covered under Insuring Clause 1, including as a result of a complaint made to the Advertising Standards Authority (ASA), the Office of Communications (OFCOM), Trading Standards Officers or any other regulatory or self-regulatory body.
[2292|Body Text Indent] The Insurer will only pay such expenses if the Insured can demonstrate that:
[2293|Body Text Indent] such content would, if not withdrawn or altered, lead to a claim under Insuring Clause 1. (Indemnity) equal to or in excess of the expenses necessarily incurred in the withdrawal or alteration of the content; and
[2294|Body Text Indent] the expenses incurred are necessary to successfully avoid such claim.
[2295|Body Text Indent] Any payment made under this Clause will exclude the Insured’s lost profit, mark-up, or VAT or its equivalent and compensation for management time or any lost files or commissions from any other client or potential client. If a claim is later made the amount of expenses paid under this Section will be deducted from the Indemnity Limit for that claim.
[2296|## Heading 3] Compensation for Court Attendance
[2297|Body Text] If the Insured has to attend court as a witness in connection with a claim covered under Insuring Clause 1 the Insurer will provide compensation to the Insured at the following rates per day for each day on which attendance is required:
[2298|Body Text] any director or partner of the Insured: GBP 500 (five hundred pounds sterling);
[2299|Body Text] any Employee of the Insured: GBP 250 (two hundred and fifty pounds sterling).
[2300|## Heading 3] Costs for Prosecuting Infringement of the Insured’s Intellectual Property Rights
[2301|Body Text] Up to a maximum of GBP 25,000 (twenty-five thousand pounds sterling) in the aggregate in the Period of Insurance, for the reasonable and necessary costs and expenses incurred by the Insured, with the Insurer’s prior written consent, in the pursuance of any claim first made by the Insured against a third party during the Period of Insurance, for infringement of intellectual property rights first discovered by the Insured during the Period of Insurance where the ownership of such rights is vested in the Insured.
[2302|Body Text] For the purposes of this Insuring Clause the Insurer will only give prior consent where the Insured has provided, at their own expense, an opinion from a solicitor, barrister or suitably qualified intellectual property agent evidencing the existence of the Insured's intellectual property rights, the infringement of those rights, a measurable loss and a reasonable prospect of success.
[2303|Body Text] For the avoidance of doubt, the Insurer’s total liability to indemnify the Insured under any combination of these Insuring Clauses shall not exceed the Sum stated in the Schedule under the heading “Indemnity Limit” in respect of any one claim or series of claims arising out of one originating cause regardless of the number of Insuring Clauses that it or they might relate to.
[2304|Body Text] For the avoidance of doubt the indemnity provided under Insuring Clauses 5.-10. is not additional to and shall not increase the Indemnity Limit.

[2307|## Heading 3] Joint ventures

[2311|## Heading 3] Mergers and Acquisitions
[2312|Body Text] If, during the Period of Insurance the Insured creates or acquires a company or companies subsequent to inception and the turnover relating to all such created or acquired companies does not exceed 20% (twenty percent) of the estimated turnover of the companies covered under this Policy at inception (less the turnover for companies sold during the Period of Insurance), then this Policy shall include as an Insured any such company created or acquired automatically from the date of creation or acquisition without additional premium provided that:
[2313|Body Text] Media Business Services carried out by such company is similar to that of the Insured; and
[2314|Body Text] prior to the acquisition the acquired company’s directors or officers shall not have notified or be aware of any professional indemnity claims or circumstances; and
[2315|Body Text] the Retroactive Date applicable to the Media Business Services of the new entity is deemed to be the date of acquisition or creation;
[2316|Body Text] Where the Insured creates or acquires a company or companies subsequent to inception and the turnover relating to all such created or acquired companies exceeds 20% (twenty percent) of the estimated turnover of the companies covered under this Policy at inception (less the turnover for companies sold during the Period of Insurance), then this Policy shall include as an Insured any such company created or acquired automatically from the date of creation or acquisition provided that:
[2317|Body Text] the terms stated in a.  to iii above also apply to such created or acquired companies;
[2318|Body Text] the Insured notifies the Insurer as soon as is reasonably practicable of the creation or acquisition;
[2319|Body Text] the Insured accepts the revised premium and or terms applying to each and every such creation and or acquisition;
[2320|Body Text] all cover in respect of such created or acquired entities will terminate 30 (thirty) days following creation or acquisition if terms cannot be agreed between the Insured and the Insurer.
[2321|## Heading 1] Conditions
[2322|## Heading 3] Change of Control
[2323|Body Text] In the event that the Insured merges into or consolidates with or sells all or substantially all of its assets or shares to a third party (whether a company, corporation or any other legal entity or person) or there is any acquisition of more than 50% (fifty percent) of the voting share capital of the Insured by a third party (whether a company, corporation or any other legal entity or person) the Insured shall give written notice of such event prior to its execution. Upon receipt of such notice, the Insurer may at its absolute discretion agree to continuation of this Policy, to be confirmed by way of a written endorsement to this Policy. In the absence of such agreement and/or if notice is not forthcoming as required under this Condition, the cover provided by this Policy shall cease with immediate effect at the date of the change of control.
[2324|Body Text] For the avoidance of doubt, the Insured shall not be entitled to an indemnity in respect of any claims made under this Policy where notification of the claim occurs after a change in control (as referred to in this Condition) where the change of control was not reported to the Insurer and approved in accordance with this Condition.
[2325|## Heading 3] Premium Payment Clause
[2326|Body Text] The Insured undertakes that the premium will be paid in full to the Insurer within 60 (sixty) days of inception of this Policy (or, in respect of instalment premiums agreed by the Insurer, when due).
[2327|Body Text] If the premium due under this Policy has not been so paid to the Insurer by the 60th (sixtieth) day from the inception of this Policy, (and, in respect of instalment premiums, by the date they are due), the Insurer shall have the right to cancel this Policy by notifying the Insured via their broker in writing. In the event of cancellation, premium is due to the Insurer on a pro rata basis for the period that the Insurer is on risk but the full policy premium shall be payable to the Insurer in the event of a loss or occurrence prior to the date of termination which gives rise to a valid claim under this Policy.
[2328|Body Text] It is agreed that the Insurer shall give not less than 15 (fifteen) days prior notice of cancellation to the Insured via their Insurance Adviser. If premium due is paid in full to the Insurer before the notice period expires, notice of cancellation shall automatically be revoked. If not, this Policy shall automatically terminate at the end of the notice period.
[2329|Body Text] If any provision of this Clause is found by any court or administrative body of competent jurisdiction to be invalid or unenforceable, such invalidity or unenforceability will not affect the other provisions of this Clause which will remain in full force and effect.
[2330|## Heading 3] Reasonable Steps to Avoid Loss
[2331|Body Text] Without prejudice to the Notification and Claims Conditions in this Policy, the Insured shall take all reasonable steps to avoid or mitigate any loss, damage or liability that may result in any claim or Circumstance notifiable under this Section.
[2332|Body Text] In addition, in relation to Insuring Clause 1.h., the Insured shall protect its Computer System by:
[2333|Body Text] having Virus protection software operating in place which is running, correctly configured and regularly or automatically updated;
[2334|Body Text] having a fire wall or similar configured device to control access to its Computer System;
[2335|Body Text] encrypting and controlling the access to its Computer System and external devices including plug-in devices networked to its Computer System;
[2336|Body Text] controlling unauthorised access to its Computer System by correctly configuring its wireless network;
[2337|Body Text] changing all passwords on information and communication assets at least every 60 (sixty) days and cancel any username, password or other security protection after it knew or had reasonable grounds to suspect that it had been available to any unauthorised person;
[2338|Body Text] taking regular back-up copies of any data, file or programme on its Computer System;
[2339|Body Text] having an operational system for logging and monitoring user activity on its Computer System.
[2340|## Heading 3] Dishonest or Fraudulent Act or Omission
[2341|Body Text] In the event of a loss or claim which involves the dishonest, fraudulent or malicious act or omission of any former or present Employee the Insured shall take all reasonable action (including legal proceedings) to obtain reimbursement from the Employee concerned (and from any Employee who may have conspired to commit or have condoned such act or omission) or from the estate or legal representatives of such Employee. Any monies which but for such dishonest, fraudulent or malicious act or omission would be due to such Employee from the Insured or any monies held by the Insured for such Employee shall be deducted from any amount payable under this Section.
[2342|## Heading 1] Exclusions
[2343|Body Text] The Insurer shall not be liable to indemnify the Insured against:
[2344|## Heading 3] Adherence to Legal Advice
[2345|Body Text] Any claim arising out of or relating directly or in any way from any failure of the Insured to adhere to its own legal advice with regard to clearances of any data, text, sounds, images or similar content that is intended to be, or has been, disseminated;
[2346|## Heading 3] Asbestos
[2347|Body Text] Any claim arising directly or in any way out of or resulting from or in consequence of or in any way involving asbestos or any materials containing asbestos in whatever form or quantity;
[2348|## Heading 3] Bodily Injury/Property Damage
[2349|Body Text] Any claim for bodily injury, sickness, disease, psychological injury, emotional distress, nervous shock or death sustained by any person or any loss, damage or destruction of property unless such claim arises directly from negligent publication, negligent misstatement or negligent misrepresentation contained within any data, text, sounds, images or similar content that has been created by the Insured as part of their Media Business Services;
[2350|## Heading 3] Claims by Employees
[2351|Body Text] Any claim made against the Insured by any present or former Employee;
[2352|## Heading 3] Claims by Financially Associated Persons or Entities
[2353|Body Text] Any claim made against the Insured by any Financially Associated Person or Entity whether alone or jointly with any other person or entity. However, this Exclusion shall not apply to any claim brought against such Financially Associated Person or Entity by an independent third party which would, but for this Exclusion, be covered by this Section;
[2354|## Heading 3] Claims or Circumstances Known at Inception
[2355|Body Text] Any claim arising directly or in any way from any claim or Circumstance of which the Insured was, or ought reasonably to have been, aware prior to inception of this Policy, whether notified under any other insurance or not;
[2356|## Heading 3] Collection of Private Data Without Consent
[2357|Body Text] Any claim arising directly or in any way from your actual or alleged failure to obtain explicit consent from any private individual before collecting storing or sharing any of their personal information, including but not limited to internet search history and internet browsing habits. This Exclusion shall not apply where private data has been collected by a third party without the knowledge of the Insured;
[2358|## Heading 3] Collusion and Conspiracy
[2359|Body Text] Any claim arising from any alleged collusion, conspiracy, extortion or threatened violence;
[2360|## Heading 3] Commercial Disputes

[2362|Body Text] commission or royalty, or any other term upon which such partner or associate is to be compensated in connection with doing business with you, or any compensation or remuneration promised or owed by you pursuant to those terms; or
[2363|Body Text] the Insured’s decision to cease doing business with such a partner or associate:
[2364|## Heading 3] Contractual Liability
[2365|Body Text] Any claim arising directly or in any way from any breach or alleged breach of any contractual duty or duty of care owed or alleged to have been owed by the Insured to any third party and which is more onerous than any duty that would otherwise be implied by common law or statute.
[2366|## Heading 3] Costs and Expenses Incurred Without Prior Consent
[2367|Body Text] Any claim for costs and expenses incurred without the prior consent of the Insurer;

[2370|## Heading 3] Deliberate Acts

[2372|## Heading 3] Dishonesty
[2373|Body Text] Any claim arising directly or in any way from any dishonest, fraudulent, malicious or illegal act or omission of the Insured or any Employee, except as covered by Insuring Clause 1.l. of this Section;
[2374|## Heading 3] Employee Benefit Schemes / Stocks and Shares

[2376|## Heading 3] Employers’ Liability
[2377|Body Text] Any claim arising directly or in any way from bodily injury, sickness, disease, psychological injury, emotional distress, nervous shock or death sustained by any Employee arising out of or in the course of their employment by the Insured, or for any breach of any obligation owed by the Insured as an employer to any partner, principal, director, member or Employee or applicant for employment;
[2378|## Heading 3] False Advertising

[2502|## Heading 3] Reasonable Prospects of Success
[2503|Body Text] Other than as set out in 2 And 3 below, a greater than 50% chance of the Insured successfully pursuing or defending the claim and, if the Insured is seeking damages or compensation, a greater than 50% chance of enforcing any judgment that might be obtained.
[2504|Body Text] In criminal prosecution claims where the Insured:
[2505|Body Text] pleads guilty, a greater than 50% chance of reducing any sentence or fine or
[2506|Body Text] pleads not guilty, a greater than 50% chance of that plea being accepted by the court.
[2507|Body Text] In all claims involving an appeal, a greater than 50% chance of the Insured being successful.
[2508|Body Text] Where it has been determined than Reasonable Prospects of Success do not exist, the Insured shall be liable to pay any legal costs incurred should they pursue or defend their claim irrespective of the outcome.
[2509|## Heading 3] Territorial Limit
[2510|Body Text] For Insured Events Legal Defence and Contract & Debt Recovery the United Kingdom, channel Islands, Isle of Man, Norway, Switzerland and countries in the European Union.
[2511|Body Text] For all other Insured Events the United Kingdom, Channel Islands and the Isle of Man.
[2512|## Heading 3] We/Us/Our
[2513|Body Text] ARAG plc who is authorised under a binding authority agreement to administer this insurance on behalf of the Insurer.
[2514|## Heading 3] You/Your
[2515|Body Text] The individual, partnership or corporate body named in the Schedule, including any subsidiary and/or associated companies declared to Us.
[2516|## Heading 3] The Cover
[2517|Body Text] Following an Insured Event, the Insurer will pay Legal Costs & Expenses including the cost of appeals (and compensation awards under Insured Event Employment Compensation Awards) up to:
[2518|Body Text] GBP 100,000 for all claims related by time or originating cause; and
[2519|Body Text] an aggregate limit of GBP 1,000,000 for compensation awards under Insured Event Employment Compensation Awards;
[2520|Body Text] subject to all of the following requirements being met.
[2521|Body Text] Unless otherwise stated in this Section of the Policy, the Insured Event arises in connection with Your Business and occurs within the Territorial Limit.
[2522|Body Text] The claim
[2523|Body Text] always has Reasonable Prospects of Success and
[2524|Body Text] is reported to Us
[2525|Body Text] during the Period of Insurance and
[2526|Body Text] as soon as the Insured first becomes aware of circumstances which could give rise to a claim.
[2527|Body Text] Unless there is a conflict of interest, the Insured always agrees to use the Appointed Advisor chosen by Us
[2528|Body Text] in any claim to be heard by an Employment Tribunal and/or
[2529|Body Text] before proceedings have been or need to be issued.
[2530|Body Text] Any dispute will be dealt with through mediation or by a court, tribunal, Advisory Conciliation and Arbitration Service or a relevant regulatory or licensing body within the Territorial Limit.
[2531|Body Text] We consider that a claim has been reported to Us when We have received the Insured’s fully completed claim form.
[2532|Body Text] This Section of the Policy will pay any otherwise covered claim involving the use of or inability to use a computer, including devices such as smart phones, tablets and wearable technology. This cover is subject to all other Policy terms.
[2533|## Heading 1] Insured Events
[2534|## Heading 3] Employment
[2535|Body Text] A dispute between You and Your Employee, ex-Employee, or a prospective Employee, arising from a breach or an alleged breach of their
[2536|Body Text] contract of service with You
[2537|Body Text] related legal rights.
[2538|Body Text] You can claim under this Section of the Policy as soon as internal procedures as set out in the
[2539|Body Text] ACAS Code of Practice for Disciplinary and Grievance Procedures, or
[2540|Body Text] Labour Relations Agency Code of Practice on Disciplinary and Grievance Procedures in Northern Ireland
[2541|Body Text] have been or ought to have been concluded.
[2542|## Heading 3] What is not covered under Employment
[2543|Body Text] Any claim arising from or relating to:
[2544|Body Text] the pursuit of an action by You other than an appeal against the decision of a court or tribunal
[2545|Body Text] actual or alleged redundancy that is notified to Employees within 180 days of the start of this Section of the Policy, except where You have had equivalent cover in force up until the start of this Section of the Policy
[2546|Body Text] costs You incur to prepare for an internal disciplinary hearing, grievance or appeal
[2547|Body Text] a pension scheme where actions are brought by ten or more Employees or ex-Employees.
[2548|## Heading 3] Employment Compensation Awards
[2549|Body Text] Following a claim We have accepted under Insured Event Employment, the Insurer will pay any
[2550|Body Text] basic and compensatory award or
[2551|Body Text] an amount agreed by Us in settlement of a dispute.
[2552|Body Text] Provided that compensation is:
[2553|Body Text] agreed through mediation, conciliation or under a settlement approved by Us in advance or
[2554|Body Text] awarded by a tribunal judgment after full argument unless given by default.
[2555|## Heading 3] What is not covered under Employment Compensation Awards
[2556|Body Text] Money due to an Employee under a contract or a statutory provision relating thereto.
[2557|Body Text] Compensation awards or settlements relating to
[2558|Body Text] trade union membership, industrial or labour arbitration or collective bargaining agreements
[2559|Body Text] civil claims or statutory rights relating to trustees of occupational pension schemes.
[2560|## Heading 3] Employment Restrictive Covenants
[2561|Body Text] A dispute with Your Employee or ex-Employee which arises from their breach of a restrictive covenant where You are seeking financial remedy or damages.
[2562|Body Text] Provided that the restrictive covenant
[2563|Body Text] is designed to protect Your legitimate business interests, for a period not exceeding 12 months and
[2564|Body Text] is evidenced in writing and signed by Your Employee or ex-Employee and
[2565|Body Text] extends no further than is reasonably necessary to protect the Business interests.
[2566|Body Text] A dispute with another party who alleges that You have breached their legal rights protected by a restrictive covenant.
[2567|## Heading 3] Tax Disputes
[2568|Body Text] A formally notified enquiry into Your Business tax.
[2569|Body Text] A dispute about Your compliance with HMRC regulations relating to Your Employees, workers or payments to contractors.
[2570|Body Text] A dispute with HMRC about Value Added Tax.
[2571|Body Text] Provided that:
[2572|Body Text] You maintain proper records in accordance with legal requirements and
[2573|Body Text] in respect of any appealable  You have requested an internal review from HMRC where available.
[2574|## Heading 3] What is not covered under Tax Disputes
[2575|Body Text] Any claim arising from or relating to:
[2576|Body Text] tax returns which are submitted late or for any other reason, result in HMRC imposing a penalty, or which contain careless and/or deliberate misstatements or omissions
[2577|Body Text] an investigation by the Fraud Investigation Service of HMRC
[2578|Body Text] circumstances where the Disclosure of Tax Avoidance Scheme Regulations apply or should apply to Your financial arrangements
[2579|Body Text] any enquiry that concerns assets, monies or wealth outside of Great Britain and Northern Ireland
[2580|Body Text] Your failure to register for VAT.
[2581|## Heading 3] Property
[2582|Body Text] A dispute relating to material property which You own or is Your responsibility:
[2583|Body Text] following an event which causes physical damage to Your material property
[2584|Body Text] following a public or private nuisance or trespass
[2585|Body Text] which You wish to recover or repossess from an Employee or ex-Employee.
[2586|## Heading 3] What is not covered under Property
[2587|Body Text] Any claim arising from or relating to:
[2588|Body Text] a contract between You and a third party except for a claim under Property 3 above
[2589|Body Text] goods lent or hired out
[2590|Body Text] compulsory purchase, demolition restrictions, controls or permissions placed on land or property by any government, local or public authority.
[2591|## Heading 3] Legal Defence
[2592|Body Text] A criminal investigation and/or enquiry by:
[2593|Body Text] the police
[2594|Body Text] other body with the power to prosecute
[2595|Body Text] where it is suspected that an offence may have been committed that could lead to the Insured being prosecuted.
[2596|Body Text] The charge for an offence or alleged offence which leads to the Insured being prosecuted in a court of criminal jurisdiction.
[2597|## Heading 3] What is not covered under Legal Defence
[2598|Body Text] Any claim relating to a parking offence.
[2599|## Heading 3] Compliance & Regulation
[2600|Body Text] Receipt of a Statutory Notice that imposes terms against which You wish to appeal.
[2601|Body Text] Notice of a formal investigation or disciplinary hearing by any professional or regulatory body.
[2602|Body Text] A civil action alleging wrongful arrest arising from an allegation of theft.
[2603|Body Text] A claim against You for compensation under the Data Protection Act 2018 provided that
[2604|Body Text] You are registered with the Information Commissioner
[2605|Body Text] You are able to evidence that You have in place a process to
[2606|Body Text] investigate complaints from data subjects regarding a breach of their privacy rights
[2607|Body Text] offer suitable redress where a breach has occurred and that Your complaints process has been fully engaged.
[2608|Body Text] A civil action alleging that an Insured has
[2609|Body Text] committed an act of unlawful discrimination; or
[2610|Body Text] failed to correctly exercise their fiduciary duty as a trustee of a pension fund set up for the benefit of Your Employees.
[2611|## Heading 3] What is not covered under Compliance & Regulation
[2612|Body Text] Any claim arising from or relating to:
[2613|Body Text] the pursuit of an action by You other than an appeal
[2614|Body Text] a routine inspection by a regulatory authority
[2615|Body Text] an enquiry, investigation or enforcement action by HMRC
[2616|Body Text] a claim brought against Your Business where unlawful discrimination has been alleged.
[2617|## Heading 3] Statutory Licence Appeals
[2618|Body Text] An appeal against a formal written proposal by the relevant authority to alter, suspend, revoke or refuse to renew a licence or compulsory registration required to run Your Business.
[2619|## Heading 3] Loss of Earnings
[2620|Body Text] This Insured’s absence from work to attend court, tribunal, arbitration, regulatory proceedings or a professional body’s disciplinary hearing at the request of the Appointed Advisor or whilst on jury service which results in loss of earnings.
[2621|## Heading 3] What is not covered under Loss of Earnings
[2622|Body Text] Any sum which can be recovered from the court.
[2623|## Heading 3] Personal Injury
[2624|Body Text] An event that causes bodily injury to, or the death of, an Insured.
[2625|## Heading 3] What is not covered under Personal Injury
[2626|Body Text] Any claim arising from or relating to a condition, illness or disease which develops gradually over time.
[2627|## Heading 3] Executive Suite
[2628|Body Text] This Insured Event applies only to the principal, executive officers, directors and partners of Your Business.
[2629|Body Text] An HMRC enquiry into the executive’s personal tax affairs.
[2630|Body Text] A motoring prosecution that arises from driving for personal, social or domestic use, including commuting to or from Your Business.
[2631|Body Text] A claim that arises from personal identity theft provided that the person claiming has sought and followed advice from the Executive Suite - Identity Theft Resolution helpline.
[2632|Body Text] A dispute that arises from the terms of Your Business partnership agreement that is to be referred to mediation.
[2633|Body Text] Crisis communication as described in Insured Event Crisis Communication below shall be available to the principal, executive officers directors and partners of the Business for matters occurring in their private and personal capacity that cause significant adverse publicity or reputational damage.
[2634|## Heading 3] What is not covered under Executive Suite
[2635|Body Text] Any claim arising from or relating to:
[2636|Body Text] tax returns which are submitted late or for any other reason, result in HMRC imposing a penalty or which contain careless and/or deliberate misstatements or omissions
[2637|Body Text] an investigation by the Fraud Investigation Service of HMRC
[2638|Body Text] circumstances where the Disclosure of Tax Avoidance Scheme Regulations apply or should apply to the executive’s financial arrangements
[2639|Body Text] any enquiry that concerns assets, monies or wealth outside of the United Kingdom
[2640|Body Text] a parking offence
[2641|Body Text] costs incurred in excess of GBP 25,000 for a claim under Executive Suite 4 and 5 above.
[2642|Body Text] Crisis communication for a matter that has not actually resulted in adverse publicity appearing online, in print or broadcast.
[2643|## Heading 3] Contract & Debt Recovery
[2644|Body Text] A breach or alleged breach of an agreement or alleged agreement which has been entered into by You or on Your behalf to buy, sell, hire or lease goods or services or to rent Your Business premises, provided that if You are claiming for an undisputed  You have exhausted Your normal credit control procedures.
[2645|## Heading 3] What is not covered under Contract & Debt Recovery
[2646|Body Text] Any claim arising from or relating to:
[2647|Body Text] an amount which is less than GBP 200
[2648|Body Text] a dispute with a tenant or leasee where You are the landlord or lessor
[2649|Body Text] the sale or purchase of land or buildings
[2650|Body Text] loans, mortgages, endowments, pensions or any other financial product
[2651|Body Text] computer hardware, software internet services or systems which
[2652|Body Text] have been supplied by You or
[2653|Body Text] have been tailored to Your requirements
[2654|Body Text] a breach or alleged breach of a professional duty by an Insured
[2655|Body Text] the settlement payable under an insurance policy
[2656|Body Text] dispute relating to an Employee or ex-Employee
[2657|Body Text] adjudication or arbitration.
[2658|## Heading 3] Crisis Communication
[2659|Body Text] Following an event which causes significant adverse publicity or reputational damage which is likely to have a widespread financial impact on Your Business, We will:
[2660|Body Text] liaise with You and Your solicitor (whether the solicitor is an Appointed Advisor under this Section of the Policy, or acts on Your behalf under any other policy) to draft a media statement or press release
[2661|Body Text] prepare communication for Your staff, clients, patients, suppliers and/or a telephone or website script or social media messaging
[2662|Body Text] arrange, support and represent an Insured at an event which media will be reporting
[2663|Body Text] support the Insured by taking phone calls/emails and managing interaction with media outlets
[2664|Body Text] support and prepare the Insured for media interviews
[2665|Body Text] provided that You have sought and followed advice from Our Crisis Communication helpline.
[2666|## Heading 3] What is not covered under Crisis Communication
[2667|Body Text] Any claim arising from or relating to:
[2668|Body Text] matters that should be dealt with through Your normal complaints procedures
[2669|Body Text] a matter that has not actually resulted in adverse publicity appearing online, in print or broadcast
[2670|Body Text] costs incurred in excess of GBP 25,000.
[2671|## Heading 1] Exclusions
[2672|Body Text] The Insured is not covered for any claim arising from or relating to:
[2673|Body Text] any costs or compensation awards incurred without Our consent
[2674|Body Text] any actual or alleged act, omission or dispute happening before, or existing at the start of the insurance provided by this Section of the Policy, and which the Insured knew or ought reasonably to have known could lead to a claim
[2675|Body Text] an allegation against the Insured involving:
[2676|Body Text] assault, violence, malicious falsehood or defamation
[2677|Body Text] indecent or obscene materials
[2678|Body Text] the use of alcohol or its unauthorised or unregulated manufacture, unlicensed dealing in alcohol or dealing in or using illegal drugs
[2679|Body Text] illegal immigration
[2680|Body Text] money laundering or bribery offences, breaches of international sanctions, fraud, or any other financial crime activities
[2681|Body Text] except in relation to Insured Event Crisis Communication
[2682|Body Text] defending a claim in respect of damages for personal injury (other than injury to feeling in relation to Insured Event Employment), or loss or damage to property owned by the Insured
[2683|Body Text] National Minimum Wage and/or National Living Wage Regulations
[2684|Body Text] patents, copyright, passing-off, trade or service marks, registered designs and confidential information (except in relation to Insured Event Employment Restrictive Covenants
[2685|Body Text] a dispute with any subsidiary, parent, associated or sister company or between shareholders or partners (except in relation to mediation under Insured Event Executive Suite 4)
[2687|Body Text] a franchise agreement
[2688|Body Text] an agency agreement through which one party has the legal capacity to alter the legal relations of the other
[2689|Body Text] a judicial review
[2690|Body Text] a dispute with Us, the Insurer or the party who arranged this cover not dealt with under the Arbitration Condition
[2691|Body Text] the payment of fines, penalties or compensation awarded against the Insured (except as covered under Insured Event Employment Compensation Awards); or costs awarded against the Insured by a court of criminal jurisdiction.
[2692|## Heading 1] Conditions
[2693|Body Text] Where the Insurer’s risk is affected by the Insured’s failure to keep to these conditions the Insurer can cancel this Section of Your Policy, refuse a claim or withdraw from an ongoing claim. The Insurer also reserves the right to recover Legal Costs & Expenses from You if this happens
[2694|## Heading 3] The Insured’s Responsibilities
[2695|Body Text] An Insured must:
[2696|Body Text] tell Us immediately of anything that may make it more costly or difficult for the Appointed Advisor to resolve the claim in the Insured’s favour
[2697|Body Text] cooperate fully with Us, give the Appointed Advisor any instructions We require, and keep them updated with progress of the claim and not hinder them
[2698|Body Text] take reasonable steps to claim back Legal Costs & Expenses and, where recovered, pay them to the Insurer
[2699|Body Text] allow the Insurer to take over and conduct in the Insured’s name, any claim.
[2700|## Heading 3] Freedom to Choose an Appointed Advisor
[2701|Body Text] In certain circumstances as set out in 2 below the Insured may choose an Appointed Advisor. In all other cases no such right exists and We shall choose the Appointed Advisor.
[2702|Body Text] If:
[2703|Body Text] a suitably qualified advisor considers that it has become necessary to issue proceedings or proceedings are issued against an Insured, or
[2704|Body Text] there is a conflict of interest
[2705|Body Text] the Insured may choose a qualified Appointed Advisor except where the Insured’s claim is to be dealt with by the Employment Tribunal, We shall always choose the Appointed Advisor.
[2706|Body Text] Where the Insured wishes to exercise the right to choose, the Insured must write to Us with their preferred representative’s contact details.
[2707|Body Text] Where the Insured chooses to use their preferred representative, the Insurer will not pay more than We agree to pay a solicitor from Our panel and will pay only the costs that the Insurer would have been liable to pay. (Our panel solicitor firms are chosen with care and We agree special terms with them which may be less than the rates available from other firms.)
[2708|Body Text] If the Insured dismisses the Appointed Advisor without good reason, or withdraws from the claim without Our written agreement, or if the Appointed Advisor refuses with good reason to continue acting for an Insured, the Insurer’s liability in respect of that claim will end immediately.
[2709|Body Text] In respect of pursuing a claim relating to Insured Event Contract & Debt Recovery You must enter into a Conditional Fee Agreement (unless the Appointed Advisor has entered into a Collective Conditional Fee Agreement) where legally permitted.
[2710|## Heading 3] Consent
[2711|Body Text] The Insured must agree to Us having sight of the Appointed Advisor’s file relating to the Insured’s claim. The Insured is considered to have provided consent to Us or Our appointed agent to have sight of their file for auditing and quality and cost control purposes.
[2712|Body Text] An Insured must have Your agreement to claim under this Section of the Policy.
[2713|## Heading 3] Settlement
[2714|Body Text] The Insurer can settle the claim by paying the reasonable value of the Insured’s claim.
[2715|Body Text] The Insured must not negotiate or settle the claim without Our written agreement.
[2716|Body Text] If the Insured refuses to settle the claim following advice to do so from the Appointed Advisor the Insurer reserves the right to refuse to pay further costs.
[2717|## Heading 3] Barrister’s Opinion
[2718|Body Text] We may require the Insured to obtain and pay for an opinion from a barrister if a dispute arises regarding the merits or value of the claim. If the opinion supports the Insured, then the Insurer will reimburse the reasonable costs of that opinion. If that opinion conflicts with advice obtained by Us, then the Insurer will pay for a final opinion which will be binding on the Insured and Us. This does not affect the Insured’s rights under the Arbitration Condition below.
[2719|## Heading 3] Arbitration
[2720|Body Text] If any dispute between the Insured and Us arises from this Section of the Policy, the Insured can make a complaint to Us as described under How to Complain below and We will try to resolve the matter. If We are unable to satisfy the Insured’s concerns and the matter can be dealt with by the Financial Ombudsman Service the Insured can ask them to arbitrate over the complaint.
[2721|Body Text] If the dispute cannot be dealt with by the Financial Ombudsman Service, it can be referred for independent arbitration to a qualified person agreed unpin by both parties. The loser of the dispute shall be liable to pay the costs incurred.
[2722|Body Text] If We and the Insured fail to agree of a suitable person to arbitrate the matter We will ask the President of the relevant Law Society to nominate. The arbitration shall be subject to the Arbitration Acts and the arbitrator’s decision shall be binding on both parties.
[2723|## Heading 3] Other Insurance
[2724|Body Text] The Insurer will not pay more than their fair share (rateable proportion) for any claim covered by another policy, or any claim that would have been covered by any other policy if this Section of the Policy did not exist; even if the other insurer refuses the claim.
[2725|## Heading 3] Fraudulent Claims and Claims Tainted by Dishonesty
[2726|Body Text] If the Insured makes any claim which is fraudulent or false, this Section of the Policy may become void and all benefit under it may be lost.
[2727|Body Text] An Insured shall at all times be entirely truthful and open in any evidence, disclosure or statement they give and shall act with complete honesty and integrity throughout. Where, on the balance of probabilities and having considered carefully all the facts of the claim, it appears to the Appointed Advisor that the Insured has breached this condition and that the breach has:
[2728|Body Text] affected Our assessment of Reasonable Prospects of Success, and/or
[2729|Body Text] prejudiced any part the outcome of Your claim
[2730|Body Text] the Insurer shall have no liability for Legal Costs & Expenses incurred from the date of the Insured’s breach.
[2731|## Heading 3] Acts of Parliament
[2732|Body Text] All legal instruments, bodies and rules referred to within this Section shall include the equivalent in Wales, Scotland, Northern Ireland, the Isle of Man and the Channel Islands and any subsequent amendment or replacement legislation.

However, if Our advisors consider that Your helpline usage is becoming  they will tell You. If following that warning usage is not reduced to a more reasonable level, We can refuse to accept further calls.

We give advice about business-related legal matters within UK and EU law and tax matters within the UK. Your query will be dealt with by a qualified specialist who is experienced in handling legal and tax-related matters. Use of this service does not constitute reporting of a claim.

The service offers document review and telephone or written advice and is subject to a charge. If You would like Us to arrange Redundancy  please call Us between 9am and 5pm on weekdays (except bank holidays).

We provide telephone advice to help executives keep their personal identity secure. Where identity theft is suspected, Our specialist caseworkers can help the victim to restore their credit rating and correspond with their card issuer, bank or other parties. Identity theft expenses are insured under Insured Event Executive Suite 3 when Your executives use this helpline.

[2744|Body Text] Where an event has led to actual publicity online, in print or broadcast, that could damage Your Business, You are insured against the costs of crisis communication services under Insured Event Crisis Communication when You use this helpline.
