[3282|Normal] means reasonable and necessary expenses that the Named Insured incurs on the Named Insured’s behalf, or on behalf of a party for whom the Named Insured is Vicariously Liable, to provide support activity to parties affected by a Privacy Breach, including the cost to set up and operate a call  and to provide a maximum of twenty-four (24) months of credit, identity or healthcare record monitoring services, fraud alert services, identity theft assistance services and credit or identity repair and restoration services. Breach Support and Credit Monitoring Expenses must be incurred with Insurer's prior written consent.
[3283|Normal] Bricking Event
[3284|Normal] means the unauthorised or malicious reprogramming of software or firmware installed on the Named Insured’s computer hardware or electronic equipment, including such reprogramming resulting from a Hacking Attack, which renders the Named Insured’s computer hardware or electronic equipment nonfunctional or useless for its intended purpose, without being physically damaged.
[3285|Normal] Bricking Loss
[3286|Normal] means the cost to replace the Named Insured’s computer hardware or electronic equipment due to loss of use of such computer hardware or electronic equipment caused by a Bricking Event; provided, however, that the amount of Bricking Loss payable under this Policy shall not exceed 25% more than the cost to replace the Named Insured’s computer hardware or electronic equipment with computer hardware or electronic equipment that is functionally equivalent to that which existed prior to the Bricking Event. Bricking Loss does not include any costs to replace the Named Insured’s computer hardware or electronic equipment or Other Property which sustains physical damage due to a Security Breach.
[3287|Normal] Business Equipment
[3288|Normal] means any machinery, vehicle or electronic device or equipment that: (a) is owned by or leased to the Named Insured; (b) is operated by the Named Insured to conduct the Named Insured’s business; and (c) can send and receive Data.  Business Equipment does not include any Products.
[3289|Normal] Card Association
[3290|Normal] means Visa International, MasterCard, Discover, JCB, American Express and any similar credit or debit card association that is a participating organisation of the Payment Card Industry Security Standards Council.
[3291|Normal] Claim
[3292|Normal] means, with respect to:
[3293|Normal] Insuring Clauses A and B,
[3294|Normal] a written demand made against the Insured for Damages or non-monetary relief;
[3295|Normal] a written request received by an Insured to enter into a Standstill Agreement, a stay or to waive a statute of limitations relating to either a pre-action litigation correspondence or legal proceedings against an Insured; or
[3296|Normal] the service of civil proceedings or the institution of arbitration or other alternative dispute resolution proceedings against the Insured seeking Damages, a temporary restraining order, or a preliminary or permanent injunction.
[3297|Normal] A Claim under Insuring Clauses A and B shall not include a Privacy Regulatory Proceeding or PCI DSS Demand.
[3299|Normal] Insuring Clause C, a Privacy Regulatory Proceeding;
[3300|Normal] Insuring Clause D, a PCI DSS Demand;
[3301|Normal] Insuring Clause E, a Bodily Injury Claim;
[3302|Normal] Insuring Clause F, a Property Damage Claim;
[3303|Normal] Insuring Clause G, written notice by an Executive to the Insurer of an Adverse Media Report, Security Breach or Privacy Breach;
[3304|Normal] Insuring Clause H, written notice by an Executive to the Insurer of a Security Breach or Privacy Breach;
[3305|Normal] Insuring Clause I, written notice by an Executive to the Insurer of a System Failure;
[3306|Normal] Insuring Clause J, written notice by an Executive to the Insurer of a Cyber Extortion Threat;
[3307|Normal] Insuring Clause K, written notice by an Executive to the Insurer of Financial Fraud, Telecommunications Fraud, Utilities Fraud, Phishing Fraud or Client Phishing Fraud;
[3308|Normal] Insuring Clause L, written notice by an Executive to the Insurer of a Bricking Event;
[3309|Normal] Insuring Clause M, written notice by an Executive to the Insurer of an Occurrence;
[3310|Normal] Insuring Clause N, a written request by an Executive to the Insurer for indemnification of Reward Expenses;
[3311|Normal] Insuring Clause O, a written request by an Executive to the Insurer for indemnification of Court Attendance Costs.
[3312|Normal] A Claim under any  Liability Insuring Clause will be deemed to have been first made against an Insured when any Insured first receives written notice of such Claim.
[3314|Normal] A Claim under any First Party Insuring Agreement of this Policy will be deemed to have been first made when the Insurer first receives written notice of such Claim.
[3315|Normal] Client Account
[3316|Normal] means a bank account held or maintained by the Named Insured’s client or the Named Insured’s customer, from which the Named Insured, as an authorised user, may deposit, withdraw, transfer or disburse Money.
[3317|Normal] Client Phishing Fraud
[3318|Normal] means the malicious use of intentionally misleading telephone calls, emails, texts, instant messages or other electronic communications or malicious websites to fraudulently induce the Named Insured’s client, customer or vendor to transfer, pay or deliver Money, Securities or Other Property to an unintended party by impersonating an Insured.
[3319|Normal] Client Phishing Fraud Loss
[3320|Normal] means:
[3321|Normal] the Named Insured’s loss of Money, Securities or Other Property which the Named Insured’s client, customer or vendor intended to transfer, pay or deliver to the Named Insured, but which was transferred, paid or delivered to an unintended party due to Client Phishing Fraud; and
[3322|Normal] the cost of reimbursing the Named Insured’s client, customer or vendor for their direct loss of Money, Securities or Other Property due to Client Phishing Fraud, provided such reimbursement is made by the Named Insured with Insurers prior written approval.
[3323|Normal] Cloud Provider
[3324|Normal] means any third party that provides computing resources to the Named Insured that are delivered as a service over a network or the internet (commonly known as “cloud computing”), including Software as a Service, Platform as a Service and Infrastructure as a Service.
[3325|Normal] Computer System
[3326|Normal] means an interconnected electronic, wireless, web or similar system, including all computer hardware and software, used to process and store Data or information in an analogue, digital, electronic or wireless format, including, but not limited to, computer programs, Data, operating systems, firmware, servers, media libraries, associated input and output devices, mobile devices, devices that are connected to and controlled by the internet (also known as “smart devices”), networking equipment, websites, extranets, off-line storage facilities (to the extent they hold Data) and electronic backup equipment.
[3327|Normal] Court Attendance Costs
[3328|Normal] means the actual loss of earnings and reasonable costs and expenses incurred by an Insured after a total of three (3) days of required attendance at mediation, arbitration proceedings, hearings, depositions and trials relating to the defense of a Claim under any  Liability Insuring Clause of this Policy.
[3329|Normal] Covered Property
[3330|Normal] means:
[3331|Normal] tangible real and personal property, including Other Property, in which the Named Insured has an insurable interest as of the start of the Period of Insurance;
[3332|Normal] tangible real and personal property, including Other Property, that the Named Insured acquires during the Period of Insurance;
[3333|Normal] property, including Other Property, of others for which the Named Insured had assumed liability prior to loss; and
[3334|Normal] the Named Insured’s financial interest in property, including Other Property, belonging to others.
[3335|Normal] Covered Property does not include currency, Money, Securities, precious metal in bullion form, notes, evidences of debt or title, letters of credit, stamps, tickets or precious and semi-precious stones; fine art; land, water or any other substance in or on land; animals, standing timber or growing crops; watercraft or aircraft; vehicles of Executives or Employees, or vehicles otherwise insured for physical loss or damage; underground mines or mine shafts or any property within such mines or shafts; property in transit; property sold by an Insured under conditional sale, trust agreement,  plan or other deferred payment plan after delivery to customers; satellites; offshore property; dams, water shafts, power tunnels, dikes, levees, gates and flumes; or outside plants, including owned electrical power transmission and distribution lines, beyond 1,000 feet from the Named Insured’s business premises.
[3336|Normal] Cryptojacking
[3337|Normal] means the intentional, unauthorised and malicious use of or access to an Insured Computer System to mine for digital currency.
[3338|Normal] Cyber Extortion Expenses
[3339|Normal] means reasonable and necessary costs and expenses, other than Cyber Extortion Monies, that the Named Insured incurs with Insurers prior written consent as a direct result of a Cyber Extortion Threat, including the cost to retain or hire a third party specialising in IT security to determine the validity and severity of a Cyber Extortion Threat.
[3340|Normal] Cyber Extortion Monies
[3341|Normal] means Money, digital currency of any kind, including bitcoin, or Other Property that the Named Insured pays with Insurers prior written consent to any person or group reasonably believed to be responsible for a Cyber Extortion Threat, to prevent or terminate such Cyber Extortion Threat.
[3342|Normal] Cyber Extortion Threat
[3343|Normal] means a credible threat or series of related credible threats, including a demand for Cyber Extortion Monies, which is directed at the Named Insured to:
[3345|Normal] steal, alter, release, reveal, divulge, disseminate, destroy, publicly disclose or misuse Private Information taken from the Named Insured through unauthorised access to, or unauthorised use of, an Insured Computer System;
[3346|Normal] infect an Insured Computer System with malicious code or ransomware;
[3347|Normal] corrupt, damage or destroy an Insured Computer System;
[3348|Normal] restrict or hinder access to an Insured Computer System, including the threat of a  Attack;
[3349|Normal] perpetrate or carry out a Phishing Attack;
[3350|Normal] steal, alter, release, reveal, divulge, disseminate, destroy, publicly disclose or misuse the Named Insured’s confidential or proprietary information, or the Personally Identifiable Information of an Insured; or
[3351|Normal] damage the Named Insured’s reputation or the Named Insured’s brand by posting false or misleading comments about the Named Insured or the Named Insured’s organisation on social media websites or platforms.
[3352|Normal] A series of continuing Cyber Extortion Threats, related or repeated Cyber Extortion Threats, or multiple Cyber Extortion Threats resulting from the same attack, event or incident will be considered a single Cyber Extortion Threat and will be considered to have occurred at the time the first of such Cyber Extortion Threats occurred.
[3353|Normal] Cyber Limit of Liability
[3354|Normal] means the amounts stated in the Schedule which shall be the maximum amount payable by Insurers under each Insuring Clause for each Claim, and in the aggregate for all Claims first made during the Period of Insurance, including Defence costs, where applicable and regardless of the number of Claims or claimants. If the Cyber Limit of Liability for any Insuring Clause is exhausted, the Insurer's obligations under that Insuring Clause shall cease. The Maximum Aggregate Limit of Liability stated in the Schedule shall be the maximum amount payable by Insurers under this Policy for all Claims first made during the Period of Insurance, including Defence costs, where applicable, regardless of the number of Claims, claimants or Insuring Clauses. All amounts the Insurer pays under this Policy will reduce, and may completely exhaust, the Maximum Aggregate Limit of Indemnity.
[3355|Normal] Cyber Operation
[3356|Normal] means the use of a Computer System by, at the direction, or under the control of a sovereign state to disrupt, deny, degrade, manipulate or destroy information in a Computer System of or in another sovereign state.
[3357|Normal] Damages
[3358|Normal] means:
[3359|Normal] a monetary judgment, award or settlement including liquidated, punitive, exemplary or multiple awards but only to the extent that they are insurable under the law pursuant to which this Policy is construed;
[3360|Normal] awarded legal fees and costs; and
[3361|Normal] prejudgment and post-judgment interest awarded against an Insured on that part of any judgment paid or to be paid by the Insurer.
[3362|Normal] Damages  not include any:
[3363|Normal] of the Insured’s future profits or royalties, restitution or disgorgement of any of the Insured’s profits;
[3364|Normal] of the costs to comply with orders granting injunctive or non-monetary relief, including specific performance, or any agreement to provide such relief;
[3365|Normal] loss of any Insured’s fees or profits, the return or offset of any Insured’s fees or charges, or any Insured’s commissions or royalties provided or contracted to be provided;
[3366|Normal] taxes, fines, penalties or sanctions;
[3367|Normal] contractual liquidated Damages that exceed the amount for which the Insured would have been liable in the absence of the contract;
[3368|Normal] any amount which an Insured is not financially or legally obligated to pay;
[3369|Normal] disgorgement of any remuneration or financial advantage to which an Insured was not legally entitled;
[3370|Normal] settlements negotiated without Insurers prior written approval;
[3371|Normal] monetary judgments, awards, settlements or any other amounts which are uninsurable under the law pursuant to which this Policy is construed or any legal fees and costs awarded pursuant to such judgments, awards or settlements; or
[3372|Normal] PCI DSS Fines and Assessments.
[3374|Normal] Data
[3375|Normal] means information, facts, concepts, code or any other information of any kind that is recorded or transmitted in a form to be used, accessed, processed, transmitted or stored by a computer system.
[3376|Normal] Defence Costs
[3377|Normal] means all reasonable costs and expenses incurred, with the Insurer’s prior written consent, in the investigation, defence and settlement of any Claim. Defense Costs does not include the Insured's own costs and expenses including any wages or salaries of an Insured, or fees, overhead or other charges incurred by or paid to any Insured for any time spent in co-operating in the investigation or defence of a Claim or a potential Claim.
[3378|Normal] Denial of Service Attack
[3379|Normal] means an event caused by unauthorised or unexpected interference or a malicious attack, which is intended by the perpetrator to overwhelm the capacity of a Computer System by sending an excessive volume of Data to such Computer System to prevent access to such Computer System.
[3380|Normal] Dependent System Failure
[3381|Normal] means an unplanned outage, interruption, failure, suspension or degradation of service of a Service Provider Computer System, however caused.
[3382|Normal] Digital Assets
[3383|Normal] means Data and computer programs that exist in an Insured Computer System. Digital Assets does not include computer hardware.
[3384|Normal] Digital Assets Loss
[3385|Normal] means reasonable and necessary expenses and costs that the Named Insured incurs to replace, recreate or restore Digital Assets to the same equivalent standard, condition and functionality as was the case immediately before the Digital Assets were damaged, destroyed, altered, misused or stolen, including research costs incurred in recreating Digital Assets, expenses for materials and machine time, and amounts representing Employee work time to replace, recreate or restore Digital Assets, which will be determined on a predefined billable hour or per-hour basis as based upon the Named Insured’s schedule of Employee billable hours. Digital Assets Loss will be determined in accordance with the Loss Determination Section of this Policy.
[3386|Normal] Employee
[3387|Normal] means:
[3388|Normal] any person employed by the Named Insured under a contract of service, training or apprenticeship; and
[3389|Normal] any voluntary worker; and
[3390|Normal] any seasonal or temporary personnel; and
[3391|Normal] any self-employed person or entity acting as a freelance consultant;
[3392|Normal] but only if such person or entity is working under the Named Insured’s direction, control and supervision.
[3393|Normal] Escrow Account
[3394|Normal] means a bank account held or maintained by the Named Insured on behalf of the Named Insured’s client or customer.
[3395|Normal] Essential Service
[3396|Normal] means any service that is essential for the proper operation and maintenance of vital functions of a sovereign state, including, but not limited to, financial services (including services related to financial institutions and associated financial market infrastructure), health services, utility services, emergency services, and/or services that are essential for the proper operation of the food, energy and/or transportation sector.
[3397|Normal] Excess
[3398|Normal] means the first amount paid in respect of each Claim as stated in the Schedule, inclusive of Defence Costs.  The Cyber Limit of Liability is additional to the Excess.
[3399|Normal] Executive
[3400|Normal] means any of the Named Insured’s directors or officers, including any chief executive officer, chief financial officer, chief operations officer, chief technology officer, chief information officer, chief privacy officer, general counsel or other in-house lawyer, and risk manager, or any person in a functionally equivalent position.
[3401|Normal] Financial Account
[3402|Normal] means the Named Insured’s Account, any Client Account and any Escrow Account.
[3403|Normal] Financial Fraud
[3404|Normal] means any of the following:
[3405|Normal] an intentional, unauthorised and fraudulent written, electronic or telephonic instruction transmitted to a financial institution, directing such institution to debit, transfer, withdraw or disburse Money or Securities from a Financial Account, which instruction purports to have been transmitted by the Named Insured or an Executive or Employee, but was in fact fraudulently transmitted by a third party without the Named Insured’s knowledge or consent; or
[3406|Normal] the theft of Money or Securities from a Financial Account or the Named Insured’s corporate credit cards as a result of a Hacking Attack.
[3407|Normal] Financial Fraud Loss
[3408|Normal] means:
[3409|Normal] the loss of the Named Insured’s Money or Securities as a direct result of Financial Fraud, and
[3410|Normal] the loss of Money or Securities that the Named Insured sustains to reimburse the Named Insured’s client or customer for the theft of their money or Securities as a direct result of Financial Fraud, provided such reimbursement is made with Insurers prior written consent.
[3411|Normal] Financial Fraud Loss does not include any amounts reimbursed to the Named Insured by any financial institution.
[3412|Normal] First Party Insured Event
[3413|Normal] means with respect to:
[3414|Normal] Insuring Clause G, an Adverse Media Report, Security Breach or Privacy Breach;
[3415|Normal] Insuring Clauses H, a Security Breach or Privacy Breach;
[3416|Normal] Insuring Clause I, a System Failure;
[3417|Normal] Insuring Clause J, a Cyber Extortion Threat;
[3418|Normal] Insuring Clause K a), a Financial Fraud;
[3419|Normal] Insuring Clause K b), a Telecommunications Fraud or Utilities Fraud;
[3420|Normal] Insuring Clause K c), a Phishing Fraud or Client Phishing Fraud;
[3421|Normal] Insuring Clause L, a Bricking Event;
[3422|Normal] Insuring Clause M, a Hacking Attack;
[3423|Normal] Insuring Clause N, a Security Breach, Privacy Breach, Phishing Attack, System Failure, Cyber Extortion Threat, Financial Fraud, Telecommunications Fraud, Utilities Fraud, Phishing Fraud or Client Phishing Fraud; and
[3424|Normal] Insuring Clause O, Court Attendance Costs incurred by the Insured.
[3425|Normal] Hacking Attack
[3426|Normal] means any of the following directed at or enacted upon an Insured Computer System:
[3427|Normal] unauthorised access to, or unauthorised use of, an Insured Computer System, including any such unauthorised access or unauthorised use resulting from the theft of a password from an Insured Computer System or from an Insured;
[3428|Normal] a  Attack against an Insured Computer System;
[3429|Normal] infection of an Insured Computer System by malicious code, or the transmission of malicious code from an Insured Computer System; or
[3430|Normal] an Act of Cyber Terrorism.
[3431|Normal] Impacted State
[3432|Normal] means a sovereign state where a Cyber Operation has had a major detrimental impact on:
[3433|Normal] a)	the functioning of that sovereign state due to disruption of the availability, integrity or delivery of an Essential Service in that sovereign state; and/or
[3434|Normal] b)	the security or defence of that sovereign state;
[3435|Normal] Provided, however, that an Impacted State shall not result from an attack, or a related series of attacks, solely impacting the Insured.
[3436|Normal] Income Loss
[3437|Normal] means the net profit loss that the Named Insured sustains during the Period of Restoration as a direct result of a System Failure.  Income Loss will be determined in accordance with the Loss Determination Section of this Policy.
[3438|Normal] Informant
[3439|Normal] means any person who provides information regarding an illegal act committed by another person which causes a First Party Insured Event, solely in return for Money that the Named Insured pays or promises to pay.
[3440|Normal] Informant does not include:
[3441|Normal] any person who commits an illegal act which causes a First Party Insured Event, whether acting alone or in collusion with others;
[3442|Normal] any Insured;
[3443|Normal] any of the Insured’s auditors, whether internal or external;
[3444|Normal] any person or firm hired or retained to investigate a First Party Insured Event; or
[3445|Normal] any person responsible for the supervision or management of a party described in paragraphs (a) through (d) above.
[3446|Normal] Initial Breach Consultation Costs
[3447|Normal] means reasonable and necessary fees that the Named Insured incurs on the Named Insured’s behalf, or on behalf of a party for whom the Named Insured is Vicariously Liable, to retain qualified legal counsel to provide the Named Insured with initial advice regarding the appropriate response to an actual or suspected Privacy Breach or Security Breach. Initial Breach Consultation Costs will not be subject to an Excess if the Named Insured retains counsel pre-approved by Insurers.
[3448|Normal] Insured
[3449|Normal] means the Named Insured and the following as relating to the Named Insured:
[3450|Normal] the Named Insured’s current or previous partners, directors, principals, members or Employees;
[3451|Normal] any other person who becomes a partner, director, principal, member or Employee of the Named Insured; and
[3452|Normal] any entity that becomes an additional Insured under the terms of the Material Changes section of this Policy.
[3453|Normal] Insured Computer System
[3454|Normal] means:
[3455|Normal] a Computer System that is owned and operated by the Named Insured or that is leased to the Named Insured and operated by the Named Insured; and any Insured Telecommunications System;
[3456|Normal] with respect to Insuring Clauses B, C, D, G and J only, Insured Computer System also includes a Computer System operated by a BPO Service Provider or an Outsourced IT Service Provider, which is used to provide services to the Named Insured, or for processing, maintaining, hosting or storing Data for the Named Insured, pursuant to a written contract with the Named Insured to provide such services; and
[3457|Normal] with respect to Insuring Clauses E and F only, Insured Computer System also includes Business Equipment, but only while owned and operated by the Named Insured.
[3458|Normal] Insured Location
[3459|Normal] means, and is limited to, the Named Insured’s business premises.
[3460|Normal] Insured Telecommunications System
[3461|Normal] means any telecommunications system that is owned, rented, leased, licensed or borrowed by the Named Insured and under the Named Insured’s direct operational control.
[3462|Normal] Insurer
[3463|Normal] means HCC International Insurance Company PLC.
[3464|Normal] Interruption Expenses
[3465|Normal] means reasonable and necessary expenses, excluding Special Expenses, incurred by the Named Insured to avoid or minimise the suspension of the Named Insured’s business as a result of a System Failure, which the Named Insured would not have incurred in the absence of such System Failure, including, but not limited to, the use of rented/leased external equipment, substitution of other work or production procedures, use of third party services or additional staff expenditures or labour costs. The amount of Interruption Expenses recoverable shall not exceed the amount by which the covered Income Loss is reduced by such incurred expenses.
[3466|Normal] Media Material
[3467|Normal] means communicative material of any kind or nature used in the advertising, publicity or promotion of the Named Insured’s own  which the Named Insured is responsible, including, but not limited to, words, pictures, sounds, images, graphics, code and Data, regardless of the method or medium of communication of such material or the purpose for which the communication is intended. Media Material does not include any tangible Products.
[3468|Normal] Merchant Services Agreement
[3469|Normal] means an agreement between the Named Insured and an Acquiring Bank, Card Association, brand, network, credit or debit card processor, independent sales organization, gateway, or membership service, which enables the Named Insured to accept payment by credit card, debit card or prepaid card.
[3470|Normal] Money
[3471|Normal] means a medium of exchange in current use and authorised or adopted by a domestic or foreign government, including, but not limited to, currency, coins, bank notes, bullion,  cheques, registered cheques and money orders.
[3472|Normal] Multimedia Wrongful Act
[3473|Normal] means any of the following, whether actual or alleged, but only if directly resulting from the dissemination of Media Material by an Insured:
[3474|Normal] defamation or other tort related to disparagement of character, harm to reputation or feelings of any person or organisation including libel, slander or defamation, product disparagement and malicious falsehood, trade libel or any claim relating to outrage or emotional distress, if directly resulting from the foregoing;
[3475|Normal] unintentional breach of confidentiality or other invasion, infringement or interference with rights of privacy or publicity including false light, intrusion upon a person’s seclusion and the public disclosure of private facts;
[3476|Normal] unintentional infringement of intellectual property rights including copyright, title, slogan, trademark, domain name or metatag, moral rights, misappropriation of, formats, characters, trade names, character names, titles, plots, musical compositions, voices, slogans, graphic material or artwork, passing off and plagiarism and commercial appropriation of name or likeness;
[3477|Normal] negligence in Media Material, including a Claim alleging harm to any person or entity that acted or failed to act in reliance upon such Media Material;
[3478|Normal] false arrest, detention or imprisonment;
[3479|Normal] trespass, wrongful entry or eviction, eavesdropping, or other invasion of the right of private occupancy; or
[3480|Normal] unfair competition, but only when arising out of a peril described in paragraphs a) through f) above.
[3481|Normal] Named Insured
[3482|Normal] means the company or firm stated in the Schedule as Insured, but shall not include:
[3483|Normal] the current or previous partners, directors, principals, members or Employees of any company or firm stated in the Schedule; or
[3484|Normal] any other person who becomes a partner, director, principal, member or Employee of any company or firm stated in the Schedule.
[3485|Normal] Named Insured’s Account
[3486|Normal] means a business account maintained by the Named Insured at a financial institution from which the Named Insured, or any Insured authorized by e Named Insured, may request the transfer, payment or delivery of Money or Securities.
[3487|Normal] Notification
[3488|Normal] means the Named Insured’s written notice to affected individuals in the event of a Security Breach or Privacy Breach, whether such written notice is made by the Named Insured voluntarily or to comply with Privacy Regulations.
[3489|Normal] Notification Expenses
[3490|Normal] means reasonable and necessary expenses that the Named Insured incurs on the Named Insured’s own behalf, or on behalf of a party for whom the Named Insured is Vicariously Liable, to provide Notification of a Security Breach or Privacy Breach, including printing costs, mailing and postage expenses, and the costs to engage a third party to mail Notification letters and prepare substitute or website notices.
[3491|Normal] Occurrence
[3492|Normal] means the sum of all individual covered losses, or a series of individual covered losses, under Insuring Clause M that are directly caused by any one Hacking Attack.
[3493|Normal] Operations
[3494|Normal] means the Named Insured’s business activities occurring at an Insured Location which rely on Covered Property.
[3495|Normal] Other Property
[3496|Normal] means any tangible property, other than Money or Securities, which has intrinsic value.
[3497|Normal] Outsourced IT Service Provider
[3498|Normal] means a third party that provides information technology services to the Named Insured, under a written contract with the Named Insured to provide such services, including, but not limited to, hosting, security management, co-location, and Data storage. Outsourced IT Service Provider includes any Cloud Provider.
[3499|Normal] PCI Data Security Standard (known as PCI DSS)
[3500|Normal] means the Payment Card Industry Security Standards Council Data Security Standard in effect now, or as hereafter amended, which all merchants and processors must follow when storing, processing and transmitting cardholder Data.
[3501|Normal] PCI DSS Demand
[3502|Normal] means a written demand for PCI DSS Fines and Assessments received by the Insured directly or indirectly from or through an Acquiring Bank, Card Association or payment card processor due to the Insured’s non-compliance with the PCI Data Security Standard, or a request for information received by the Insured from an Acquiring Bank, Card Association or payment card processor regarding a suspected Security Breach or Privacy Breach.
[3503|Normal] PCI DSS Fines and Assessments
[3504|Normal] means monetary fines, penalties or assessments, including fraud recoveries, card reissuance costs, operational expenses or compliance case costs, which the Insured is legally obligated to pay under the terms of a Merchant Services Agreement, but only where such monetary fines, penalties or assessments result from a Security Breach or Privacy Breach.
[3505|Normal] Period of Indemnity
[3506|Normal] means the period beginning on the earlier of the date of Notification or the first Adverse Media Report (whichever applies), and ending on the earlier of:
[3507|Normal] the date when gross revenues are restored to the level they had been prior to Notification or the first Adverse Media Report (whichever applies); or
[3508|Normal] 180 consecutive days after the date of Notification or the first Adverse Media Report (whichever applies).
[3510|Normal] The Period of Indemnity shall not be affected by the expiration of the Period of Insurance.
[3511|Normal] Period of Insurance
[3512|Normal] means that as stated in the Schedule.
[3513|Normal] Period of Restoration
[3514|Normal] means the period beginning on the date when the System Failure began and ending on the earlier of:
[3515|Normal] the date when an Insured Computer System is restored or could have been repaired or restored with reasonable speed to the same condition, functionality and level of service that existed prior to the System Failure, plus a maximum of thirty (30) additional consecutive days after the restoration of an Insured Computer System to allow for restoration of the Named Insured’s business; or
[3516|Normal] the last day of the period stated in the Schedule as the Period of Restoration for Insuring Clause I (System Failure).
[3517|Normal] Personally Identifiable Information
[3518|Normal] means any driving license or other government-issued identification number; unpublished telephone number; savings account, current account, credit card or debit card number each when in combination with the security code, access code, password or pin for such account or card number; any personal data as defined under the Data Protection Act 2018 or the General Data Protection Regulation 2016/679 or any amending or superseding legislation; any private personal information as defined under the law of a country other than the United Kingdom, which law is intended to provide for the protection of such private personal information; not including any lawfully available data accessible by the general public.
[3519|Normal] Phishing Attack
[3520|Normal] means the use by a third party of fraudulent and intentionally misleading telephone calls, emails, texts, instant messages or other electronic communications or malicious websites to impersonate the Named Insured, the Named Insured’s brand, the Named Insured’s services or Products to solicit Private Information from an Executive or Employee.
[3521|Normal] Phishing Fraud
[3522|Normal] means the malicious use of intentionally misleading telephone calls, emails, texts, instant messages or other electronic communications or malicious websites to fraudulently induce an Insured to:
[3523|Normal] transfer or deliver Other Property to an unintended party by impersonating another Insured or the Named Insured’s client, the Named Insured’s customer or the Named Insured’s vendor; or
[3524|Normal] transfer or disburse Money or Securities from a Financial Account to an unintended party by impersonating another Insured or the Named Insured’s client, the Named Insured’s customer or the Named Insured’s vendor.
[3525|Normal] Phishing Fraud Loss
[3526|Normal] means:
[3527|Normal] the loss of Money, Securities or Other Property that the Named Insured sustains due to Phishing Fraud;
[3528|Normal] the loss of Money or Securities that the Named Insured sustains to reimburse the Named Insured’s client or customer for the loss of their Money or Securities as a direct result of Phishing Fraud, provided such reimbursement is made with Insurers prior written approval; and
[3529|Normal] expenses that the Named Insured incurs with Insurers prior written approval to create and issue a specific press release or to establish a specific website to advise the Named Insured’s customers and prospective customers of Phishing Fraud.
[3530|Normal] Print Media
[3531|Normal] means newspapers, newsletters, magazines, books and literary works in any form, brochures or other types of publications, and advertising materials including packaging, photographs and digital images.
[3532|Normal] Privacy Breach
[3533|Normal] means any of the following:
[3534|Normal] the unauthorised collection, disclosure, use, access, destruction or modification of Private Information;
[3535|Normal] the inability to access or failure to provide Private Information;
[3536|Normal] the theft or loss of Private Information, including the theft or loss of Private Information stored on an unsecured Data storage or mobile device, including any smartphone, tablet or laptop which is owned by the Named Insured and operated by the Insured, or owned and operated by an Employee or Executive who has agreed in writing to the Named Insured’s corporate mobile device acceptable use and security policy (also known as a “Bring Your Own Device” policy);
[3537|Normal] the surrender of Private Information in a Phishing Attack;
[3538|Normal] failure to implement, maintain or comply with privacy policies and procedures stating the Named Insured’s obligations relating to Private Information, including but not limited to the Named Insured’s Privacy Policy;
[3539|Normal] failure to develop or administer an identity theft prevention program;
[3540|Normal] failure to implement specific security practices with respect to Private Information, as required by any statute, rule, regulation or other law;
[3541|Normal] an infringement or violation of any rights to privacy;
[3542|Normal] breach of a person’s right of publicity, false light or intrusion upon a person’s seclusion;
[3543|Normal] failure to comply with Privacy Regulations pertaining to an Insured’s responsibilities with respect to Private Information, but only with respect to an act listed in paragraphs (a) through (h) above; or
[3544|Normal] failure to comply with Privacy Regulations prohibiting unfair or deceptive trade practices or consumer fraud pertaining to an Insured’s responsibilities with respect to Private Information, but only with respect to an act listed in paragraphs a) through h) above.
[3545|Normal] A series of continuing Privacy Breaches, related or repeated Privacy Breaches, or multiple Privacy Breaches resulting from the same event or incident will be considered a single Privacy Breach and will be considered to have occurred at the time the first of such Privacy Breaches occurred.
[3546|Normal] Privacy Breach Response Costs
[3547|Normal] means
[3548|Normal] Initial Breach Consultation Costs;
[3549|Normal] reasonable and necessary Public Relations Expenses that the Named Insured incurs, with Insurers prior written approval, prior to or following the publication of an Adverse Media Report to avert or mitigate any material damage to the Named Insured’s reputation or the Named Insured’s brand, which results or reasonably could result from the Adverse Media Report;
[3550|Normal] reasonable and necessary legal fees that the Named Insured incurs on the Named Insured’s own behalf or on behalf of a party for whom the Named Insured is Vicariously Liable to:
[3551|Normal] determine the scope, cause and extent of an actual or suspected Privacy Breach or Security Breach;
[3552|Normal] determine the applicability of, and the Named Insured’s obligations to comply with, Privacy Regulations due to an actual or suspected Privacy Breach; and
[3553|Normal] draft a Notification letter to be sent to parties affected by a Privacy Breach.
[3554|Normal] reasonable and necessary fees and costs that the Named Insured incurs on the Named Insured’s behalf, or on behalf of a party for whom the Named Insured is Vicariously Liable, to retain a qualified IT forensics firm or computer security expert to investigate and identify the source and scope of a Security Breach or Privacy Breach; and
[3555|Normal] overtime salaries of non-exempt Employees assigned to handle enquiries from parties affected by a Privacy Breach.
[3556|Normal] Privacy Policy
[3557|Normal] means the Named Insured’s published policies provided to Employees or third parties that govern the collection, use, disclosure, correction, dissemination, confidentiality, integrity, accuracy or availability of Private Information.
[3558|Normal] Privacy Regulations
[3559|Normal] means foreign, federal, state or local statutes, rules, regulations and other laws, as they currently exist and as amended, associated with the confidentiality, access, control, and use of Private Information.
[3560|Normal] Privacy Regulatory Proceeding
[3561|Normal] means a civil or administrative proceeding, regulatory action, request for information or investigation instituted against an Insured by a Regulatory Authority because of a Security Breach or Privacy Breach. Privacy Regulatory Proceeding does not include a PCI DSS Demand.
[3562|Normal] Private Information
[3563|Normal] means:
[3564|Normal] proprietary or confidential information owned by a third party that is in the care, custody or control of the Insured, or is used by the Insured with the consent of such third party; and
[3565|Normal] Personally Identifiable Information.
[3566|Normal] Products
[3567|Normal] means any tangible goods or devices that are manufactured, produced, processed, prepared, assembled, packaged, , sold, handled or distributed by the Named Insured, by others trading under the Named Insured’s name, or by a person or organisation whose business or assets have been acquired by the Named Insured; and containers, materials, parts or equipment furnished in connection with such goods or devices.
[3568|Normal] Programming Error
[3569|Normal] means an error which occurs during the development or encoding of a computer program, software or application and which would, when in operation, result in a malfunction or incorrect operation of a Computer System.
[3570|Normal] Property Damage
[3571|Normal] means physical injury to, or impairment, destruction or corruption of, any tangible property, including the loss of use thereof. Data is not considered tangible property. Property Damage does not include the loss of use of the Named Insured’s computer hardware or electronic equipment which is caused by a Bricking Event.
[3572|Normal] Property Damage Claim
[3573|Normal] means any of the following alleging a Property Damage Wrongful Act:
[3574|Normal] a written demand for Damages or non-monetary relief made against an Insured for Property Damage caused by a Security Breach or Privacy Breach;
[3575|Normal] a written request received by an Insured to enter into a Standstill Agreement, a stay or to waive a statute of limitations relating to either a pre-action litigation correspondence or legal proceedings against an Insured for Property Damage caused by a Security Breach or Privacy Breach; or
[3576|Normal] the service of a civil lawsuit or the institution of arbitration or other alternative dispute resolution proceedings against an Insured seeking Damages for Property Damage caused by a Security Breach or Privacy Breach.
[3577|Normal] Property Damage Wrongful Act
[3578|Normal] means an Insured’s actual or alleged failure to prevent or avoid Property Damage caused by a Security Breach or Privacy Breach.
[3579|Normal] Public Relations Expenses
[3580|Normal] means expenses that the Named Insured incurs to retain or hire a  public relations consultant or public relations firm to protect or restore the Named Insured’s reputation, which is damaged or reasonably could be damaged by an Adverse Media Report.
[3581|Normal] Regulatory Authority
[3582|Normal] means the governmental agency or regulatory authority responsible for investigating and enforcing Privacy Regulations, including an authorised Data Protection Authority under the EU General Data Protection Regulation.
[3583|Normal] Regulatory Compensatory Award
[3584|Normal] means a sum of Money which an Insured is legally obligated to pay as a Regulatory Authority’s award or fund for parties affected by a Privacy Breach, due to an adverse judgment or settlement arising out of a Privacy Regulatory Proceeding, including consumer redress funds. Regulatory Compensatory Award does not include any criminal fines or penalties of any nature whatsoever.
[3585|Normal] Regulatory Fines and Penalties
[3586|Normal] means civil fines or penalties imposed by a Regulatory Authority against an Insured as a result of a Privacy Regulatory Proceeding. Regulatory Fines and Penalties does not include any amounts deemed uninsurable under the law pursuant to which this Policy is construed, criminal fines or penalties of any nature or PCI DSS Fines and Assessments.
[3587|Normal] Reward Expenses
[3588|Normal] means the reasonable amount that the Named Insured pays with Insurers prior written approval to an Informant for information not otherwise available which leads to the arrest and conviction of any person who commits an illegal act that causes a First Party Insured Event.
[3589|Normal] Securities
[3590|Normal] means negotiable or non-negotiable instruments or contracts representing Money or Other Property but does not include Money.
[3591|Normal] Security and Privacy Wrongful Act
[3592|Normal] means any of the following, but only if actually or allegedly committed by an Insured:
[3593|Normal] the failure to prevent or hinder a Security Breach or Privacy Breach;
[3594|Normal] the failure to timely disclose a Security Breach or Privacy Breach affecting Private Information;
[3595|Normal] the failure to dispose of Private Information within the required period in violation of Privacy Regulations;
[3596|Normal] the failure to prevent the transmission of malicious code or computer virus from an Insured Computer System to the Computer System of a third party;
[3597|Normal] a Privacy Breach;
[3598|Normal] the failure to prevent or hinder participation by an Insured Computer System in a  Attack directed against the internet site or Computer System of a third party; or
[3599|Normal] infliction of emotional distress or mental anguish, but only if directly resulting from a peril described in paragraphs a) through f) above.
[3600|Normal] Security Breach
[3601|Normal] means any of the following, whether a specifically targeted attack or a generally distributed attack:
[3602|Normal] a Hacking Attack; or
[3603|Normal] the theft or loss of an unsecured Data storage or mobile device containing Private Information, including any smartphone, tablet or laptop which is owned by the Named Insured and operated by an Insured, or owned and operated by an Employee or Executive who has agreed in writing to the Named Insured’s corporate mobile device acceptable use and security policy (also known as a “Bring Your Own Device” policy).
[3604|Normal] A series of continuing Security Breaches, related or repeated Security Breaches, or multiple Security Breaches resulting from a continuing attack, event, incident or failure of computer security will be considered a single Security Breach and will be considered to have occurred at the time the first of such Security Breaches occurred.
[3605|Normal] Service Provider Computer System
[3606|Normal] means a Computer System that is owned or leased by, and under the direct operational control of, a BPO service provider or Outsourced IT Service Provider.
[3607|Normal] Special Expenses
[3608|Normal] means reasonable and necessary costs and expenses that the Named Insured incurs to:
[3609|Normal] prevent, preserve, minimise, or mitigate any further damage to Digital Assets, including the reasonable and necessary fees and expenses of specialists, outside consultants or forensic experts;
[3610|Normal] preserve critical evidence of any criminal or malicious wrongdoing;
[3611|Normal] purchase replacement licenses for computer programs because the copy protection system or access control software was damaged or destroyed by a System Failure; or
[3612|Normal] notify affected parties of a System Failure.
[3613|Normal] System Failure
[3614|Normal] means an unplanned outage, interruption, failure, suspension or degradation of service of an Insured Computer System, including, but not limited to, any such outage, interruption, failure, suspension or degradation of service caused directly by a Hacking Attack, Voluntary Shutdown, administrative error or Programming Error. System Failure does not include any Dependent System Failure.
[3615|Normal] Telecommunications Fraud
[3616|Normal] means the intentional, unauthorised and fraudulent gaining of access to outgoing telephone service through infiltration and manipulation of an Insured Telecommunications System.
[3617|Normal] Telecommunications Fraud Loss
[3618|Normal] means the charges that the Named Insured incurs for unauthorised calls directly resulting from Telecommunications Fraud.
[3619|Normal] Unauthorised Trading
[3620|Normal] means trading, which, at the time of the trade, exceeds permitted financial limits or is outside of permitted product lines.
[3621|Normal] Utilities Fraud
[3622|Normal] means the intentional, unauthorised and fraudulent use of or access to an Insured Computer System as a direct result of a Hacking Attack, including Cryptojacking, which results in the fraudulent use of electricity, water, natural gas, oil, internet access, mobile Data, cable or satellite services, sewage, Cloud Provider services or other utilities, services or resources.
[3623|Normal] Utilities Fraud Loss
[3624|Normal] means the overage charges or increased expenses that the Named Insured incurs as a direct result of Utilities Fraud, provided that:
[3625|Normal] such overage charges or increased expenses are charged to the Named Insured in a periodic billing statement by the provider of the utility, service or resource, pursuant to a written contract or agreement executed between the Named Insured and such provider before the Utilities Fraud occurred; and
[3626|Normal] such overage charges or increased expenses are not charged at a flat fee which does not scale with the rate of use of the utility, service or resource.
[3627|Normal] In determining the amount of Utilities Fraud Loss payable, due consideration will be given to  Insured’s prior utility expenses and the probable utility expenses the Named Insured would have incurred had no Utilities Fraud occurred.
[3628|Normal] Vicariously Liable
[3629|Normal] means the Named Insured’s legal responsibility for the liability of others, including legal responsibility the Named Insured assumes in a contract. The existence of vicarious liability will not create or confer any rights or duties under this Policy to any third party, other than as provided in this Definition.
[3630|Normal] Voluntary Shutdown
[3631|Normal] means an intentional and discretionary total or partial shutdown of an Insured Computer System based upon an Executive’s reasonable belief that such total or partial shutdown is necessary to mitigate, minimise or avoid the economic impact of a Hacking Attack on the Named Insured’s business.
[3632|Normal] Waiting Period
[3633|Normal] means the amount of time, as set forth in the Schedule, that must elapse before any loss or expenses may be payable under Insuring Clauses H (BrandGuard) or I b) (System Failure: Non-Physical Business Interruption). The Waiting Period applies to each Period of Restoration and Period of Indemnity.
[3634|Normal] War
[3635|Normal] means:
[3636|Normal] a)	armed conflict involving physical force by one sovereign state against another sovereign state, whether either such state is fully or partially recognised, and whether war has been declared or not; and/or
[3637|Normal] b)	civil war, rebellion, revolution, insurrection, riot or civil commotion, military or usurped power or martial law.
[3640|Normal] Wrongful Act
[3642|Normal] means with respect to:
[3643|Normal] Insuring Clause A, a Multimedia Wrongful Act;
[3644|Normal] Insuring Clauses B, a Security and Privacy Wrongful Act;
[3645|Normal] Insuring Clauses C and D, a Security Breach or Privacy Breach;
[3646|Normal] Insuring Clause E, a Bodily Injury Wrongful Act; and
[3647|Normal] Insuring Clause F, a Property Damage Wrongful Act.
[3649|Normal] Exclusions applicable to all Insuring Clauses
[3650|Normal] This Policy does not apply to any Claim:
[3651|Normal] made by or on behalf of an Insured against another Insured. However, this Exclusion does not apply to a Claim under Insuring Clause B (Security and Privacy Liability) which is brought by any past, present or future Employee against the Named Insured.
[3653|Normal] based upon, arising from or in any way involving any of the following committed by an Insured, whether acting alone or in collusion with other persons:
[3654|Normal] a , intentional, deliberate, malicious, fraudulent, dishonest or criminal act or omission;
[3655|Normal] any intentional violation of law; or
[3656|Normal] the gaining of any profit or advantage to which an Insured is not legally entitled.
[3657|Normal] However, Insurers may pay Defence Costs incurred in connection with the defence of any conduct described in this Exclusion until such time as there is a final, non-appealable adjudication in a judicial, administrative or alternative dispute proceeding, or by an Insured’s own admission in a proceeding or otherwise. Insurers will have the right to recover Defence Costs incurred in defending any such Claim from any Insured found to have committed the conduct described in this Exclusion. This Exclusion does not apply to any Insured who did not commit, participate in or have prior knowledge of any conduct to which this Exclusion would otherwise apply.
[3659|Normal] for Bodily Injury or Property Damage. However, this Exclusion does not apply to a Bodily Injury Claim, Property Damage Claim or Occurrence.
[3661|Normal] based upon, arising from or in any way involving any of the following, regardless of any other cause or event that contributes concurrently or in any sequence to the Claim:
[3662|Normal] electrical or mechanical failures or interruption, including electrical disturbance, spike, brownout or blackout;
[3663|Normal] any regional, countrywide or global outage, failure, disruption or reduction in supply of any utility service or infrastructure, including electricity, gas, water, telephone, cable, internet, satellite or telecommunications, or any failure, outage, disruption, degradation or termination of any critical part of such service or infrastructure; or
[3664|Normal] the cessation of the Named Insured’s business activities due to a shutdown by order of any public authority for whatever reason.
[3666|Normal] based upon, arising from or in any way involving the actual or alleged inaccurate, inadequate or incomplete description of the price of goods, Products or services.
[3668|Normal] based upon, arising from or in any way involving any breach of any express, implied, actual or constructive contract, warranty, guarantee or promise. However, this Exclusion does not apply to:
[3669|Normal] any liability or obligation an Insured would have had in the absence of such contract, warranty, guarantee or promise;
[3670|Normal] an actual or alleged breach of the Named Insured’s Privacy Policy;
[3671|Normal] an actual or alleged breach of an express, implied, actual or constructive contract, warranty, guarantee or promise to protect Private Information;
[3672|Normal] a Claim under Insuring Clause B (Security and Privacy Liability) for an unintentional breach by an Insured of the provisions of a confidentiality or non-disclosure agreement relating to the confidentiality of Private Information; or
[3673|Normal] a Claim under Insuring Clause D (PCI DSS Liability) for an unintentional breach of the provisions of a Merchant Services Agreement relating to compliance with the PCI DSS Standard.
[3674|Normal] based upon, arising from or in any way involving any liability assumed by any Insured under a contract or agreement. However, this Exclusion does not apply to:
[3675|Normal] any liability an Insured would have had in the absence of such contract or agreement;
[3676|Normal] a Claim under Insuring Clause A (Multimedia Liability) or Insuring Clause B (Security and Privacy Liability) for liability Assumed Under Contract; or
[3677|Normal] a Claim under Insuring Clause D (PCI DSS Liability) for liability for PCI DSS Fines and Assessments assumed by the Named Insured under a Merchant Services Agreement.
[3679|Normal] based upon, arising from or in any way involving seepage, pollution or contamination of any kind, including but not limited to asbestos, smoke, vapor, soot, fumes, acids, alkalis, chemicals and waste. However, this Exclusion does not apply to a Bodily Injury Claim or Property Damage Claim.
[3681|Normal] based upon, arising from or in any way involving Income Loss caused by or resulting from Unauthorised Trading.
[3683|Normal] based upon, arising from or in any way involving;
[3684|Normal] the actual or alleged purchase or sale of Securities;
[3685|Normal] the actual or alleged loss of value of any Securities;
[3686|Normal] the offer of, or solicitation of an offer, to purchase or sell Securities; or
[3687|Normal] the violation of any Securities law.
[3688|Normal] However, Exclusion 10.4) does not apply to a Privacy Regulatory Proceeding or a Claim under Insuring Clause B (Security and Privacy Liability) alleging violation of Securities laws concerning the security, access or use of a customer’s Private Information which was obtained in the course of a Securities transaction.
[3690|Normal] based upon, arising from or in any way involving the actual or alleged government enforcement of any local or foreign regulation.  However, this Exclusion does not apply to a Privacy Regulatory Proceeding.
[3692|Normal] based upon, arising from or in any way involving:
[3693|Normal] any employer-Employee relations, policies, practices, acts or omissions;
[3694|Normal] any actual or alleged refusal to employ any person; or
[3695|Normal] any misconduct with respect to Employees.
[3696|Normal] However, this Exclusion does not apply to a Claim under Insuring Clauses B (Security and Privacy Liability), C (Privacy Regulatory Defense and Penalties) or G (Breach Event Costs) which is based upon or arising from a breach of the Personally Identifiable Information of any Employee.
[3698|Normal] based upon, arising from or in any way involving any actual or alleged harassment or discrimination including, but not limited to, discrimination based on age, , race, gender, creed, national origin, marital status, sexual preferences, disability or pregnancy.
[3700|Normal] arising directly or indirectly from the operation or administration of any pension or other employee benefit scheme or trust fund, or the sale or purchase or dealing in any stocks, shares or securities or the misuse of any information relating to them or the breach of any related legislation or regulation.
[3702|Normal] for any loss, damage, liability, cost or expense:
[3703|Normal] directly or indirectly caused by, resulting from or in connection with any War;
[3704|Normal] resulting from a Cyber Operation carried out as part of any War; or
[3705|Normal] resulting from a Cyber Operation that causes a sovereign state to become an Impacted State;
[3706|Normal] Provided, however, that 3) above shall not apply to the direct or indirect effect of a Cyber Operation on an Insured Computer System or a Service Provider Computer System that is not physically located in an Impacted State but is affected by a Cyber Operation.
[3708|Normal] based upon, arising from or in any way involving:
[3709|Normal] any Insured’s failure to comply with or follow the PCI Data Security Standard or any payment card company rules; or
[3710|Normal] the implementation or maintenance of, or compliance with, any security measures or standards relating to any payment card Data including, but not limited to, any fine or penalty imposed by a payment card company on a merchant bank or payment processor that an Insured has paid or agreed to reimburse or indemnify.
[3711|Normal] However, this Exclusion does not apply to a PCI DSS Demand.
[3713|Normal] based upon, arising from or in any way involving:
[3714|Normal] any actual or alleged unfair competition, price fixing, deceptive trade practices or restraint of trade; or
[3715|Normal] the violation of any antitrust statute, legislation or regulation
[3716|Normal] However, Exclusion 17.1) does not apply to:
[3717|Normal] allegations of unfair competition that form a part of a Claim under Insuring Clauses A (Multimedia Liability), B (Security and Privacy Liability) or C (Privacy Regulatory Defense and Penalties); or
[3718|Normal] allegations of deceptive trade practices that form a part of a Claim under Insuring Clauses B (Security and Privacy Liability) or C (Privacy Regulatory Defense and Penalties).
[3720|Normal] based upon, arising from or in any way involving any actual or alleged infringement of any patent.
[3722|Normal] based upon, arising from or in any way involving the misappropriation, theft, copying, display or publication of any trade secret. However, this Exclusion does not apply to a Claim under Insuring Clause B (Security and Privacy Liability) for failure to prevent the misappropriation of a trade secret which results from a Security and Privacy Wrongful Act.
[3724|Normal] based upon, arising from or in any way involving the confiscation, commandeering, requisition or destruction of, or damage to, computer hardware by order of a government de jure or de facto, or by any public authority for whatever reason.
[3726|Normal] based upon, arising from or in any way involving any unsolicited communication of information or advertising by telephone, email, fax, text or any other means prohibited by law, or any actual or alleged violation of the Telephone Consumer Protection Act (47 U.S.C.§227), the Telemarketing and Consumer Fraud and Abuse Prevention Act (15 U.S.C. §§ 6101-6108), or the CAN-SPAM Act (15 U.S.C. §§ 7701-7713), each as amended, or any regulations promulgated under the foregoing statutes, or any similar U.S federal, state or local law.
[3728|Normal] arising directly or indirectly from:
[3729|Normal] ionising radiations or contamination by radioactivity from any nuclear fuel or from any nuclear waste from the combustion of nuclear fuel;
[3730|Normal] the radioactive, toxic, explosive or other hazardous properties of any explosive nuclear assembly or nuclear component thereof.
[3732|Normal] arising from any act or omission that occurred prior to the Retroactive Date stated in the Schedule.
[3734|Normal] for any loss, cost, liability or expense caused by, resulting from, or in connection with, a Dependent System Failure.
[3736|Normal] Exclusions applicable to all First Party Insuring Clauses
[3737|Normal] Insurers will not be liable under any First Party Insuring Clause of this Policy for:
[3739|Normal] any direct loss, costs or expenses incurred by any person falling within definition a) and b) of the Insured:
[3741|Normal] any liability to any third party for whatever reason, including contractual penalties, Damages or legal costs and expenses of any type.
[3743|Normal] sanctions, fines or penalties imposed by law.
[3745|Normal] any Claim based upon, arising from or in any way involving fire, smoke, explosion, lightning, wind, water, flood, earthquake, volcanic eruption, tidal wave, landslide, hail, force majeure or any other physical event, however caused. However, this Exclusion does not apply to an Occurrence.
[3747|Normal] business interruption loss or costs or expenses resulting from lost productivity, including the throttling or capping of bandwidth by an internet or mobile Data service provider due to Utilities Fraud.
[3749|Normal] Exclusions applicable to Insuring Clauses A (Multimedia Liability) and B (Security and Privacy Liability)
[3750|Normal] This Policy does not apply to any Claim:
[3752|Normal] made directly by or on behalf of any client or customer of the Insured which is based upon a breach of any duty owed by the Insured under a contract to provide professional services.  However, this Exclusion will not apply to any Claim made by a data subject relating to their own Personally Identifiable Information.
[3754|Normal] Exclusion applicable to Insuring Clauses E (Bodily Injury Liability Cover) and F (Property Damage Liability Cover)
[3755|Normal] Insurers will not be liable under Insuring Clauses E and F for:
[3756|Normal] any Bodily Injury Claim or Property Damage Claim based upon, arising from or in any way involving actual or alleged warranties or representations made at any time with respect to the fitness, quality, durability, performance or use of Products, or the providing of, or failure to provide, warnings or instructions for Products.
[3757|Normal] Exclusions applicable to Insuring Clause H (BrandGuard)
[3758|Normal] Insurers will not be liable under Insuring Clause H for any costs,  or expense:
[3760|Normal] that the Named Insured incurs to re-establish the Named Insured’s reputation, including Public Relations Expenses.
[3761|Normal] incurred in any Claim that is insured by any other insurance, except excess insurance.
[3763|Normal] incurred because of an Adverse Media Report that also affects or refers in similar terms to a general security issue, an industry, or the Named Insured’s specific competitors without any specific allegations regarding a Security Breach or Privacy breach committed by the Insured, or by others acting on the Named Insured’s behalf, for whom the Named Insured is legally responsible, including BPO Service Providers or Outsourced IT Service Providers.
[3765|Normal] or any amounts paid or payable under Insuring Clause G (Breach Event Costs).
[3767|Normal] Exclusions applicable to Insuring Clause I (System Failure)
[3768|Normal] Insurers will not be liable under Insuring Clause I for:
[3769|Normal] the cost of restoring, updating or replacing Digital Assets to a level beyond that which existed prior to the System Failure.
[3771|Normal] physical damage to, or the costs to repair or replace, any computer hardware or Data .
[3773|Normal] the economic or market value of Digital Assets.
[3775|Normal] the costs or expenses incurred to identify, patch or remediate software Programming Errors or Computer System vulnerabilities.
[3777|Normal] the cost to upgrade, improve, repair, redesign, reconfigure or maintain an Insured Computer System to a level of functionality beyond that which existed prior to the System Failure.
[3779|Normal] the cost of restoring, replacing or repairing any electronic media.
[3781|Normal] the cost to upgrade, improve, repair, redesign, reconfigure or maintain a Service Provider Computer System.
[3783|Normal] loss of goodwill or harm to the Named Insured’s reputation.
[3784|Normal] Exclusions applicable to Insuring Clause K (Cyber Crime)
[3785|Normal] Insurers will not be liable under Insuring Clause K for:
[3787|Normal] any Claim based upon, arising from or in any way involving any actual or alleged unauthorised acquisition, access, use or disclosure of Private Information that is held or transmitted in any form. However, this Exclusion does not apply to Financial Fraud which directly results from the use of Private Information.
[3789|Normal] any Claim based upon, arising from or in any way involving the seizure, confiscation, nationalisation, requisition or destruction of an Insured Telecommunications System by or under the order of any government or local authority.
[3791|Normal] amounts that have been wholly or partially reversed by a credit card company or financial institution.
[3793|Normal] loss of Other Property arising out of, resulting from or in any way involving the fraudulent or purportedly fraudulent use of a credit or debit card.
[3795|Normal] any Claim based upon, arising from or in any way involving any fraudulent instruction, if the sender, or any person or organisation acting in collusion with the sender, ever had authorised access to the Named Insured’s password, PIN or other security code. However, this Exclusion does not apply to Phishing Fraud Loss.
[3797|Normal] for any Claim arising directly or indirectly from the giving or surrendering of money, Securities or Other Property in any exchange for or purchase of goods, products or services:
[3798|Normal] that are not yet delivered, whether or not fraudulent;
[3799|Normal] that fail to conform to advertised quality or performance; or
[3800|Normal] that fail to conform to the quality or performance expected from the standpoint of the Insured.
[3802|Normal] for any Claim arising directly or indirectly from any potential income, including interest and dividends, not realised by the Named Insured, the Named Insured’s customers or clients.
[3804|Normal] Exclusions applicable to Insuring Clause M (Property Damage Loss)
[3805|Normal] Insurers will not be liable under Insuring Clause M for:
[3806|Normal] any amounts which are covered in whole or in part under any other valid and collectible insurance.
[3808|Normal] costs to upgrade, redesign, reconfigure or maintain an Insured Computer System to a level of functionality beyond that which existed prior to a Hacking Attack.
[3810|Normal] loss of market or loss of use.
[3812|Normal] loss, damage or deterioration resulting from any delay.
[3814|Normal] loss, damage, cost or expense of whatsoever nature caused by or resulting from the actual or threatened malicious use of pathogenic or poisonous biological or chemical materials, regardless of any other cause or event contributing concurrently or in any other sequence thereto.
[3816|Normal] loss resulting from the lack of any of the following services or systems:
[3817|Normal] incoming electricity, fuel, water, gas, steam or refrigerant;
[3818|Normal] outgoing sewerage; or
[3819|Normal] incoming or outgoing voice, Data, video or satellite services.
[3821|Normal] However, this Exclusion does not apply to loss resulting from an outage of any of the foregoing services or systems, if such services or systems are under the Named Insured’s direct operational control and the outage is directly caused by a Hacking Attack.
[3823|Normal] loss resulting from damage caused by changes in temperature or changes in humidity, whether atmospheric or not.
[3824|Normal] Notification and Claims Conditions
[3825|Normal] Claims Notification for all Insuring Clauses apart from Insuring Clauses H (BrandGuard) and M (Property Damage Loss)
[3826|Normal] As a condition precedent to their right to cover under this Policy, an Executive must provide written notice to Insurers, of any Claim as soon as practicable during the Period of Insurance, but no later than sixty (60) days after expiration of the Period of Insurance.
[3828|Normal] Claims Notification for Insuring Clause H (BrandGuard)
[3829|Normal] As a condition precedent to their right to cover under this Policy, an Executive must provide written notice to Insurers, of any Claim during the Period of Indemnity.
[3831|Normal] Claims Notification and Conditions for Insuring Clause M (Property Damage Loss)
[3833|Normal] The Insured's duties in the event of an Occurrence are as follows:
[3834|Normal] As a condition precedent to their right to cover under this Policy, an Executive must provide immediate written notice to Insurers, of any Occurrence;
[3835|Normal] The Named Insured must:
[3836|Normal] make best efforts to protect the Covered Property from further loss or damage;
[3837|Normal] promptly separate the damaged and undamaged property, put it in the best possible order and furnish a complete inventory of the lost, destroyed, damaged and undamaged property showing in detail the quantities, costs, Actual Cash Value, replacement value and amount of loss claimed;
[3838|Normal] give a signed and sworn proof of loss to the Insurers within 120 days after the loss, unless that time is extended in writing by the Insurers. The proof of loss must state the Named Insured’s knowledge and belief as to:
[3839|Normal] the time and origin of the loss;
[3840|Normal] the Named Insured’s interest, and that of all others, in the Covered Property;
[3841|Normal] the Actual Cash Value and replacement value of each item and the amount of loss to each item; all encumbrances; and all other contracts of insurance, whether valid or not, covering any of the Covered Property;
[3842|Normal] any changes in the title, use, occupation, location, possession or exposures of the Covered Property since the effective date of the Period of Insurance; and
[3843|Normal] by whom and for what purpose any Insured Location was occupied on the date of the loss, and whether it then stood on leased ground;
[3844|Normal] include a copy of all descriptions and schedules in all policies and, if required, provide verified plans and specifications of any buildings, fixtures, machinery or equipment destroyed or damaged; and
[3845|Normal] as often as may be reasonably required exhibit to any person designated by Insurers all that remains of any property, submit to examination under oath by any person designated by Insurers and sign all written records of examinations, and produce for examination, at the Insurer's request, all books of accounts, business records, bills, invoices and other vouchers, or certified copies if originals are lost, at such reasonable times and places that may be designated by the Insurer and permit extracts and machine copies to be made.
[3847|Normal] The Insurer has the option to take all or any part of damaged Covered Property at the agreed or appraised value. The Insurer must give written notice to the Named Insured of its intention to do so within thirty (30) days after receipt of proof of loss.
[3848|Normal] There may be no abandonment of any property to the Insurer.
[3849|Normal] This Policy gives control of Covered Property that suffers insured physical damage as follows:
[3850|Normal] the Named Insured will have full rights to the possession and control of damaged Covered Property in the event of insured physical damage to such Covered Property, provided proper testing is done to show which Covered Property is physically damaged;
[3851|Normal] using reasonable judgment, the Named Insured will decide if the physically damaged Covered Property can be reprocessed or sold;
[3852|Normal] Covered Property so judged by the Named Insured to be unfit for reprocessing or selling will not be sold or disposed of except by the Named Insured or with the Named Insured’s consent; and
[3853|Normal] any salvage proceeds shall be paid to the Insurer at the time of loss settlement, or to the Named Insured, if received prior to loss settlement and such proceeds will reduce the amount of loss payable accordingly.
[3854|Normal] If the Named Insured and the Insurer disagree on the value of the Covered Property or the amount of loss to which the Property Damage Loss applies, either party may make written demand for an appraisal of the loss. In this event, each party will select a competent and impartial appraiser. The two appraisers will select an umpire. If they cannot agree, either may request that selection be made by a judge of a court having jurisdiction. The appraisers will state separately the value of the property and amount of loss. If they fail to agree, they will submit their differences to the umpire. A decision agreed to by any two will be binding. Each party will pay its chosen appraiser and bear the other expenses of the appraisal and umpire equally. If there is an appraisal, the Insurer will still retain the right to deny the Claim.
[3856|Normal] Notice of Potential Claim
[3857|Normal] If, during the Period of Insurance, an Executive becomes aware of any incident, act, fact or circumstance that could reasonably be a basis for a Claim under any  Liability Insuring Clause of this Policy, and if the Executive gives written notice to the Insurers during the Period of Insurance that describes:
[3858|Normal] the specific details of the incident, act, fact or circumstance that could reasonably be the basis for the Claim;
[3859|Normal] the possible Damages, Regulatory Fines and Penalties or other amounts to which this Policy applies that may result or has resulted from the incident, act, fact or circumstance; and
[3860|Normal] the details regarding how the Executive first became aware of the incident, act, fact or circumstance,
[3861|Normal] then any Claim arising out of such reported incident, act, fact or circumstance will be considered to be a Claim first made on the date when the Insurers first received written notice complying with the above requirements.
[3863|Normal] Defence, Settlement and Investigation of Claims under the  Liability Insuring Clauses
[3864|Normal] Insurers have the right and duty to defend any Claim under any  Liability Insuring Clause of this Policy, even if the allegations of the Claim are groundless, false or fraudulent, including the right to appoint a lawyer to defend any such Claim.
[3865|Normal] The Insurer's payment of Defence Costs or any other amounts reduces, and may completely exhaust, the Cyber Limit of Liability available to pay Damages, where applicable, under this Policy.
[3866|Normal] The Insurer's duty to defend any Claim, or pay any Damages, Defence Costs or other amounts, shall cease upon exhaustion of the applicable Cyber Limit of Liability or the Maximum Policy Aggregate Limit, whichever is first. Upon exhaustion, the Insurer will have the right to withdraw from the defence of a Claim by tendering control to the Insured.
[3867|Normal] No Insured shall pay any Damages, Defence Costs, Regulatory Compensatory Award, Regulatory Fines and Penalties or PCI DSS Fines and Assessments, or settle or offer to settle any Claim, assume any contractual obligation, admit liability, make any payment, or confess or otherwise consent to any judgment without Insurers prior written approval. Insurers shall not be liable for any Damages, Defence Costs, Regulatory Compensatory Award, Regulatory Fines and Penalties, PCI DSS Fines and Assessments, settlement, judgment, assumed obligation, admitted liability or payment to which the Insurers have not given their prior written approval.
[3868|Normal] Insurers will not settle any Claim or pay any Damages, Regulatory Compensatory Award, Regulatory Fines and Penalties or PCI DSS Fines and Assessments without the Insured’s consent.
[3869|Normal] If an Insured refuses to consent to any settlement or compromise recommended by Insurers that is acceptable to the claimant, and such Insured elects to contest the Claim or continue any legal proceedings in connection with such Claim, the Insurers liability for such Claim shall not exceed:
[3870|Normal] the amount for which the Claim could have been settled, less the remaining Excess, plus Defence Costs incurred up to the date such Insured withheld consent to such settlement, plus
[3871|Normal] seventy percent (70%) of any Defence Costs and Damages, Regulatory Compensatory Award, Regulatory Fines and Penalties or PCI DSS Fines and Assessments, whichever applies, incurred after the date such Insured withheld consent to such settlement or compromise, subject always to all other terms and conditions of this Policy, including, but not limited to, the applicable Excess and the Cyber Limit of Liability.
[3872|Normal] However, the above will not apply to any settlement where the total incurred Defence Costs and Damages, Regulatory Compensatory Award, Regulatory Fines and Penalties or PCI DSS Fines and Assessments, whichever applies, do not exceed the applicable Excess.
[3874|Normal] Choice of Counsel / Lawyer (applicable to all Insuring Clauses)
[3875|Normal] Insurers may consider an Insured’s choice of counsel or lawyer to defend any Claim, or to advise and consult on the appropriate course of action with respect to any First Party Insured Event, but the final decision on selection of counsel or lawyer rests with Insurers. No Insured shall appoint counsel or lawyer without Insurers prior written approval.
